 yā anubhūtiḥ aja āmeya ananta ātma ānanda vigrahā amahat ādi jagat māyā citra bhittim namāmi tām iṣṭa aniṣṭa apti hāna aucchoḥ tad siddhiḥ yad ṛśā śruteḥ tam mām natvā iṣṭa siddhi artham vivṛṇomi ātma saṃdṛśe yā iti svatasmid hatām dyotayati anubhūteḥ anubhāvya tve ghaṭa ādivat ananubhūtitva prasaṅgāt  na ca svatassitasya prāga bhāva ādayaḥ svatas anyatas  vā siyanti atas ajā atas  asyāḥ  na anye api bhāva vikārāḥ janma ādi tvāt teṣām ceti ānā ca na ciirma tvam rūpa ādivat  atas ameyā na asyāḥ  meyaḥ  dharmaḥ api astauti arthaḥ atas anantā antasya api meya tve atavarma tvāt  ameya tve api ananya tvāt na tahattā citaḥ kālata stāvat ānantyam siddham janma abhāvāt  ata evam deśataḥ  vastutas api anyathā ghaṭa ādi va janma prasaṅgāt  na arja vibhāgi asti na aṇūnām ca aja tvam rūpa ādima tvāt  ghaṭa ādivat  na ca anaṃśa tvam sarva diś saṃbandhāt saṃyoga abhyupaga mātra na hi anaṃśasya saṃyogaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ anaṃśasya api ced saṃyogasyāt  saṃyukta pradeśa atirikta pradeśa antara abhāvāt na dvitīya ssaṃyogaḥ etena kha ātma manasām ca saṃyogaḥ  vyākhyātaḥ kalpitāḥ ca idam śāssyuḥ tad saṃyogaḥ api kalpita eva syāt  tasmāt saṃyoge sa aṃśa tvam anaṃśa tve asaṃyogāt  kārya asiddhe jāṇu siddhiḥ tasmāt vibhaktaḥ  na avikāraḥ asti tad uktam ayāvat vikāram tu vibhāgaḥ  lokavat iti tasmāt citaḥ aja tve vibhāgaḥ  na abhyapeyaḥ avibhāge ca na itaretarābhāva siddhiḥ atammā anantā vidhā api nanvidaṃtayā cetyam bhāti anidaṃtayā eva tu cit  atas tayoḥ bhedaḥ prasiddha taraḥ  loke itaretarābhāvaḥ ca tvam ca āvocaḥ asakṛt  na cetyam cita ssvarūpam dharmaḥ  vā ghaṭa ādi vadrpādivat ca iti atas tayoḥ bhedaḥ abhyupeyaḥ anyathā abhi nāyāḥ citaḥ abheda ācetyānām api na mithas  bhedaḥ  bhāseta bhāsate tu atas  sa na na asti anyathā vibhāgāta kārya tā anumāna ādi vyavahāraḥ tava api na syāt  tasmācicce tyayoḥ bhedaḥ abhyupeyaḥ prasiddheḥ iti abā ucyate satyam prasiddhiḥ asti ata eva vyavaharāmaḥ kiṃtu na asyāḥ  mūlam paśyāmaḥ katham ucyate yadi api dṛś dṛśyayoḥ bheda dṛṣṭissamasti tathā api na sā hagdṛśyayoḥ sa bhavet  dṛśaḥ adṛśya tvāt  na hi adṛṣṭasya dṛṣṭāt  dṛṣṭasya vā adṛṣṭāt  bhedaḥ  draṣṭum śakyaḥ dharmi pratiyogi apekṣa tvāt  bheda dṛṣṭeḥ na ca adṛṣṭaḥ  dhaum pratiyogī vā sarvasya sarvatas  yugapaḍha़eda dṛṣṭi prasaṅgāt  tasmāt ṛṣṭayoḥ eva paraspara apekṣayā bheda dṛṣṭi ssaṃbhavati na tu dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭayoḥ adṛṣṭayoḥ vā atas  dṛś dṛśyayaḥ aṃda prasiddheḥ na mūlam paśyāmaḥ nanu adṛśyā api dṛś  na aprasiddhā svayaṃprathanāt  atas  bheda dṛṣṭi ssyāt iti ced  kaḥ ayam bhedaḥ  nāma kim svarūpam eva bhedinaḥ uta dharmaḥ svarūpam ced  bheda dṛṣṭeḥ pratiyogi apekṣā na syāt  na hi sva rūpa dṛṣṭiḥ pratiyogi apekṣā anyathā pratiyoginaḥ api pratiyogi apekṣa tvāt  bheda dṛṣṭeḥ anavasthā anyonya āśraya tā vā iti na kiṃci dṛśyeta dṛṣṭam eva pratiyogi apekṣayā dṛśyata iti cetna dṛśya arthā apekṣā dṛṣṭa tvāt  tāvat mātrasya na api dṛṣṭi anta rārthā apekṣā pūrva sāmagrauta eva tāvat mātra dṛṣṭeḥ punar api saṃbhavāt  tasmāt na svarūpa haṣṭiḥ pratiyogi apekṣā atas  pratiyogi apekṣa dṛṣṭi tvāt na bhedaḥ  bhedinam svarūpam eva atha dharmaḥ saḥ api na abhinnaḥ ukta doṣa prāptaḥ tasmāt katham cit bhinnaḥ jñāna antara gamyaḥ  rūparama ādivateṃdaḥ abhyupeyaḥ nanu na jñāna antareṇa api vastu svarūpā ninnam bhedam pratīmaḥ na ca bheda bhaidinoḥ bhedaḥ anavasthā prasaktar iti ced  kim sarva ca eva bhedam nirākaropi uta bheda bhedinaḥ  reva yadi sarvatra eva na naḥ kiṃcid chidyate atha bheda bhaidinoḥ tadā ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt bhedaḥ cediṣyate sa bhinnaḥ jñāna antara jñeya eṣṭavyaḥ anyathā tad abhāva prasaṅgāt  evam anyonya abhāvaḥ  api yadi saḥ anyaḥ  bhedāt  na ced  na ati deśaḥ kāryaḥ evam ca sati na dṛś dṛśyayoḥ bhedaḥ  draṣṭum śakyaḥ na api anyonyā bhāvaḥ na hi dṛśaḥ svayaṃdṛṣṭeḥ pratiyogi apekṣa dṛṣṭi antara dṛśyam rūpa antaram svam samasti svayaṃdṛṣṭitva hānāt  na ca svayam dṛṣṭeḥ kadācid api adṛṣṭi saṃbhavati svarūpaṃbhūtāyāḥ  dṛṣṭe ranya anapekṣa tvāt  anya apekṣa tve svarūpasya eva anya apekṣa tvena anityatva prasaṅgāt  dṛśya tve ca bheda abhāvayoḥ na dṛś dharma tvam dṛśya antaravat adṛśya tve ca tayoḥ asiddhiḥ svayaṃprabha tve dṛśaḥ  bheda stayā ūna syāt  sadābhānāt ca pratiyogi anapekṣa si hatvā at  bheda abhāvatva hāniḥ tasmāt na dṛśaḥ  bheda abhāvau dhaum na api svarūpam anapekṣatva prasaṅgāt  na ca ekasya he rūpe na ca tayoḥ api bhedaḥ svayaṃprabha tve anapekṣatva prasaṅgāt ca atha abheda eva bheda abhāva yoī śi dṛśye api tathā syāt  tatra abhede api kim bheda eva uta abhāva eva yadi bheda eva tatra yadi bhedasya dṛśaḥ ca abheda eva tadā kim bheda eva uta dṛś eva yadi bheda eva tadā dṛś abhāvā nna asyā bhedaḥ na api kiṃcid  prakāśeta atha bheda svayaṃprakāśaḥ nāmni vipratipattiḥ atha dṛś eva tadā na asyāḥ  bhedaḥ evam dṛśyasya atas  na dṛś dṛśyayoḥ bheda siddhiḥ atha abhāva eva tadā abhāvasya dṛśaḥ ca abhede yadi abhāva eva haka tadā haḍna syāt  tathā dṛśyam ca iti śūnyam syāt  tad api na prakāśeta dṛśaḥ abhāvāt  atha hagā iva tadā na abhāva iti na hagdṛśyayoḥ itaretarābhāva siddhiḥ kiṃca abhāvāced na anyaḥ  bhedaḥ bheda abhāvāt na anyonya abhāvaḥ sidhyet  bhinnayaḥ sau na abhinnasya eva itaretara apekṣa tvāt  na ca eka smin  eva itara itara apekṣā saṃbhavet  dyāśraya tvāt tasyāḥ bhedā bhāve bhāva abhāvayoḥ api abhedam syāt  kim punarbhāvānām tatra ekam eva vastu syāt  tatra kuta itaretarābhāvaḥ tasmā na abhāva eva bhedaḥ yadi ca bheda eva abhāvaḥ  na anyaḥ kaścid  tadā bhinnayoḥ api anyonya ani bhāva avirodhāt  ekaḥ  bhāva ssyāt  tadā kasya kutaḥ bhedaḥ dvitīya abhāvāt na ca ekasya eva bhedaḥ eka abhāva prasaṅgāt  eka abhāve ca anyā bhāvāt  punar api bhedaḥ  na syāt  tadā nai na api anekam iti na kiṃcivastu syāt  tasmāt bheda eva abhāvaḥ  na anya iti yuktam tasmāt bheda abhāvau  icchatā tau mithas  bhinnau vastuna ścetyeṣṭavyam na tu anyathā atas tau na dṛśa ssvarūpam na api dharmau  iti yuktam tayoḥ ca dṛśḥ apatve na dṛśaḥ  bhedaḥ agrū patve na dṛś dharma tvam rūpa ādivat  na ca dṛś dṛśyayodharma dharmi tu ajñānam samasti ghaṭa rūpayoḥ iva eka jñāna agamya tvāt tayoḥ na ca eka nānā gamya tve api dharma dharmi tvam atipramaṅgāt  tasmā dbha da itaretarābhāvau na dṛśaḥ  dharmau  iti sthitam ata eva na dṛśyasya api tau dhaum nyāyyau na hi dṛśaḥ tayoḥ abhāve tad apekṣayā dṛśyasya api tau saṃbhavataḥ ekasmin  api bhāve tad prasaṅgāt  na ca svatas  bhedaḥ svābhāvaḥ svayam iti śakyam vaktama tayoḥ bhāvasya ca abhāva prasaṅgāt  na ca bheda ābhā vānāgandhitasya sphurataḥ api bheda abhāva jñāne pratiyogi tvam sva ātmanaḥ api tad prasaṅgāt  tasmāt ṛśaḥ atad dharma tvāt dṛkpati yogi tayā dṛśyasya api tau dhau na sta iti sthitam māna asaṃbhavāca tau na staḥ katham ucyate tau celvayaṃmānau na dṛśya dhaum dṛgvat  eka jñāna agamya tvāt svayaṃmāna tve ca tayoḥ daśaḥ dṛśyāt mithas ca bhedaḥ  na syāt  pūrva uktena nyāyena atha anyamānau tadā api meya tvāt na tau dṛśaḥ  bheda abhāvau ghaṭa ādi bheda abhāvavat  meyasya eva ca tau tahat  bheda abhāva tvāt ca na tau dṛś saṃbandhinau sa eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ bheda abhāva pratiyogi tve dṛśaḥ ahalam ghaṭa ādivat prasajyeta atas  anyā dṛś eṣṭavyā sā api pratiyoginī ced  agiti śuddhā dṛś eṣṭavyā atas  dṛś pati yogi kaḥ  bheda abhāvau na dṛśye staḥ staḥ ced  tayoḥ kim mānam na akṣa ādauni na api manaḥ tad agocara tvāt dṛśaḥ na ca agocarāt  bhedaḥ agoca rasya ca abhāvaḥ  gocare api jñātum śakyate akṣaṇā śabda bhedā bhāva adṛṣṭeḥ gocara tve ca uktaḥ  doṣaḥ na api hagā iva tayaḥ rmānam tasyāḥ  api hi sā agocara eva ātma mānā api hi sā avadhi tvena avadhimat māna tvena ca yugapad  kṛtsnā vartitum na kṣamate aṃśabhyām ced māna avadhibhāvaḥ aṃśāḥ ca na asyāḥ tad māna abhāvāt anityatva prāpteḥ ahatva prasaṅga ācā nyathā haṅmānau ced tau na dṛkpati yogikau  anya bheda ādivat  yad mānau ca yau na tau tad pratiyogikau kim tu anya pratiyogi kau  eva yathā ghaṭa paṭayaḥ mithaḥ bheda abhāvau evam dṛś mānau  api tādṛś pati yogikau  eva iti nyāyyam abhāva jñānam ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdha ā  iṣyate na ca daśaḥ anyā upalabdhiḥ asti yad abhāvāt abhāvaḥ  jñeyaḥ atas  na dṛśaḥ bhāva jñānam samaṃsti kvacid api ta tu abhāvāt na ca prāptā nupalabdhi bhāva jñāna hetuḥ upalabdhau  api tad prasaṅgāt  prāpta anupalabdhau bhatyām eva abhāva jñānam na tu sā tahetu riti ced  tathā api tasyāḥ  abhāvāt na dṛśaḥ abhāva jñānam atha tayā vinā api abhāva jñānam dṛśi syāt  sphurantyām api syāt  dṛśye api tathā kim na syāt  na ca dṛś dṛśyayaḥ viśeṣaḥ abhāva jñānam cediṣyate nanu dṛśassa eva upalabdhiḥ atas  dṛś abhāvāt eva dṛśaḥ abhāva jñānam dṛśyasya tu anyathā iti ced  kim dṛśaḥ abhāva eva tajñānam ucyate na anyat  kiṃvā anyat tad viṣayam jñānam api bhāva rūpam kiṃcid asti yadi asti tasya hetuḥ api asti anyathā tad abhūteḥ na ca tad ahetu jāyate anya abhāva jñānasya api hetu janma prasaṅgāt  na ca prāpta anupalabyādira bhāva jñāna hetuḥ atra saṃbhavati na hi upa labdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ sva sattayā vinā anyatas  dṛśaḥ asti ananya upalabdhi tvāt  sattve ca upalabdhim syāt eva atas  na prāpta anupalabdhiddeśaḥ na api anupalabdhi mātra svābhāvā danyat  svābhāva eva ced anupalabdhiḥ na tayā anyat meyam na api asyāḥ  mānam kiṃcid  na ca meya eva abhāvaḥ sva jñāna hetuḥ abhāva antareṣa dṛṣṭa tvāt aniṣṭa tvāt ca na ca atra prati yogi smṛti ādi asti agrāhya tvādṛśaḥ sva ātma mānā api sā na ātma abhāva jñāna aṃśatām bhajeta sarva jñāna aṃśatva prasaṅgāt  yacepa asya nānasa jāyamānasya dṛnityā api svayaṃprathanā daṃśa ssyāt  tadā aviśeṣāt sarveṣām bhāva abhāva jñānānām mā aṃśa iti marve bhāva abhāvā dṛś vi śeṣaṇa tām prāpnuyuḥ nanu jñāna antarāṇām gati antaram asti dṛśaḥ abhāva jñānasya na anyā gatiḥ astauti ced  mā bhūt tarhi tad  bhavati eva iti ced  tathā api bhrāntitva upapatteḥ na ananya gati tvam na ca bhrānte gatiḥ anveṣyā gatiḥ ced asti katham bhrāntiḥ gatimatām api bhrānti tve sarva jñānānām bhrāntitva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt na ātma māna api dṛś  svābhāva jñāna aṃśaḥ tasmāt pratiyogi smṛti ādi api na abhāva jñāna hetuḥ aca asti nanu evam na evam iti dṛśam api nyarūru rurūpaḥ atas tā nirūpaṇa ajñānasya viṣayaḥ na ca nirūpaṇa ajñānam api dṛśam svarūpam eva anitya tvāt  nitya tvāt ca tava dṛśaḥ na ca atyantam aviṣaye nirūpaṇā maṃbhavati na hi kaścid nṛśṛṅgam taidaṇya ādibhiḥ nirūpayati atas  jñāna viṣaya tām dṛśaḥ api iccha mā vā nirū ru rurūpaḥ amūm aviṣaya tvāt iti ced  nanu eṣā api nirūpaṇā tvayā kriyate na ca atyanta aviṣaye nirūpaṇā saṃbhavati aviṣa yatu prasaṅgāt  na ca āviṣayā sā sva rūpa hānāt  na ca svayam eva viṣayaḥ ekasya viṣaya viṣayi bhāva anupapatteḥ na ca aviṣaye nṛśṛṅga ādau tām kaścid kadācid kurvan dṛśyata ityādyā asyāḥ ca nirūpaṇāyā atyanta aviṣaya eva viṣayaḥ anyathā hi na tatra nirūpaṇām nivārayet  na ca anya viṣayā sā na hi tatra nirūpaṇā nivārayitum iṣṭā śakyā vā na ca aviṣayā eva eṣā ukta doṣa prasaktaḥ ata eṣā nirūpaṇā ukta viṣayā eva yadi eṣā tad diṣayā syāt  kim na anyā anyā ced na syāt  na eṣā api aviśeṣāta atha na iyam svatham viṣayaukaroti kim tu anyasyā api tad viṣaya tvaṃ vāraṃyantau tasya aviṣaya tām eva sthāpayati idam eva hi asyāḥ  stat diṣaya tvam api yad etad aviṣayatva sthāpanam tasya na tu viṣayau karaṇam atas asyāḥ  nirūpaṇāyā anyasya āca viśepaḥ  astauti ced  evam haga ātmani api draṣṭavyam iyān  tu viśeṣaḥ—dṛś ātmā svayaṃprakāśa tvāt aviṣayaḥ api sidhyati anyaḥ tu atyanta aviṣayaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ api na midhyet iti tasmā dṛś ātmani marva prakāśaka tayā eva ananyaprakā śye svata eva anu ditān astamitena ātma prakāśe na prakāśamāne aviṣayatva nirū paṇa ajñānena api tasya aviṣaya tvam eva dṛḍhaukriyate na tvamau viṣayaukriyate anyathā tad nirūpaṇā eva na syāt  atas sarva jñānānām aviṣaya tvāt dṛśaḥ pratiyogi smṛtyā api hetuḥ dṛśaḥ abhāva jñāne na astauti sthitam atas  hetu abhāvā na asya iva dṛśaḥ abhāva jñānam nanu dharmi jñānam hetuḥ asti kaḥ  dhaum yasmin dṛśye abhāvaḥ  jñeyasma iti ced  pratiyogi ajñāne kaḥ  dhaum jñeyaḥ pratiyoginam hi apekṣya anyaḥ  dhaḥ syāt  anyathā sa eva pratiyogī kasmāt na bhavet  sa ced prati yogī anyaḥ  dhaum na syāt iti ced  mā bhūt  kim tena na dharmiṇā vinā abhāva jñānam iti ced  pratiyogi api nu eṣyaḥ na hi tena api vinā abhāva jñānam na api dhaum yadi pratiyogita jñānābhyām vinā api abhāva jñānam kim na dharmita jñānābhyām api vinā syāt  syāced  sadā eva dṛś bhāva jñānam syāt  na ced sadā na jātu aviśeṣāt  dharmi pratiyogibhyām ced aviśeṣitam abhāva jñānam na tadṛśa eva dṛśya eva ca syāt  kim tu sarvasya eva sarva ca eva ca syāt  aviśeṣita tvāt eva na vā kasyacid  kā api ata eva nanu sarvasya sarvatra itaretara abhāva iṣṭa eva katham ayam doṣaḥ smākam śṛṇu itaretara abhāva ādi viśeṣaḥ api aviśeṣi tatve na syāt  atas  kvacid kiṃcid iti prāptam sarvam tathā eva niṣedhyam syāt  tatas ca na kvacid na kiṃcid iti śūnyatā pramā āpatet  tathā niṣedhaḥ aśakya iti ced  aśakya niṣedha prāptiḥ eva doṣaḥ aśakya tvāt  niṣedhaḥ ca na syāt  tasmāt  pratiyogi ādi abhāvāt na dṛśā abhāvaḥ  jñeyaḥ kiṃca meyasya saṃdigdha bhāvasya ca abhāvaḥ  mānameyaḥ dṛś ta ameyā asaṃ digdha bhāvā ca svayaṃprabha tvāt eva atas asyāḥ  na abhāvaḥ  mānameyaḥ na ca asvayaṃprabhaḥ amānasmidhyet  svayaṃprabha tve cotaḥ doṣaḥ tasmāt na dṛśaḥ abhāvaḥ  dṛśye māna abhāvāt itaretarābhāvam vinā bheda anupapatteḥ uta tvāt  saḥ api na hagdṛśyayoḥ asti tasmāt ṛśaḥ abheda abhāva tvāt  deśataḥ kālataḥ  vastutas ca ānantyam siddham nanu evam dṛś dṛśyayoḥ abheda itaretara bhāvaḥ ca prasajyate tatas ca ananta bheda bhinnasya aneka abhāva dharmavataḥ  dṛśya prapañcasya dṛśaḥ abhedāt ṛśaḥ api tathātva prasaṅgāt  trividham api ānantyam hauyeta trividhasya api antasya tathā eva bhāvāt iti ced  taca na na hi abheda gandhaḥ api dṛś dṛśyayaḥ ti bheda prasiddhi virodhaḥ ca abhedam vadata ssyāt  katham ca sarva prāṇabhṛtām prasiddhataram sarva vyavahāra āśrayam ca bhedam apahatya hagdṛśyayoḥ pramāṇam vinā abheda ssāpa trapeṇa śakyate vaktam nanu bhavatai vā uttaḥ abhedaḥ  bhedam nirākurvatā na aham abhedam vacmi pramāṇā bhāvāt  bheda prasiddhi virodhāt ca bheda nirākṛtau yathā prasi hiḥ na virudhyate evam abheda uktā  apauti ced  satyam yadi abhede pramāṇam asti na tu tena vinā pramiḍiḥ bādhyā aśakya tvāt  sarva vyavahāra lopa prasaṅgāt ca tasya tasya bādhasya api bādhyatva prasaṅgāt  na aham pi prasiddhim bādhe kim tu asyāḥ  māna mūla tām tad dādhe pina prasiddhi naśyet  vicandra ādi prasiddhivat yathāvastu darśanāt  prāc avināśa upapatteḥ nanu katham abhede pramāṇa abhāvaḥ  dṛś dṛśyayoḥ kim atra pṛcchayate na hi abhedaḥ pratibhāti tayoḥ na api nyāyatassaṃbhavati tad pratibhāsaḥ  vā tamaḥ prakāśayoḥ iva prasiddhataraḥ ca bhedaḥ tatra kim pṛcchayate na hi kaścid amūḍhaḥ pṛcchati katham tamaḥ prakāśayaḥ stena eva rūpeṇa abhede pramāṇa abhāva iti yadi kaścid bhedam brūyāta asau praṣṭavyaḥ  bhavati katham prasiddhi nyāya viruddhaḥ abheda ucyata iti na tu anyaḥ katham na tāvat ṛś dṛśyayoḥ abhedaḥ pratau titas  tad abhāvāt na api nyāyataḥ tamaḥ prakāśa vaviruḍa svabhāva tvāt ata eva na aikya jñānam api tayoḥ katham ca dṛś dṛśyayoḥ svānyamāna tayā eka jñāna āgamya yoḥ abheda jñānam abhedaḥ  vā yadi ca dṛśyaḥ  dṛśaḥ abhinnaḥ dṛś eva syāt  anāsya dṛśyatā atha abhinnā dṛś  dṛśyāt  dṛśyā eva sā na dṛś iti dṛśyaḥ api adṛśyassyāt  yadi ca dṛśyā haga ātmanā jñāyeta dṛśyasya hara jñāna jñeya tvam hatvam jaḍa jñāna abhāvaḥ ca pramajyata atha haka dṛśya ātmanā jñāyeta dṛśaḥ  dṛśya jñāna jñeyatva mahatvam havana ca ābhānam dṛśya ajñānam ca prasajyeta atas  nābhedaḥ abheda jñānam vā dṛś dṛśyayoḥ na api dharma dharmi tvam na hi ekasya dṛśaḥ  dṛśyasya dharma tvena dharmi tvena vā dṛśya tvam tad ṛtvam ca yugapad kā anyena yujyate na api aṃśā bhyām anaṃśa tvāt  dṛśya aṃśasya ca ahavāt  na ca dharma dharmi tvam api syayaṃprakāśam eva abhedāt  dharma dharmi tvahānāt dṛśyām aṃbandhāt ca na api dṛśyam eva dṛśā asaṃbandhāt  tasmāt nābhedaḥ  dṛś dṛśyayoḥ na api dharma dharma bhāvaḥ kiṃca ye ete hagdṛśyayoḥ abheda tad jñāne iṣyate te kim dayosmataḥ  toḥ ca kim vā ekasmin  eva sati bhāti ca uta iyoḥ satoḥ ekasmin  eva bhāti kim vā ekasmin  eva sati dayoḥ bhātoḥ na tāvat prathame kalye te staḥ bhedata jñāna yoḥ bhāvāt  tayoḥ bhāve api itare sta iti ced  kim bheda jñāna viṣaya eva abheda jñānam uta anyatra yadi tatra eva tad api bheda jñānam eva tad eka artha tvāt anyathā itarat api abheda jñānam dayoḥ eka artha tvāt syāt  atha anyatra tadā api na iyā ura bheda jñānam tasmāt nādyaḥ kalpaḥ  nyāyyaḥ na api dvitīyaḥ tatra api ekasya eva bhāvāt  bhānāca na dvayoḥ abhedata jñāne tṛtīya tu kalye dvitīyasman  api na bhāti tatra kutaḥ abheda jñānam yoḥ bhātaḥ  bheda jñānam nābhātoḥ bhāda bhātoḥ vā kiṃca—yasmin bhāti yaḥ anyaḥ  na bhāti nāmau tatas abhinnaḥ bhātaḥ ghaṭāt iva me ruḥ abhede tu abhātaḥ  api bhānam bhātaḥ api abhānam vā syāt  na hi ekasya eva aviyām vinā bhāna ābhāne yugapata virodhāt  avirodhe marvasya marvadā tad prasaṅgāt  ekasya eva bhānam uktam ayuktam syāt  ekasya eva aṃśābhyām bhāna ābhāne sta iti ced  tadā api na bhātaḥ aśasya ābhānam na api abhātaḥ  bhānam na aṃśinaḥ api ekasya bhāna ābhāne ukta doṣa prāptaḥ aṃśa antarābhyām ced  anavasthā atas  dṛś dṛśyayoḥ eka bhāne api anya ābhānam ced  bheda eva tayoḥ nanu evam saha upalambha niyamāt dṛś dṛśyayoḥ abhedaḥ prāptaḥ na hi dṛśā vinā dṛśyam bhāti na api dṛśya vinā dṛś  atassaha eva bhānāt  abheda iti ced  tad na abhede sahabhāna ayogāt iyohi sahabhānam na ekasya eva na hi dṛśā eva dṛś  saha bhātauti bhavatā api ucyate na api dṛśyena eva dṛśyam saha bhātauti kim tu dṛś dṛśyayoḥ sahabhānam ucyate atas tayoḥ bhedaḥ  bhāti eva tava api anyathā sahaḥ tyayogāt  na ca bheda jñānasya api abheda eva arthaḥ sarvatra eva bheda abhāva prasaṅgāt  nanu bhinnayoḥ ghaṭa paṭayoḥ asahā api bhānam dṛṣṭam atas tadailakṣaṇyāt dṛś dṛśyayoḥ abheda iti ced  tad na bheda dṛṣṭi virodhāt  na ca ghaṭa ādi vailakṣaṇyāt abheda eva vailakṣaṇyam dṛṣṭa virodhi grāhyam huk dṛśyatva vailakṣaṇyasya avi rodhina iṣṭasya bhāvāt  na hi ghaṭa paṭa jñāna vailakṣaṇyā daśva mahiṣa jñānasya tayoḥ abhedaḥ dṛṣṭa virodhāt  evam acāpi draṣṭavyam na ca ghaṭa ādīnām api bhedaḥ asahabhānam janma nāśā dayaḥ dṛśyatā ca syādṛśaḥ abhede dṛśi teṣām am aṃbhavasya ukta tvāt dṛśaḥ  vā dṛśyāt abhede bheda āt ayassyaḥ atas ca dṛśaḥ api halāt  dṛśyam api na sidhyet  na ca ekasya dṛśaḥ  dṛtvam dṛśya tvam ca yugapad krameṇa vā aṃśābhyām vā yajyata iti uktam tasmāt sarva vyavahāra lopa prasaṅga anna abhedaḥ  dṛś dṛśyayoḥ nanu tayoḥ bheda jñāna asaṃbhavaḥ tvayā eva uktaḥ atas abhedaḥ prāptaḥ na prāptaḥ abheda jñāna asaṃbhavasya api mayā eva ukta tvāt tasmāt na bhedaḥ kaḥ ca ayam mahā upalam maniyamaḥ  nāma na tāvat  saha upalabhyatva niyamaḥ dṛśaḥ anupalabhya tvāt  na api saha upa labdhi tvam dṛśyasya anupalabdhi tvāt hagdṛśyayoḥ saha eva bhānam na pṛthak iti artha iti ced  tad na dṛśaḥ  nitya tvāt  svayaṃprabha tvāt ca sat ābhāna upapapatteḥ dṛśyasya vidyut ādeḥ atathā tvāt  na saha bhānam yadi api dṛśā vinā na dṛśyam bhāti tathā api dṛśyam vinā dṛś bhātauti na saha eva bhānam tayoḥ nanu anya saṃvid kāle vidyut dattat saṃvid api na asti katham jñāyate na asti iti vidyut saṃvidaḥ tadā abhānāt iti ced  kim vidyut na bhāti uta saṃvid api na bhāti na tāvat saṃvid api na bhāti tasyāḥ tadā api bhānāt  na hi saṃvidaḥ  bhede pramā iti uktam nanu anya saṃvid ta dā bhāti na vidyu diśeṣitā iti ced  kim vidyut diśeṣita tā nāma saṃvidara svarūpam uta saṃvedyasya yadi saṃvidaḥ sā api bhāti eva saṃvid bhānāt  saṃvedya svarūpam ced  tad abhānān na saṃvidobhānam kiṃca vidyu diśeṣita tvam nāma saṃvidaḥ  yadi vidyut diṣaya tvam tacet saṃvedyam na saṃvidara svarūpam anavasthā ca asaṃvedyam ced  na sidhyet  svayaṃprabham ced  na saṃvidaḥ  bhidyeta atassaṃvidi bhāntyām tad api bhāti eva nanu ghaṭa saṃvid paṭa saṃvid iti saṃvidā bheda pratīteḥ tā jāyante naśyanti ca iti ced  tad na maṃvidā sva saṃvedya tvāt  kṣaṇikatvāca anyonya aviṣaya tvāt bheda dṛṣṭya yogāt  na ca ekasmin  eva sva ātmani bheda dṛṣṭiḥ dvitīya apekṣa tvāt tasyāḥ yadi ekasya āssaṃvidaḥ anyāssaṃvidaḥ  viṣayaḥ yāsām bheda iṣyate tāsām tasyāḥ ca bhedaḥ  na syāt  viṣaya virṣāya bhāvāt  ghaṭa tad saṃvidoḥ iva ekasya aneka rū pāyogāt ca tatra kutasma vijdasmidhyet  saṃvidām anyonya aviṣaya tve ca bheda asi dviruktā atha tāsām tasyāḥ  mithas ca bheda iṣyate ghaṭa tad saṃvidoḥ api bheda eṣṭavyaḥ viṣaya viṣayi bhāvāt  tahat eva tatas ca ghaṭa naula ādi viśeṣasya viṣaya eka āspada tvāt na saṃvijhedaḥ sidhyet  saṃvidām api saṃvid iṣaya tve ghaṭa ādi vadasva saṃvedya tvam asaṃvit tvam ca syāt  ghaṭa ādayaḥ api saṃvida eva iti ced  tad na teṣām tad saṃvidaḥ anya tve sati saṃvid tve pramāṇa abhāvāt  yadi te api saṃvid assyuḥ na viṣayā bhaveyuḥ na hi ghaṭa saṃvibaṭasya anyasya vā tadā eva viṣayaḥ  bhāti na ca ātmanaḥ api sā viṣaya tayā bhāti ekasya yugapadiṣaya viṣayi bhāva ayogāt ca viṣayasya ca anya tvāt  ghaṭavat  yadi saṃvid saṃvid antarasya viṣayaḥ tadā sā viṣaya tayā eva bhāseta na tu viṣayitayā ghaṭavat  vipayitayā eva tu bhāti ghaṭaḥ tu na tathā atas  ghaṭa viṣaya vailakṣaṇya aviṣaya tvam eva saṃvidaḥ tasmāt daṭa ādeviṣayasya asaṃvid tvam eva niścinumaḥ aviṣayatva vyāna tvāt saṃvidaḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ ca tad abhāvāt ata saṃvidām api saṃvid viṣaya tve ghaṭa ādivat asaṃvid tvam syāt iti yuktam uktam ghaṭa saṃvidaḥ api anyadā viṣaya tā syāt iti ced  na viṣaya ākāra rahi tāya āssaṃvidaḥ kadācid api viṣaya bhāva adṛṣṭaḥ sakṛti payasya anyadā vipayitā adṛṣṭaḥ ca ghaṭasya na hi ghaṭaḥ kadācid api viṣayau dṛṣṭaḥ kāla bhedena ca viṣaya viṣayi bhāva abhyupagame sthāyitva prasaṅgaḥ katham amaṃvinnā saṃvitmidhyet  svayam katham vā anyam sādhayet  atassvasam vedyā iti ced  yadi asiddhā anyam na sādhayet  na ātmānam api miḍā mādhayet  asiddha tvāt  na api miḍā siddha tvāt eva na ca sidyā api sādhyā sādhyatā anihattaḥ yadi asiḍā ātmānam sādhayet  tathā eva anyam api sādhayet  na anyam ced  na ātmānam api na ca anyasya āssaṃvidaḥ siddhā ātmāna manyam ca sādhayet  anyasyā api anya sādhya tve anavasthā prāpteḥ anya saṃvedya tve ca na ātma saṃvedya tā saṃvidaḥ tasmāt asaṃvedya eva saṃvid  saṃvedyam ca asaṃvid eva atassaṃvedyasya ghaṭa sukha ādessaṃvidaḥ ca abheda gandhaḥ api na pramāṇavān ata eva na saṃvidaḥ api bhedaḥ sarvasya eva bhedasya saṃvedya āśraya tvāt saṃvedya tvāt ca saṃvedyasya ca asaṃvidharma tvāt  na vastuna ssvarūpam bheda iti ca uktam saṃvid antara abhyupagame ca teṣām saṃvi ddiṣaya tve ghaṭa ādivat asaṃvid tvāt aviṣaya tve ca tad asiddheḥ svayaṃprakāśa mātra tve ca availakṣaṇyāt  bheda asaṃbhavāt ca nanu ekā jāyate anyā naśyati iti janma nāśa vyavasthayā eva vailakṣaṇyam   ata eva ca bheda iti ced  tad na bheda asiddhau vyavasthā siddheḥ bheda vyavasthā vailakṣaṇyānām ca anyonya āśraya tvāt na eka sya api siddhiḥ janma nāśau  api abhinnau ced  saṃvidaḥ tayaḥ rapi bhedaḥ  na syāt  bhede api saṃvedyau ced  na saṃvid aḥ tau asaṃvedya tve bheda asiddhiḥ tasmāt ṛgdṛśyayosmaha upalambhe api nābhedaḥ na api saha upalambha iti sthitam ata ekasmin bhāti yaḥ anyaḥ  na bhāti tayaḥ bhedaḥ  yukta iti iyosmataḥ  rekasmin bhāti abheda tajñāne dṛś dṛśyayoḥ iti ayam api tṛtīyaḥ kalpaḥ  nirastaḥ antye api kalpa ekasya eva bhāvān na iyā uḥ abheda tad jñāne ekasya eva bhāve api dayoḥ bhānādabheda jñānam syāt iti ced  tadā api na bhedena bhātoḥ abheda tad jñāne bheda abheda jñāna yaḥ kaviṣaya tve bhedaḥ abhedaḥ  vā arthassyāt  na bheda abhedau iyoḥ ekasya vā natarām anya viṣaya tve uktam ca etad  purastāt  katham ca ekasmin  eva sati dayam bhāti kim ca ekam asti yadi dṛśyam eva tadā haga bhāvān na kiṃcid  bhāyāt  yadi dṛś eva tadā api na iyam bhāyāt  hamāra tve bheda jñāna ayogasya ukta tvāt katham ca dṛśya prapañcaḥ  bhāna na asti eva iti ucyate tasmāt ṛgdṛśyayaḥ bhedaḥ asti __ atha ucyeta–yadi api dṛś dṛśya ātmanā tayaḥ bhadosti tathā api brahma ātmanā abhedaḥ api asti eva brahmaṇa eka tvāt  tasmāt ca anayoḥ ananya tvāt iti tad ca ayuktam bheda abhāva prasaṅgāt  na ṭekasmāt brahmaṇaḥ ananya tve tayaḥ mithaḥ bhedaḥ  nyāyyaḥ tasya api bheda prāpteḥ tasya abhede api tayoḥ bheda śced syāt  tasmāt tayoḥ na ananya tvam mithas  bhinnayoḥ ghaṭa paṭayaḥ  riva stambhāt yena rūpeṇa ānayoḥ bhedaḥ atas  rūpa antareṇa abhedaḥ  brahmaṇā iti ced  te rūpe tayoḥ abhinne ced  brahmaṇaḥ api pūrvavateṃdaḥ tayoḥ vā bhedaḥ  na syāt  bhinne ced  tayaḥ rūpayaḥ bhedaḥ astauti nābhedaḥ  dṛś dṛśyayoḥ na ca anayaḥ  rūpa dayam samasti na hi dṛśaḥ  dṛśyam rūpam na api dṛśyasya dṛś  na ca tṛtīyam rūpam asti tasmāt na dṛśaḥ  rūpa dayam na api dṛśyasya iti tayoḥ bhedaḥ abheda eva vā anyonyam na bhedā bhedau rūpa dayā bhāvāt na ca eka rūpa eva bheda abheda jñāne aikārthya prasaṅgāt iti uktam ekam virūpam iti ca viprati ṣitam ekasmācehe rūpe bhinne na tasya te rūpe bhinna tvāt  yathā na anyonyam rūpe yathā ca tad ekam na tayaḥ rūpam abhede tad ekam eva iti na ekam dvi rūpam syāt  tasmāt  brahmā api ekam ced  hageva vā syāt  dṛśyam eva vā na tu ubhayam na api anya virūpam atas  brahma ātmanā anayoḥ abheda iti ayuktam nanu idam dṛṣṭa viruddham avocaḥ ekam aneka rūpam na bhavati iti eka hi aneka rūpam paśyāmaḥ na ca dṛṣṭe arthe anupapannam nāma eka rūpam ca ekam iṣyate dṛṣṭa tvāt  evam ekam aneka rūpam api eṣṭa vyam dṛṣṭa tvāt eva ata ekam hirūpam iti vipratiṣiddham iti yuktam iti ced  darśanam parāmṛśya vadantu bhavantaḥ kim rūpiṇa ekasmāt abhinnāni eva rūpāṇi dṛśyante uta bhinnā nyeva athavā bhinna abhinnāni yadi ekasmāt abhinnāni eva dṛśyante— tadā na aneka rūpam ekam dṛṣṭam syāt  aneka adṛṣṭeḥ eka sya eva ca dṛṣṭeḥ atha ucyeta anekāni eva rūpāṇi dṛśyante tebhyaḥ ca abhinnaḥ rūpī dṛśyata iti tadā api ekasmāt rūpāda bhedena dṛṣṭasya rūpa antarebhyaḥ abhedaḥ  na draṣṭum śakāte yathā tasya eva rūpasya anyathā tasya api rūpasya rūpa antarebhyaḥ abheda dṛṣṭeḥ sarva rūpāṇām abheda dṛṣṭi prasaṅgāt  na aneka rūpam ekam dṛśyeta atha bhinnāni eva rūpiṇaḥ  rūpāṇi tadā na aneka rūpa tvam rūpiṇaḥ rūpāṇam iva katham ca atyanta bhinnānām rūpa rūpi bhāvaḥ rūpāṇām api rūpa rūpitva prasaṅgāt  artha bhinna abhinnāni rūpiṇaḥ  rūpāṇi dṛśyante tadā api kim ekena rūpeṇa bhinnāni anyena abhinnāni uta ekena eva bhinnāni bhinnāni ca tatra prathame kalpe ekaikasya rūpasya he he rūpe sta iti virūpa tvam tayoḥ ca rūpayoḥ bheda abhede pratyeka virūpa tvam iti anavasthā rūpa rūpāṇām tathā rūpiṇaḥ api rūpaiḥ bheda abhede pratirūpam de he rūpe anye eṣṭavye tābhyām ca bheda abhede apare he he rūpe iti rūpi rūpāṇām api anavasthā tatas ca varṣa śatena api vāla agra māvasya api tattvam draṣṭum vaktam vā na śakyam syāt  kenacid api amūḍhena tathā hi rūpa rūpiṇaḥ mithaḥ bheda abheda dṛṣṭi artham he he rūpe paśyatā rūpa tad rūpayoḥ tad rūpa tad rūpayoḥ ca he he rūpe draṣṭavye tathā rūpi tad rapayoḥ tad rapa tadrapayoḥ ca bheda abheda dṛṣṭi artham eva he he rūpe draṣṭavye na hi rūpe adṛṣṭvā tābhyām bheda abhedau tahataḥ  draṣṭum śakyate tasmāt rūpa rūpiṇoḥ bheda abhedau draṣṭum icchatā anantāni rūpāṇi pratyekam teṣām ca draṣṭavyāni prasajyante na ca tathā dṛśyante dṛṣṭeṣṭhaṣyananteṣu rūpeṣu sākṣāt bheda abhedaḥ  na kayoḥ cit sidhyataḥ tathā hi na rūpa rūpiṇoḥ api sākṣā mithas  bheda abheda āviṣṭau kim tu rūpābhyām rūpayoḥ api yasya bhedaḥ  na tasya abhedaḥ yasya abhedaḥ  na tasya bheda iti bheda abhedau  ekasya kasyacid na dhaum staḥ tahataḥ  dyau  api sta iti ced  na ekaḥ api atarga tvāt  rūpayohi tau dhaum na tahataḥ rūpa dharmau  api tau tad abhedāt tad dharmau  upacayete iti ced  abhede kim iti upacāraḥ na hi rūpayoḥ tau  upa caryete bhedasya api bhāvāt apacāra iti ced  na asti tarhi mukhyam bhinna abhinna tvam rūpa rūpiṇoḥ upacāra iṣṭeḥ atha ucyeta idam eva tad mukhyam bhinna abhinna tvam yau  etau rūpa dhamaum bheda abhedau taiti upacaritau tasya tayoḥ ca bhinna abhinna tvāt  anyasya mukhyasya abhāvāt  athavā na upacaritau tau anya dharmaḥ  hi anyatra upacārya ssyāt  na ca anya tvam eva rūpayoḥ taddataḥ ca bhinna abhinnatvā uktaḥ idam eva tarhi bhinna abhinna tvam rūpayaḥ staddataḥ ca katham siddham yad prasādāt rūpa gau bheda abhedau rūpā dṛś dṛśyayoḥ bheda abheda nirāsaḥ ntarābhyām rūpavatī upacaryete na tāvat rūpayoḥ tahataḥ ca bhinnā bhinna tvam sākṣāt  anyatra api tathā aprasaṅgāt aniṣṭa tvāt ca na ca anya gau bheda abhedau tatra upacāaum̐ katham na tāvat pūrvottau rūpa gau bheda abhedau tatra upacaraṇauyau tad upacārāt bheda abheda siddhiḥ tad siddhau tad upacāra iti itaretara āśrayatva prasaṅgāt  rūpa antarābhyām ca tau rūpayoḥ bheda abhedau atas tad upacāre tad bhāve api na rūpayoḥ taddataḥ ca bhinna abhinna tvam sidhyet  kim tu yadi sidhyet rūpa antarābhyām eva sidhyet  na svarūpi rūpā bhyām tad api na sidhyet  rūpata itas bhinna abhinnatva asiddhe stad adhīna tvāt ca tasya yadi nāma sidhyet  tathā api rūpiṇaḥ  ye rūpe tābhyām eva bheda abhedau rūpasya svakīya rūpa dāreṇa sidhyataḥ na tu rūpiṇā uktena nyāyena atas  rūpa rūpiṇoḥ ekena rūpeṇa bhedaḥ anyena abheda iti asmin pakṣa kvacid api bheda abheda asiddheḥ ayam pakṣaḥ anupapannaḥ atha ekena eva rūpeṇa abhedaḥ  bhedaḥ ca tayoḥ tadā bheda abheda buddhyoḥ eka eva arthaḥ syāt  yadyena rūpeṇa ekasya buddheviṣayaḥ tad tena eva ced anyasyā api tadā katham tayoḥ aneka artha tā atas tayoḥ bhedaḥ abhedaḥ  vā eka eva arthaḥ tayoḥ ca pakṣayoḥ doṣa uktaḥ tasmāt na aneka rūpam ekam dṛṣṭam kadācid kenacid pramāṇena upapannam vā atas  brahmā api ekam ced  na aneka rūpam iti yuktam eva uktam atas  brahma ātmanā dṛś dṛśyayoḥ abheda iti ayuktam dṛś dṛśya rūpābhyām brahmaṇa ekasya aneka rūpatva yogāt tathā dṛś dṛśyayoḥ api ekaikasya aneka rūpa tā yogāt brahma rūpeṇa abhedaḥ anya rūpeṇa bheda iti anyāyyam hagdṛśyayoḥ ca abrahma rūpa tve tābhyām bhinnam brahma syāt  bhinna tve janma nāśā brahmatvāt ayaḥ  doṣā ghaṭa ādivat prasajyeran ahave ca asvayaṃprakāśa tvāt na sidhyet  yadi sidhyet  dṛśya tayā eva sidhyet  tatas ca dṛśya jātāt bhinna tvam anyāyyam dṛśya tve ca itara dṛśī avadṛśaḥ  bhedaḥ abhedaḥ ca na sidhyet  atha e tad doṣa parijihīrṣayā abhinnam eva brahma iṣyate tadā api na hābhyām abhinnam virūpatva ayogāt dṛśyāt abheda uktaḥ  doṣaḥ dṛśaḥ ced abhedaḥ astu na atra kaścid doṣaḥ yadi sā eva brahma na anyathā aneka rūpa tā anupapatteḥ eka vastunaḥ tasmā dṛś dṛśyayaḥ bheda gandhaḥ api asti atas  dṛś dṛśyayoḥ bheda abhāve abheda prāpta īdṛśya prapañca gatam vividham api antavat tvam dṛśī api prasajyata iti yad uktam tad parihṛtam katham ca abhede dṛśi ukta doṣa prāptiḥ na hi abhede api ekasya he rūpe saṃstaḥ atas  dṛśyam eva vā syāt  dṛś eva vā dṛśyam eva ced  tad api na bhāseta dṛś eva ced  tadā na dṛśyam bhāseta api katham tagata doṣa prāptiīśi tasmāt ṛgdṛśyayoḥ abhede dṛśyam āvatve tasya api pramāṇa abhāvā dṛś abhāvāca dṛśi dṛśya doṣa aprāpteḥ dṛś māca tve ca dṛśya abhāvā dṛśi tadā ūṣā prāpteḥ dṛśyā de api dṛśasta doṣa aprāpteḥ sva gata doṣa abhāvāca nirdoṣā eva dṛś abhyupeyā sarvaiḥ doṣaḥ api bhavana dṛś eva ced syāt  na doṣa ssyāt  na hi sā eva tasyāḥ  doṣaḥ anya tve na asya āssaṃbandhaḥ anya an anya tvam ced  vairūpya ayogā nirastam atas  bheda ādi abhāvāt  janma ādi doṣa gandhaḥ api dṛśam na ḍhaukata iti sthitam kiṃca dṛśye api ete doṣāḥ pramāṇataḥ  nirūpyamāṇā na saṃbhāvayitum śakyante kutas tad saṃbandha adṛśi syuḥ tathā hi anyatve ananya tve ca na dharma dharmi bhāvaḥ anya an anya tvam ca nirastam atas adharmaka tvāt  guṇān api asaṃspṛśat vastu katham doṣān saṃspṛśet  kiṃca bhedasya vastunaḥ  bhede bheda abhede ca tasya tasya bheda avastunaḥ ca anyaḥ anyaḥ  bheda iti anavasthānāt na kaścid bhedaḥ  vastu saṃspṛśet  abhede tu ekam eva tad ca vastu eva na tu bheda eva vastu abhāve tasya api abhāvāt tad eva vasu iti ced  astu tathā api ekam eva vastu tad ca na dṛśyam tasya sa apekṣa tvāt at vitīya tā siddheḥ atas  dṛś eva tasya assvata smiddheḥ ekatva upapatteḥ na ca asyā eka tvam dharmaḥ ukta doṣa prasa ṅgāt  atas  nirbhedam adharmakam vastu eka śabdena vivakṣyate bheda dharma abhāva itare dharmāḥ pratyuktāḥ tad adhauna tvāt teṣām bhinnayoḥ hi itaretarābhāvaḥ atas  bheda abhāve sa na syāt  atas ca vastu asaṃkara asiddheḥ ekam vastu syāt  bhāva abhāvānā mitaretara abhāva abhyupagame anavasthā anabhyupagame vaḥ tu saṃkara asiddhiḥ na ca abhāvam vinā janma ādi siddhiḥ na hi ajñāte prāc abhāve kasyacid janma niścayam syāt  na hi adṛṣṭasya dṛṣṭi mātra janma sādhayet  na ca adarśane asiddhe adṛṣṭa dṛṣṭiḥ sidhyet  atas  prāgabhāva abhāve dṛśyasya darśanasya ca janmā bhāvaḥ janma abhāve na anye api bhāva vikāra āssyaḥ janma pūrva tvāt teṣām atas  kūṭastham sadā eka rūpam vastu svatassiddham asiddham eva vā kaipya ayogāt ca asiddham eva ced  asat kalpam siddham eva ced  dṛś eva vastu na anyat  sati api prāc abhāve na asataḥ  janma śṛṅgavat  na ca akarīkā janiḥ kriyā tvāt  gamivat  na ca asiddha āśrayā sā draṣṭum śakyā āśraya adṛṣṭeḥ anumeyā ced  sa kartakā eva kriyā antaravat  siddhāśrayā ced  niṣphalā anavasthā ca prāc asataḥ  janma ced  janeḥ api janma prāk  abhāvāt  prāk  bhāve tahataḥ api prāmbhāvaḥ anyathā jana svātantryam syāt  janeḥ ca janmani anavasthā atas  janma nāma na kiṃcid  kasya cit apa pannam paśyāmaḥ evam nāśa ādayaḥ api nirūpyamāṇā na avatiṣṭhante tasmāt muṣṭhuktam dṛśye api na ete doṣā nirūpya māṇāsaṃbhavanti kutas tad saṃbandhāt dṛśi syuḥ iti tasmāt anantā eva anubhūtiḥ iti sthitam yadi na bhinnaḥ na api abhinnaḥ na api bhinna abhinnaḥ anubhūteḥ prapañcaḥ kā tarhi tasya gatiḥ tām vakṣyāmaḥ nanu anubhaviva ātmanā vinā na asti anubhūtiḥ tad katham sā anantā na eṣa doṣaḥ yatasma eva saḥ katham ucyate saḥ api anubhūti svabhāvaḥ ced  na asyāḥ  bhedaḥ anyathā saḥ anā tma iti na anubhavitā atasma eva ātmā ananta tvāt ca athavā ananta tvāt sava paramātmā tad lakṣaṇasya tasyām paripūrṇa tvāt  anya tve tad ayogāt ca atas ananta tvāt sava paramātmā ata eva ānanda vigrahā ānandaḥ asya assvarūpa mā iva na anayoḥ bheda gandhaḥ apauti arthaḥ nanu aparyāya śabdānām bhinna artha tā dṛṣṭeḥ bhedaḥ anayoāyyaḥ amukhya artha tā vā ānanda śabdasya iti ced  na bheda bhedi śabdābhyām vyabhicārāt  na hi bhinnaḥ ghaṭa iti paryāyau bhinnaḥ paṭa iti api darśanāt  na ca bhinnāaum̐ bhedasya bhede anavasthānāt  ata eva bheda abhedayoḥ api abhedāt  tad śabda avaṣya bhinnāaum̐ bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ ca ghaṭa iti atra na ca ābābheda śabdaḥ  bheda nitti māca paraḥ dharmaddaya para tayā prayuktaḥ anyathā ghaṭa śabda eva vācyaḥ  na bheda abheda śabdau aprakṣālana ādi paṅkasya durāda sparśanam varam iti nyāyāt  tathā tava eva abhinna ghaṭa śabdau abhinnāaum̐ abhedaḥ ced  ghaṭāt bhinnaḥ atad dharma ssyāt  paṭavat  bhinnā bhinnaḥ ced  saḥ api abhedaḥ anyaḥ ced  atad dharmaḥ anavasthā ca tasmāt bheda abheda ghaṭa śabdā api aparyāyā abhinna arthāḥ ca evam ca api draṣṭavyam bheda abheda taicchabdebhyaḥ anyatra aparyāyāṇā mabhinna artha tā na asti iti ced  tad na asti hi sā prakṛṣṭa prakāśa ssavitā ityādidhapi na hi prakarṣa prakāśau savitari bhinnau tathā api na aprakṛṣṭa prakāśa smavitā bhinnau ced  prakarṣaḥ aprakāśam syāt  prakāśaḥ ced na tatas  bhinnaḥ aprakāśa ścanna sa vitū rūpam prakāśa eka rūpa tvāt  savituḥ nanvāṣṇya mapi sa vitū rūpam satyam tathā api na tad  prakarṣa śabda arthaḥ prakṛṣṭa prakāśaḥ candra iti api darśanāt  tasmāt na prakarṣa prakāśau savitari bhinnau tathā api na paryāya tvam prakṛṣṭam tama iti api darśanāt  nanu aneka arthaiḥ saha prayujyamānasya prakṛṣṭa śabdasya na tad tad abhinna artha tvam naula ādi śabdavat iti ceta tad na bheda śabda ādivat  tad tad abhinna arthatva upapatteḥ bheda bhaidinoḥ iva prakarṣa prakāśayoḥ api savitari bheda anupapatteḥ ukta tvāt  nanu eva manyāni api bahūni udāharaṇāni saṃbhavanti maṃbhavantu tāni api tava eva mukham apidadhati na naḥ kiṃcid chidyate sarvathā na aprakāśaḥ prakāśa viśeṣaṇam tasma ajñāna ānanda śabdayoḥ nāvā artha bhedaḥ anumeyaḥ āgama virodhāt ca nanu āgama arthe niścite tad virodha udbhāvyeta na adya api abhinna vastu āgama artha iti niścita miti ced  tad na niścita tvāt ananta ādi śabdareva na hi te bhedam sahante nyāyataḥ api bhedaḥ  nirastaḥ tarhi abheda avirodhāt ānanda śabdasya adaḥkha tvam artha iti ced  tad na amukhya artha tvāt na hi mukhye arthe saṃbhavati amukhyaḥ arthaḥ  grāhyaḥ aduḥkha tvam ca tad chandaiḥ eva siddham ananta ādi śabdaiḥ ca na ānanda śabdam apekṣate yadi aparyāyāṇām bhinna artha tā eva tadā brahma vākya gatānām sarva śabdānām aparyāya tvāt bahu bhedam brahma uktam syāt  ānanda śabdaḥ ca amukhya arthaḥ api aparyāya tvāt  bhinna artha ssyāt  atha ucyeta anya nivṛtti arthānām nivṛtte ravaḥ tu tvāt na abheda virodhi tvam ānanda śabdasya api duḥkha nivṛtti artha tvāt na virodhitā anivṛtti arthāḥ tu bhinna arthā iti tāḥ nanda śabdasya mukhya artha tve api anya nivṛtti arthatva upapatte rnābheda virodhi tvam satya jñāna ādi śabdavat tathā hi ātmā eva ānandaḥ aānandaḥ  brahma iti vyajānāt aānandā ḍova khalu imāni bhūtāni jāyante ityādi śruteḥ brahmā tmā ānanda śabdānām ekārtha tā avagamāt tathā hi tasmāt ā etasmāt ātmana ākāśa saṃbhūtaḥ iti tad śabdena abrahma vi dāpnoti param iti sūcitam brahma parāmṛśya tad eva asatyam jānam anantam brahma iti lakṣitam ayaḥ  veda nihitam guhāyām iti pratyaktayā vedya tvena uktam etad śabdena parāmṛśya taca eva ca ātma śabdam prayujya tasya brahma ātmanaḥ  jagat prakṛti tām pradarśya ante aānandaḥ  brahma iti vyajānāt iti brahma ānandayaḥ reka tām sva mukhena aivolā tasya brahma ānandasya aānandāya iva khalu imāni bhūtāni jāyante iti jagat prakṛti tā darśanāt  pūrva uktasya brahma ātmana ānandasya ca ekatā pratīteḥ brahma ātmā nandānām ekatā eva su dṛḍham niścīyate tatra yathā brahma anyat  aham ca anya iti bhrāntyā bhedam manvānasya brahma asmoti pratyak brahmaṇoḥ abrahmān ātma tā nirāsena ekatā eva śrutyā bodhyate—evam brahma ātma ānanda bhede bhrānti gṛhaute janaḥ tāḥ  dāsena abheda eva bodhyate na bheda gandhaḥ api spṛśyate yathā ca ghaṭa ākāśa mahā ākāśayoḥ sūrya jala sūryayoḥ ca bheda nirāmena abheda eva bodhyate ghaṭa ākāśaḥ  mahā ākāśa ityādi vākyaiḥ na tu anyonya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya tayā bhedaḥ evam acāpi draṣṭavyam tasmāt ānanda ādi śabdānām mukhya artha tve api abheda avirodha annā mukhya arthī grāhyaḥ nanu viṣaya indriya saṃyoga jam sukham ānanda śabdasya mukhyaḥ arthaḥ sa katham yathā ukta ātmā eva syāt  na sa tahaṇaḥ api te saṃvedya tvāt  sārvabhauma upakramam ca uttarottara śataguṇa utkarṣa śśrūyamāṇa  ānandaḥ katham ātmā syāt  na hi sa eva tasmā chataguṇassyāt  janyaḥ ced ānandaḥ sādhana utkarṣāt utkṛṣyeta tasmāt na āca mukhyaḥ arthaḥ  grāhya iti ced  na eṣa doṣaḥ kūṭastha ātma svarūpa tve api ānandasya api anubhavasi eva bhrāntyā eva janyatva ādi prasiddhi upapatteḥ yathā pādhi janma nāśa bheda alpatva mahattva śuḍya śuddhi vedya tvāt ayaḥ  bodhe tabaune avivekāt  kalpyante yathā ca ākāśe—evam ānande pauti na kaścidirodhaḥ tathā hi śubha karmaṇā upasthāpite viṣaya viśeṣe tad indriya saṃyogā jāte antaḥkaraṇatti viśeṣe prasanne sati nirmala iva āda  mukham ātmā eva ānandaḥ prakaṭaubhavati tad diṣaya sukham iti prasiddha loke tasya sva abhivyacaka vaiśvarūpyāt eva vaiśvarūpyam tad avivekāt na svatas  aikarūpyāt  nanu eka rūpasya svayaṃjyotiṣaḥ anabhivyakti ayogāt  na anyat abhivyañjakam samasti satyam tathā api avidyayā anabhivyaktam iva atas  yad bhāve abhivyaktam iva tad tasya abhivyañcakam brūmaḥ atas tasmin śuddhe sukha ātmā pratibhāti aśuddhe na bhāti asukhavat ca bhāti yathā ādarśa śuddhe mukha rūpam śuddham bhāti aśuddhe na bhāti aśuddhavat ca bhāti rūpe bhāti api tad śuddhiḥ na bhāti bhinnā api bhedini bhāti api bhedaḥ  na bhāti abhinnaḥ api evam ātmani bhāti api ānandaḥ abhinnaḥ api na bhāti anā tmā api duḥkham bhāti aśuddhiḥ iva rūpasya atas antaḥkaraṇa śuddhatkarṣāt eva ānanda utkarṣaḥ ekatve api uttarottara utkarṣom ghaṭā kāśa maṭha ākāśa mahā kāśavat yojyam evam ca sati aśrotri yasya ca akāma hatasya iti akāma hatatva utkarṣāt uttarottara śataguṇam ānanda utkarṣaḥ śrayamāṇa  upapannaḥ  bhavati na anyathā tasmāt ātmā eva ānandaḥ anyathā mokṣaḥ apuruṣa artha ssyāt  sukha abhāvāt duḥkha abhāvāt pum artha iti ced  sukha abhāvāda pum arthaḥ api syāt  niravadya uttamaḥ pum arthaḥ  mokṣa iṣṭaḥ ma ca evam sati na syāt  yadi ātmā eva sukham tasya nitya prāpta tvāta na sukha prāptiḥ tava apauti ced  tarhi duḥkha prāpti abhāvāt ta nivṛttiḥ api na syāt  bhrāntyā duḥkham prāptam iva atas ta nittiḥ pum artha iti ced  sukham api aprāptam iva iti tad prāptiḥ pum arthaḥ hasta gata vismṛta suvarṇa prāptivat  yadi aprāpta prāptiḥ eva pum arthaḥ mokṣaḥ apum artha ssyāt  na hi mokṣaḥ aprāptaḥ prāpyate anityatva prasaṅgāt  tasmāt ātmā eva sukham priya tvāt ca ātmā eva sukham prasiddhaḥ  hi ātmā eva priyaḥ  loke śrutiḥ ca ātmā eva priyaḥ  na anya iti āha atat etad preyaḥ puttrāt ityādyā anyasya sarvasya ātma artha tvena priya tvam na tu svatas  aaātmanaḥ tu kāmāya sarvam priyam bhavati iti ca śrutiḥ sarvasya ātma artha tvena priya tvāt ca ātmā eva priyaḥ na hi tasmin  apriye tad arthaḥ priyaḥ  bhavet  na ca ātmā anya artha tvena priyaḥ ananya artha tvāt  anyasya ca ātmā artha tvāt arthitva anupapatteḥ yaḥ  hi anya arthom ghaṭaḥ saḥ arthaḥ  na dṛṣṭaḥ ghaṭa arthā mṛd ityādi api pum arthasya eva dāra darśanam strīpuṃsayoḥ api śarīram eva anya artham na tu ātmā na ca sukham tad artham ca mukkā anyat priyam prasiddham atas nanya artha tvāt  priya tvāt ca ātmā eva sukham na anyat  tasya anya artha tvena priyatva upapatteḥ tasmāt ātmā eva sukham yad artha marvam yad ca na anyātha tad sakham prasiddham sā ca pramidiḥ na ātmanaḥ anyatra mamastoti ātmā eva sukham daḥkham api na anya artham tathā api na tad artha kiṃcid apāditsyate vidhīyate vā śastra śyena ādi api ātmana smukha artha daḥkha parihāra artha vā na anya duḥkha mātra paryavasāyi duḥkha parihāraḥ api na anyārtha  iti ced  na sukha artha tvāt tasya bhāra ādi ārtānām tad nivṛttau viṣaya viśeṣa anuparakta ātma sukha abhivyakti dṛṣṭeḥ ata eva atra daḥkha nivṛtti vyatireka īraṇa anya dipaya rūpam apaśyantaḥ ātmanaḥ ca sukha tām ajānantaḥ sukham ca anubhavantaḥ  duḥkha nittiḥ eva sukha miti manyamānāḥ sarvatra sā eva sukham iti bhrāntāḥ kecid  nanu ātma artham sukham iṣṭam na tad artham eva tarhi ātmā eva iṣṭa taraḥ na hi tasmin  aniṣṭe tad artham iṣṭam syāt  ata ātmā eva mukhyam sukham itarat tad artha tvāt sukham atas amukhyam kim he sukhe staḥ mukhyam amukhyam ca bāḍham staḥ nanaktam kim na smarasi antaḥkaraṇatti viśeṣa ātma sukha abhi vyacake avivekāt  sukhatva bhramaḥ  lokasya buddhi vṛttau  iva bodha bhramaḥ vṛtti avivekāt ca tad armān sukha bodhayoḥ āropya sukham vedyam ātma artham jāyate bodhaḥ ca ityādi vyavahāra iti hi uktam atas asti mukhyam amukhyam ca sukham bodha iva amukhyam ca sukham abhipretya ana ha vai sa śarīrasya sataḥ priya apriyayoḥ apa hatiḥ asti aaśarauram vāva santam na priya apriye spṛśataḥ iti ā dyā aśru śśruti smṛtayaḥ paṇḍitāḥ ca kecid mokṣe sukha sya api abhāvam āhuḥ na punar mukhyam api tasya kūṭastha bodha ātma svarūpa tvāt  bhāva abhāva anupapatteḥ yathā ana pretya maṃjñāḥ ti ityādyā śrutiḥ amukhya bodha abhāva abhiprāya eva aavināśau vā are ayam ātmā ana hi draṣṭuṃdṛṣṭeviparilopaḥ  vidyate ityādi śrutibhyaḥ  yuktitaḥ ca bodha ātmanaḥ kūṭasthatva avagamāt  tasmāt sukham ātma artham iti prasiddheḥ amukhya sukha āśraya tvāta ātmanaḥ anya artha tā prasiddeḥ ca amukhya ātma āśraya tvāt ātmanaḥ  anya artha tāyāḥ  nirasta tvāt  ātmā na anyārthaḥ sarva ca ātmā artham sukham ca na anya artham sukha artham ca sarvam iti sukha ātmanoḥ lakṣaṇa abhedāt abheda eva iti siddham yadi tu ātma naḥ anyat  ātma artha sukham tad dedyam iṣyeta gṛha kṣetra ādivat  tad ā ātma āśrayam na bhāmeta bhāsate tu atha ucyeta amukhya sukha duḥkha ādivat  anātmā api sukham ātma āśrayam bhātauti tarhi vedya sukha abhyupagame api ātma artha sukham iti prasiddheḥ bhrānti mūlatva atyāgāt ātma nassukha rūpa tvam śruti yukti anubhava siddha na apalapanīyam tasmāt ātmā eva ānanda iti sthitam ata idam uktam ātma tvāt ānanda vigrahā anubhūtiḥ iti evam ca sati na eṣām padānām anyonya viruddha artha tvena amam gatiḥ āśaṅkanauyā avirodhena ekasmin  eka rase brahmaṇi saṃgateḥ darśita tvāt  evam sarvatra brahma vākyeṣu padānām aviraḥ dhena saṃgatiḥ draṣṭavyā mukhyeṣa ānanda ādiṣu vyutpannā āna nda ādi śabdāḥ samāna adhikaraṇa tayā yadā prayujyante tadā teṣām arthānām anyonya niyamya niyāmaka bhāvena avirodhena vyavasthitānām sarva pramāṇa agocarāt eka rasāt brahmaṇaḥ anyatra paryavasāna asaṃbhavāt tad eva lakṣayanti na tu abhidadhati śabdā iti apadārtha tvam abheda saṃsarga ātmaka vākya artha tvam śabda pramāṇa  katvam ca tasya iti ayataḥ  vācaḥ  nivartante aaupaniṣadam puruṣam iti ādi śāstram ca evam upapannātham bhavati tasmā chuti smṛti nyāya anubhava bala avaṣṭambhāt yathā uktam brahmā eva vastu na anyat  kiṃcid iti niścinumaḥ nanu yadi evam kā tarhi gatita prapañcasya pratyakṣa ādi viṣa yasya karma jñāna kāṇḍa āśrayasya atha ayam prapañcaḥ  na asti eva tadā pratyakṣa ādeniḥ viṣaya tvāt aprāmāṇyāta karma jñāna kāṇḍayoḥ āśraya asiddheḥ svarūpa asiddheḥ ca aprāmāṇyāta pratya kṣādeḥ ca prapañca antar pāti tvāt tad abhāve abhāvāt śruti smṛti nyāyānām ca svatas asiddheḥ na tabalāt  yathā ukta brahma vastu siddhiḥ atha etadopaparijihīrṣayā prapañcaḥ abhyupeyate tadā sa brahmaṇaḥ  bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ bhinna abhinnaḥ vā abhyupeyaḥ na anyathā na hi vastunaḥ prakāra cayam mulā anyathā siddhiḥ samasti avastu tve ca uktaḥ  doṣaḥ prasajyeta na hi dṛśṛṅga kha puṣpa ādinā avastunā yathā uktaḥ  vyavahārasmidhyet  vastu tve api prakāra traye api yathā uktam brahma na sidhyet  atas  prapañcasya bhāve abhāve api vedānta vākyebhyaḥ  yathā ukta brahma amiddheḥ tad arśana ādiṣṭa aniṣṭa prāpti parihārau  ātyantikau puṃsassidhyata iti ayuktam atas  mokṣa sya anyaḥ prakāra āśrayaṇīyaḥ na vā mokṣa iti atra ucyate na ekaḥ api doṣaḥ asmati akṣe prapañcasya māyā nirmitatva abhyupagamāt māyā āyāssa kāryāyā api vastu tvā avastu tvābhyām anirvacanīya tvāt vastu avastu pakṣa dvaya āśrayā doṣā na asmati akṣam kaṭākṣeṇa api vaukṣante tathā hi prapañcasya vastutva abhāvāt na advaita hāniḥ avastutva abhāvāt ca pratyakṣa ādya prāmāṇyādi ukta doṣa abhāvāt na yathā ukta brahma amitiḥ tad arśanāt ca māyā tad kārya nivṛtteḥ na mokṣām iddhiḥ nanu ani vacanauyām māyām nāma na jānaumaḥ jñāpayiṣyāmaḥ tām nanu vastutva abhāve prapañcasya pratyakṣa ādeḥ aprāmāṇyam syāt  tatas ca pūrva uktām marva eva doṣāḥ prādappyuḥ iti ced  vedam dṛṣṭam vastutva abhāve akṣaja ādeḥ aprāmāṇyam iti dṛśṛṅgā dau  iti ced  tad na avastutva abhāvāt prapañcasya avastu tvā bhāve api vastutva abhāvāt nṛśṛṅga māmyam ceta avastutva abhāvāt kim na vastu māmyam syāt  vastutva abhāve agrāmāṇyam svapna ādau dṛṣṭam iti ced  tvam eva tad yanirvacanīyam jānauṣe yatas  dṛśṛṅga ādi tyatvā vastutva avastutva hīnam svapna ādi udāharam i tad api vastu eva iti cetana tad yavastu tvam aprāmāṇya kāraṇam tad abhāve api aprāmāṇī adṛṣṭaḥ tad mithyā vastu iti ced  tad api vastu avastu vā ubhayathāpi taḥ dopaḥ syāt matam vastunau avivikte vastu vā vastu antarātmanā bhāma mānam mithyāvastu tad diṣayam jñānam apramāṇam iti ced  na tarhi pratyakṣa ādya prāmāṇya mata hipaya tvāt  atha uccata anirvacanauya artha tvāt svapna jñānam apramāṇam tathā jāgratā namapauti tad na bādhā bhāvāt  kim iti vā na pramāṇam svapna jñānam anirvacanauya artha tvāt jāgra jñānavat  bādhāt iti ced  tarhi bādhāt aprāmāṇyam na anirvacanauya artha tvāt kim ca tad aprāmāṇyam yad svam avajja agra jñānānām api sādhyate tad yadi bādha uttara kālam svarūpa tad kāryayoḥ abhāvaḥ sa iṣṭa eva atha prāk api abhāvaḥ sa svapne api na asti vastu yāthātmya bodhāt  bādhya tvam ced  tad apauṣṭam eva atha marvadā bādhaka bodha bhāvaḥ bodhāt prāk api bādhya tvam vā tabhayam svapne api na asti tasmāt yathā svapna prapañcasya anirvacanīya tve api śrā bodhāt  tad āśraya smarvaḥ  laukika vaidika kriyā kāraka pramāṇa  prameya ādi vyavahāraḥ apratihataḥ  vartate svāpnaiḥ eva nimittai stad prapañca nutsatya artha bodhaḥ  jāyate— evam jāgrati api marva maviruḍam draṣṭavyam nanu jāgrat prapañcasya bodhātyāk api mithyātva jñānāt na tayavahāraḥ  nyāyyaḥ svāpnasya tu mithyā tvā ajñānāt prāc prabodhāt  yuktaḥ tad yavahāra iti ced  na ayam doṣaḥ māyā maraucī udaka gandharvanagara vicandra diś moha ādi prati bhāmānām mithyātve avagate api prāc samyak bodhāt anivṛtti darśa na at nanu pratibhāsā anuvṛttau  api tatra tad nimittā pravṛttina syāta evam atra api tayā na bhāvyam matyam na asti eva atra mā tad pratibhāmam muttā svapna iva pratibhāmā anuttiḥ tu prāra bodhāt māyā ādiṣṭa pauccham i tasmāt svapnavat jāgrati api prāc baḥ dhānna virodhaḥ prapañca tadyavahāra pratibhāsasya kiṃtu daita satyatva abhiniveśa nimittāḥ pravṛttayaḥ tad mithyātva avagame na bhavanti eva tad mithyātva jñāna nimittāḥ tu pravṛttayaḥ  nittayaḥ ca bhavanti eva yāḥ tu pratibhāma mātra nimittāḥ tāḥ pūrvavat syuḥ eva loke api hi madhura ādiṣu tikta ādi pratibhāma hetavaḥ tad mithyā tu abodhe api pravṛtti nivṛtti viśeṣā dṛśyante tasmāt prapañca sya anirvacanīya tve jñāte api ā bodhāt  sarvaḥ  vyavahāra upapannaḥ tasmāt yathā ukta lakṣaṇa tve api anubhūteḥ svāvidyā māyā vyapāśrayeṇa samasta jagat atyatti ādi hetu tvena mahadā dyaśeṣa kārya vicitra vigraha tvāt pratyakṣa ādīnām karma upāsana ādi vākyānām ca viṣayatva upapattena virodha gandhaḥ api āśaṅkanauyaḥ tad etad āha— amahat ādi jagat māyā citra bhittim namāmi tām iti avyākṛtāt yad prathamam kārya jāyate ma mahān ma ādiḥ yasya tad mahat ādi mahat ādi ca tad jagaca iti mahat ādi jagat  tad ca māyā citram mahat ādi jagat māyā citram māyā iti mada mat tvābhyām anirvacanīyā avidyā ucyate nanu ucyate anirvacanīya iti ca vipratiṣiddham na ayam doṣaḥ mada mattvābhyām iti viśaṣaṇāt  mā hi yuktyā nirūpyamāṇā na astauti niścitya vaktam śakyā na api na astauti madam avilakṣaṇa tvena tad dacana ānahatvāt  tena anirvacanīyā na punar avācyā iti mada mattvābhyām iti viśeṣaṇam śrutavataḥ apauhaka codyam tava eva śobhate tayā māyayā nirmitam citram māyā citram citram iva citram tasya bhittiḥ iva bhittiḥ āśrayaḥ  yā anubhūtiḥ mā mahat ādi jagat māyā citrabhittiḥ citram cāyanīyam darśanīyam dṛśya miti arthaḥ dṛśyam anubhṛtya āśrayam iti tasya daumsthyam prakaṭayati mahasa kiraṇa āśrayam tamaḥ agni āśrayam śaitya mitivat  athavā citra vicitram nānā rūpam iti arthaḥ tasya eka rūpā anu bhṛtiḥ āśraya iti uktyā tad eva daussthyam draḍhayati ākāśā śraya yāḥ sparśa rū parama gandhāḥ rajju āśrayāḥ ca sarpa dhārā ṃīm bhūt chidra daṇḍa balauvarda mūtritatva ādaya itivat  yathā citra matyanta samāyām api bhittau  avidyamāna nimna unnata ādi bhramāna janayati evam eka rūpāyām api anubhūtau vikriyā viṣayatva bhedān ātmatva asukhitva pūrvā para antar bahis bhāva diś vibhāga atyuccā tinauca ādi bhramāna janayati iti jagat  citram iva citrabha yathā ca citram bhittim muvā pṛthak ātmānam na labhate tatra eva ca utpatti sthiti nāśān anubhavati–rāvam jagat apauti tad  citram citrasya apṛthakve api citra upādāna dravyam bhitteḥ pṛthak  ātmavat  na evam jaga citra upādānam iti āha māyā citram iti māyā hi anubhūteḥ pṛthatvā pṛthatvābhyām ani vacanauyā māyā nirmita tvam jagataḥ ‘māyām tu prakṛti vidyāt aindraḥ  māyābhiḥ puru rūpa īyate amāyā hi eṣā mayā mṛṣṭā ityādi śāstrebhyaḥ avagamyate yathā amatyam jñānam anantam brahma avijñānam ānandam brahma aavāyam puruṣa svayaṃjyotiḥ atam devāḥ  jyotiṣām jyotiḥ ana tatra sūryaḥ aya ātmā ajaraḥ amaraḥ amṛtaḥ abhayaḥ ana jāyate mriyate vā aanyadeva tad iditāt aetat aprameyam dhruvam aanantam apāram vijñāna ghana eva atattvam asi aaham brahmā asmi aayam ātmā brahma aepa ta ātmā aānandaḥ  brahma iti vyajānāt iti ādi śāmbebhyaḥ  yathā ukta lakṣaṇam brahma avagatam evam tasya māyā vyapāśrayam eva jagat sraṣṭra tvam bahu rūpa tvam ca avagantavyam śāstra balāt  anyathā avaita virodhāt ca tasmāt māyā nirmitam jagat iti siddham nanu siddhe arthe katham śāstrasya prāmāṇyam śṛṇa pramiti utpatteḥ maṃśaya ādi abhāvāt ca prapañcitam ca etad  pramāṇa vṛtta nirṇaye bhittiḥ iva bhittiḥ anubhūtiḥ yathā citrasya bhitti smākṣāt na upādānam na api maha jam citram tasyāḥ na api avasthā antaram mṛda iva ghaṭa ādiḥ na api guṇa antara āgama āmrasya iva rakta tā ādiḥ na ca asyāḥ civa janma ādau janma ādiḥ citrāt prāgavam ca bhāvāt  yadi api bhittim vinā citram na bhāti tathā api na mā citram vinā na bhāti iti evamādi anubhṛti bhitti jaga citrayoḥ yojyam citrabhittim iti dvitīyā prayogaḥ kalpita prapañca eva devatā namaskāra āt eviṣaya iti darśayitum devatā namaskāra śiṣṭa ācāra paripāla na artham maṅgala ācaraṇam vighna upaśāntya devatā guru bhaktyoḥ vā jñāna prāptau  antaraṅga tvam darśayitum — yasya deve parā bhaktiḥ yathā deve tathā garaḥ  tasya ete kathitā hi arthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ iti mantra varṇāt  garīḥ ca devatā aikyāt  pṛthaṅgamamkāraḥ atra na kṛtaḥ pradarśana artha tvāhā atra ayathā deve tathā garau iti vacanāt dā vācanikaḥ  namaskāraḥ tulya eva kṛtaḥ virodha abhāvāt bahis eva vā guru namaskāraḥ kṛtaḥ granthāt  devatā namaskāraḥ tu mamamta vedānta artham āramaṃgrahasya asya prakaraṇamya atha parām devatām aupaniṣadam puruṣam saṃkṣepataḥ  darśayitum sukha avabodha artha granya ādau  eva kṛtaḥ tatra eva ma śobhata iti brahma avidyā nimitta tvāt  maṃmārasya vedāntoti brahma vidyayā nivṛtti upapatteḥ mākṣaḥ prayojanam vedāntānām viṣayaḥ  brahma ananya sādhāraṇa tvāt  tati atipādya tvāt ca brahmaṇaḥ  vedāntānām ca pratipādya pratipādaka lakṣaṇa ssaṃbandhaḥ tāni eva prayojanā dauni prakaraṇasya api tad artha nirṇaya artha tvāt tad artha nirṇa yā artha tvam ca nyāyaiḥ artha ābhāma jñāna nirāsena samyak artha jñāna dṛḍhau karaṇāt śārīrakavat  na punar anirṇaya hetu tvāt dedāntānām na ca śārīrakeṇa asya gata artha tvam codyam tad prakaraṇa tvāt tad evam prayojana ādimad prakaraṇam nanu idam ādau vaktavyam śrotṛ pravṛtti aṅga tvāt matyam uktam eva kim tu na mi aṣṭam tad eva atra spaṣṭokriyate mukti bandhayoḥ vidyā vidyā nimitta tve pratipādita eva tatmi aṣṭīkaraṇasya sukara tvāt  nanu mada mattvābhyām anirvacanīyā avidyā kāryam anirvacanīyam nāma kiṃcid pam idam na eva loke asti yadi syāt  tabat jagat api anirvacanīyam iti pratijñāyeta na tu asti atha uccata śukti rajata māyā ādi tad  pramiimiti tad ca na tasya api asti na asti iti vā khyāte nirvacanīyatā prasiddhā ata eva tad sat eva iti kecid  asadevati anye tatasmat  amadeva vā tasya api kāraṇam na anirvacanīyam na ca avidyā kāraṇam na hi sadamatoḥ tad kāraṇayaḥ ravidyātvam avidyā ca bhrānti jñānam na tu anyā pramiḍya bhāvāt  bhrāntiḥ ca na rūpya kāraṇam aprasiddheḥ tad viṣaya tvāca kāraṇa tve tad diṣayatva ayogāt yati yahiṣayam jñānam na tad  tad kāraṇam yathā śukti jñānam bhrānteḥ ca na anirvacanīya tvam bādhasya api abhāvāt bhrānteḥ ca kāryatvāt  tātkāraṇam avidyā iti ced  tad na karaṇa doṣa kārya tvāt hāntaḥ na ca doṣaḥ avidyā anirvacanīyaḥ vā atas  na avidyā anirvacanīyā prasiddhā na api tad kāryam tasmāt nirvacanīya avidyā kāryam anirvacanīyam jagat iti ayuktam iti amāyām tu prati vidyāt iti ādau  api māyā śabdasya na anirvacanīyaḥ arthaḥ vyutpatti abhāvāt  na eṣa doṣaḥ ukta lakṣaṇasya śukti rajata ādeḥ prasiddha tvāt  tad katham iti ced  śṛṇa tad sa vicāram śrāvayiṣyāmaḥ rajatam bhāti yad dhāntau tad sadeke pare tvamat  anye anirvacanīyam tadāhuḥ tena vicāryate paśna traye api yuktaurāha sukha pratipatti artham amataḥ khyāti ayogāt sat dādhā yogāt asat sataḥ atas anirvacanīyam tad iti pakṣeṣu yuktayaḥ asataḥ  nṛśṛṅga ādeḥ pratibhāmām aṃbhavāt  pratibhāmamāna tvāt ca idam rajatam mad ityādye pakṣe yuktiḥ yadi kaścid rūyāt  nṛśṛṅgam api tad śabdāt bhātauti tasya api na tad  rūpyavat bhāti na hi nari śṛṅgam bhāti gavauva na ca bhāti api vikalpa mātra tvāt  tad pratyayasya tad aktam aśabda jñāna anupātau vastu śūnyaḥ  vikalpaḥ iti katham cāmataḥ  bhāti bhāsyata iti vā kartṛ tvam karma tvam vā atas amataḥ khyāti asaṃbhavāt khyāteḥ ca idam na asat  rūpyam mad eva tu satya rūpyavat  khyāteḥ eva sataḥ  bādhā yogāt  satya rūpya ādivat  bādhāt ca idam rūpyam na asat  atas asat eva iti dvitīye pakṣe yuktiḥ amataḥ khātya yogāt  mataḥ  bādhā yoga ādityābhyām yuktibhyā manirvacanīyam khyāte mata bādhāt  na mad iti tatra mati akṣamvidhā bhinnaḥ ātma khyātiḥ akhyātiḥ anyathā khyātiḥ iti tatra ādyam madhepataḥ darśayati adṛṣṭa tvāt amat khyātesmad khyātethā eva darśanāta idam ca rūpyam mad khyāteḥ bāhya tvasya eva bādhataḥ rūpya ābādhāt ca yukteśra tāvatā bhrānti bādhayoḥ rūpyam etad vadanī eke dhaurūpam vāmanāmayam mad idam rūpyam khyāteḥ matyarūpyavat iti anumānam athavā idam nāmat rūpyam akhyāna abhāvāt akhyāna vyāptam hi amat tvam dṛśṛṅga ādau atas  vyāpaka ākhyāna abhāvā dyāpyāmattva abhāvaḥ akhyāna abhāvaḥ ca tad viruḍa khyāti dṛṣṭa riti vyāpaka ākhyāna virudva khya ati liṅgakam anumānam rūpyasya mattva abhāve atas  khyāteḥ eva nāmata mad iti vā miham nanu na idam rajatam iti bādhāt  na rūpyasya mad tvam yuktam na ayam doṣaḥ bāhya tvasya eva bādhataḥ rūpya ābādhāca na idam iti hi bahis iva bhātaḥ rūpyasya bāhya tā mātra bādhyate na tu rūpyam api na hi na idama na rajatam iti ca bādhaḥ atas  rūpyasya mad tvam na virudhyate itatha– ayuktaṃtra tāvatā bhrānti bādhayoḥ tāvatā eva kapyasya bāhyatva mātra bādhena bhrānti bādhayaḥ  rūpya bādham vinā yuktaḥ upapatteḥ ghaṭa māna tvāt  rūpyasya api bādham parikalpya tasyāmattva kalpa na anupapatteḥ na hi ekasya eva bādhena iṣṭe siḍe iyoḥ bādha kalpanā nyāyyā kalpanā gauravāt rūpyam yā eva bādhaḥ astu iti ceta tad na dharmi bādhe bāhyatva dharmasya api bādhāt  vayoḥ bādha prasaṅgāt  atas  bāhya tā eva bādhyate na rūpyam atas ati eva tad  taca dhiya eva rūpam vāsanā kṛtam itye ke vadanti anye amataḥ khyāti ayogāt sat saṃvitti virodhataḥ nāma khyāti ranāśvāma at na ani athā ākhyātiḥ api amau idaṃdhaurakṣa jā rūpyadhau matim tad pramopataḥ dopāt idam rūpyam iti bhrāntim tad avivekataḥ anye tu evam vadanti iti anupaṅgaḥ katham na iyam rūpya khyāti rasa khyātiḥ amataḥ khyātya maṃbhavāt  madrapyam idam iti maṃvicyā virodhāt ca amadrapyam iti vadataḥ yathā rūpye khyāti hastī khyātauti vadatas  rū pyam aṃvidirodhaḥ amataḥ  api mattvena khyāti saṃbhave anyatra api anāśvāmāt mad  mattvena khyātī iti api niścayaḥ  na syāt  atas  na asat khyātiḥ anānyathā khyātiḥ apyamau ata eva maṃvidirodha ādeḥ tathā hi śuktī rūpya ātmanā khyātauti vadataḥ  rūpyam aṃvidirodhaḥ anyatra api rūpya ādi khyātau  anyathā ākhyātim aṃbhavādanāśvāsaḥ niścayaḥ śakta rūpya ātma tvasya amataḥ khyāti prama ṅgaḥ tasmāt na anyathā ākhyātiḥ na ātma khyātiḥ apyata eva bāhyamaṃvi virodhāt  abāhye bāhya khyātivat abadau buddhi khyātim aṃbhavā dana āśvāsāta bāhya tvasya asataḥ khyāti prasaṅgāt ca ani vacanauyam rūpyam sattvena khyāti iti vadataḥ sat saṃvitti virodhāt  anyathā ākhyāta auṣṭaḥ ca anāśvāmāta amataḥ sattvasya khyāti pramagāva anirvacanīyasya khyātiḥ api na iyam evam sarvatra pakṣa antara nirāsaḥ  yojyaḥ kā tamusyā gatiḥ ucyate he ete dhiyau na ekā eva tatra idam iti akṣa jā puras avasthita śaktī dam aṃśa viṣayā rūpyadhau smṛtiḥ mādṛśyādi uddodhita saṃskāra mātraja tvāta kāraṇa antara agrahaṇāt tasyāḥ ca kā karaṇa doṣa balāt pramuṣita smaraṇa abhimāna tvāt  smṛtitva anabhivyaktaḥ śukteḥ ca viśeṣa agrahaṇāt  tayoḥ idaṃrūpya grahaṇa smaraṇayoḥ nira ntara utpannayoḥ avivekāt idam rūpyam iti ekatva jñāne mām ā na adhi karaṇyena anutpanne api atpanna iva vyavaharati lokaḥ tena idaṃrūpya jñāne yathārthe adhyayathārtha vyavahāram avivikte pravartayata iti te eva avivikte bhrāntiḥ iti āhuḥ akhyātiḥ apaudṛśyā iva bhrāntiḥ na jñāna haunā suṣuptasya bhrānti tvāt  yathā ca anyepām ayathārtha jñānam bhrāntau yuktam evam ayathārtha vyavahāraḥ asmākam ayathārtha jñāna abhyupagame ca uktaḥ  doṣaḥ na asmad pakṣe kaścid doṣaḥ na idam rajatam iti bādhaḥ katham iti ced  saḥ api akhyātim eva nudan śukti rūpya vivekena anyathā vyavahāram nivartayati na tu ayathārtha khyāti prāptām tad prāpteḥ nirasta tvāt tasmāt yad yathā ākhyāti tad tathā asya iva iti sthitam ekānta mattve abhra anta tvāt asattve khyāti am aṃbhavāt  śaktim svābhāva rūpya ātmā bhāti iti anye tu atiṣṭhipan yad yathā khyāti tad tathā eva asti ced  na tad khyāti tiḥ bhrāntiḥ anyathā atipramaṅgāt  nanu yathārtha khyātyoḥ api ayathārtha vyavahāra hetu tvāt bhrānti tvam uktam tad ruktam na hi ayathārtha vyavahāra hetu tvam yathārtha tve khyāti ossākṣāt saṃbhavati anyāmām iva anayoḥ api pāramparyeṇa ced  anayoḥ iva anyāmām api tad saṃbhavāt bhrāntitva pramaṅgaḥ anyāmām yathārtha vyavahāra hetu tvāt abhrānta tvam na anayoḥ tad abhāvāt iti ced  tarhi ayathārtha tā anayoḥ abhyupeyā yathārtha tve asyāḥ  vyavasthāyāḥ kaḥ  hetuḥ smṛti grahaṇa aviveka iti ced  mmṛtesmatyāḥ kaḥ avivekaḥ  grahaṇāt  nanu uktam smaraṇa abhimāna pramopāt aviveka iti kim maḥ abhimā naḥ smṛtemasvarūpam eva uta anyaḥ svarūpam ceta tad abhāve smṛteḥ eva abhāvaḥ anyaḥ ced  tad abhāve smṛte vivekaḥ atiprasaṅgāt  atha ucyeta na jñānayoḥ avivekaḥ kiṃtu tad arthayoḥ avivekaḥ  vyavasthā hetuḥ iti kaḥ arthayoḥ avivekaḥ yadi kānā jñānam tarhi sarva jñānānām bhrānti tvam na hi kenacid api jñānena kāsyena arthaḥ  jñāyate atas  yathārtha tve khyātyoḥ na ayathārtha vyavahāra hetu tvam nyāyyam atha ucyeta idam rajata miti sāmānādhikaraṇya jñāne anutpanne api utpannābhi mānāt  pravṛttiḥ tṛtīyam vā māmānādhikaraṇya jñānam mānasamamti atas  vā pravṛttiḥ iti tarhi ayathārtha jñānā bhyupagamāt  tvayā uktā doṣāḥ tava eva pramajyante tṛtīyam ca jñānam ayathārtham icchana kim iti na adya ye tathacchami akṣasya yathārthatva artham mānam asya ayathārtha tve api avi rodhāt  yadi akṣa ādīnām yathārthatva niyamaḥ  na syāt  tadā loka vyavahāre dṛṣṭa arthe maṃbhavati api vede yathārthatva niścayā bhāvāt  adṛṣṭa arthā prattiḥ na syāt  atas akṣaja ādaunām yamya yā amādhāraṇā mām agrau tasyāḥ  yathārtha nāna janaka tvam eva atas  vedasya api yathā artha jñāna janakatā eva svabhāvena apramāṇa  jñānam tu anya nimittam iti vyavasthāpayitum ādyayaḥ yathārthatva micchāmi catara ādaunām hi pramāṇa apramāṇa jñānam ādhā raṇa tve na ayam niyamasmidhyeta manamamta mādhāraṇa tve api ātmavat avirodha iti ced  evam api mamatena ayathārtha tve kaścidirodhaḥ apramāṇam āmagraujanya tvāt  tathā bhrāntaḥ na hi pramāṇa apramāṇa dhiyossāmagrī tulyā cakṣara ādaunām tad antaḥpāti tve api dopa upetam haundriyam bhrānte hetuḥ śuddha tu abhra antaḥ manaḥvat  vedamya tvadoṣa tvāt sva śatyā mamyak dhā ojanaka tā eva bhrāntiḥ tu śabda śakti aparijñānāt  pratyakṣa ādi virodha āśaṅkayā vā puruṣasya jāyate na tu śabdāt  atas anya pakṣe api adṛṣṭa artha prahatteḥ avirodhāt  pratauti nyāya viruddham bādhaka an anurūpamakhyāti pakṣam mā cauklapaḥ bhrāntau dṛṣṭasya anyatra yojanāt anāśvāma anālambanatā ca akhyāti pakṣe api mamānaḥ daḥ ghama damattvābhyām bhrāntya bhrānti vivekaḥ ced  maḥ anya pakṣe api tulyaḥ doṣaḥ  hi iṣṭam kārya nirundhana viparītam ca kurvan dṛśyate na ca de pābhāve api agraha āśaṅkā nivṛttiḥ na hi kāraṇa bhāve kārya bhavati eva doṣa abhāva liṅgena pratyakṣā saṃvid anumeyā syāt  tava viparyaya abhāvaḥ tu doṣa abhāvena yuktaḥ anumātum hetu abhāve phala abhāvāt na ca anāśvāmaḥ arthe jñāyamāne tad jñāna virodhāt anyatas api jñānāt eva ced artha āśvāsaḥ tad anyā iva na ca anyasya viśeṣaḥ na ca dābhyām jñānā bhyām artha āśvāmaḥ na api bahubhyaḥ na api artha kriyā jñānāt arthā śvāmaḥ vyabhicārasya mamānatvāt  na ca vyabhicārā daprāmāṇyama jñānasya pramāṇa phalasya paricchitteḥ bhāvāta tāvāt eva prāmāṇyam na avyabhicārāt  mita amita ādi vyabhicāriṇām api akṣāṇām tanāve prāmāṇyāt  tad abhāve dhamasya avyabhicārasya api aprāmāṇyāta na ca phala bhāve api vyabhicārāt aprāmāṇyam kvacid ṛṣṭam prameyatva ādeśvā prāmāṇyam phala abhāvāt eva na vyabhicārāt  phala abhāvaḥ ca hetu abhāvāt  avyabhicārāt hi liṅgāt phalam atas  vyabhicāraḥ liṅgatva hetuḥ prameyatva ādeḥ na tu bādhakavat prāmāṇya upaghātī vyabhicāriṇām api akṣāṇām prāmāṇyāt  jñānam ca akṣavat eva pramāṇam na liṅgavat  na ca niścite arthe vyabhicārāt  saṃśayaḥ niścita iva sthāṇau  ardhva tvena utpattyā eva ca jñānasya niścaya ātmakatva anna aniścayaḥ  yuktaḥ aniścaya ātmaka tvam tu na iha adhikṛtam avyabhicārāt artha āśvāsam icchataḥ tu anā śvāsa eva avyabhicāra jñāne api anāśvāsāt taḍyasiddhā vyabhicāram na ātmani anyatra vā āśvāsa hetuḥ jñāna antarā siddhau anavamthā kiṃca jñānāt ced na artha āśvāmaḥ tad amidyau kena mahāvyabhicāraḥ  jñānasya gṛhyeta vyabhicāraḥ api katham midhyeta jñānasya āmādhaka tve mādhaka tve tad eva arthasya api mādhakam astu vyarthaḥ avyabhicāraḥ tasmāt khyāteḥ yathārthatva niyama abhāve api anāśvāma ādi dopābhāvāt yathārthatva agrahaḥ vyarthaḥ atas  yathārtha tve khyāteḥ bhrāntitva ayogāt yad khyāti tad asti eva iti niyantum na śakyam tarhi sa na asya iva na ca na asti eva amattve khyāti ama bhavāt  tasmāt śaktimmataḥ  mad antara rūpya ātmanā khyāti iti bhyapeyam na ca evam sati abhrā ntitvam khyāteḥ yathā khyāti tathā na asti yatas  na api śūnya khyāti prasaṅgaḥ grakārasya atuccha tvāt  rūpyasya mattvāt  rūpya prakāga ca śuktiḥ khyāti nanu śuktaḥ prakārasya ca mattve śuktiḥ yathā bhāti tathā na astauti katham brūdhe śṛṇu rūpyasya śuktya bhāva tvāt  rūpyam hi śuktara bhāvaḥ bhāva antarasya eva abhāva tvāt  uktam hi— abhāva antaram abhāvaḥ anyaḥ  na kaścid nirūpaṇāt iti tammācśuktau rūpya ātmanā na asti iti ucyate atas  iyoḥ sattve api śuktiḥ sva ātmanā samyak khyāteviṣayaḥ bhrānteḥ tu svābhāva rūpya ātmanā iti vyavasthā ata āha aśuktiḥ svābhāva rūpya ātmā bhāti iti atas  na mad eva na api śūnyam eva bhātauti bhrāntiyujyate asmad pakṣe bādhaḥ  api bhrāntyā prāptām śukta rūpya ātma tām bādhamāna eva upapanna iti anye tu atiṣṭhipan sthāpitavanta iti arthaḥ sarvathā nāmat idam rūpyam na anirvacanīyam api tu mad eva iti prāptam atra abhidamahe mattve na bhrānti bādhau mtām nāmattve khyāti bādhakaḥ  bhadamajhyāma nirvācyā vidyā vedyaiḥ maha bhramāḥ mattve śukti rūpyasya tad dauna bhrāntim syāta mati arūpyadhau riva tahat eva ca na asyāḥ  bādhaḥ amattve tu nṭa śṛṅgavat tasya na khyātiḥ atas  na bhrānti bādhau syātām na ca tau na sta eva sarva jantu pramidda tvāt marvavādibhiḥ ceṣṭa tvāt yadi kaścid rūyāttau na icchāmauti tasya prasiddhi virodhaḥ mā bhrāntiḥ iti ced  na bādhā bhāvāt  tadā adhikān yuktim api vannauti ced  tarhi iccham i bhrānti bādhau mā atas tad dā dhikām yuktim vocaḥ aniṣṭa pramagāt  kā ca tā nimi cchataḥ tadā adhikā yuktiḥ nanu rūpyasya mattve amattva ca na bhrānti bādhau masta iti avocaḥ na ca mad amat tvam virodhāt  na ca prakāra antaram asti atas tad pramiddhi nirmūla iti ced  tad na madamat tvābhyām anirvacanauyā vidyā ātmakatva abhyupagamāt rūpya tad jñānayoḥ tathā hi khyāte sat  bādhāt  na mad iti anyonya pakṣam nirākurvadbhi dibhiḥ eva rūpyasya anirvacanīya tvam sthāpitam ata eva tajñānasya api na hi jeyasya nirvācya tve tajñānasya nirvacanīya tvam nyāyyama tad jñānatva hānāt jñāna antaravat jñānasya ca nirvācya tve jñeyasya api tathā tvam syāt  anya jñāna jñeyavat  atamtayoḥ anirvacanīya tvam siddham kādā citka tvāt ca tayoḥ kāraṇam mṛgyam na ca nimitta kāraṇa mātrāt kāryam iddhiḥ ata upādānam ca mṛgyam na ca asati asya mākṣāt satyam upādānam dṛṣṭam matyā upādāna tve ca ghaṭa ādivat satya tvam māna gamya tvam ca syāt  tad ca na iṣṭam ata stad anurūpam anirvacanīyam eva upādānam eṣṭavyam tad ca na anyada jānāt  anādi mamasti na ca mā ādeḥ upādāna tā ananvayāt anavasthānāca nanu bhrāntiḥ eva ajñānam tasyāḥ  ajñānatva pramiddheḥ na hi bhrāntim aṃśayau mutvā anyasya marvamāna atigasya at na ānatā pramiddhiḥ kāraṇa tā vā maṃbhāvyā atas  bhrāntiḥ eva bhrānti antara kāraṇam tasyāḥ  api anyā tasyāḥ  api anyā iti anādi tvāt hāntaunām eva bhrānti tad saṃskārāṇām vā boja aṅkurava kārya kāraṇa tā yogāt na anyat kalpyam iti ced  tad na ana nu aya ādinā ukta uttara tvāt  na hi kāryasya kārya antare anvayaḥ piṇḍasya iva ghaṭe ananvitam ca na upādānam piṇḍa iva ghaṭasya yā tu anvitā mṛt sā eva upādānam piṇḍādaunāma na tu te anyonyasya evam bhrāntim aṃśaya tad saṃskārāṇām api kāryatve na anyonya upādāna tā yad tu teṣu āgama apāyiṣu nu eti tad eva teṣām upādānam ajñānam tasya bhāve teṣām bhāvāt abhāve ca abhāvāt  kāraṇa bhāve api abhāvaḥ  mṛt kārye api tulyaḥ saṃskāra ādi kārye api tasmāt bhāva eva bhavati na abhāva iti niyamaḥ na tu bhāve bhavati eva iti anyathā kāraṇe nitye kāryam api nityam syāta tad bhāve bhāva niyamāt  kārye tu anitye kāraṇam api anityam syāt  tad bhāva eva bhāvāt  ubhayathā api eka kāla tvāt tayoḥ na kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ puṃmoḥ śṛṅgayoḥ iva ca nanu kārya kṣaṇāt pūrvakṣaṇe kāraṇasya bhāva anna eka kāla tā tayoḥ iti cet–kim tad  pūrvakṣaṇa eva asti uta kārya kṣaṇe api yadi kārya kṣaṇe api tad bhāve api na syāt kāryam pūrvakṣaṇe abhāvāt  pūrvakṣaṇa eva ced  na syāt kāryam tad bhāve api tu abhāva eva atas  na tad  tad kāryam tad abhāve bhāvāt  tad bhāve abhāvāt ca atha tad abhāvaḥ kāraṇam tad  akāraṇam syāt  tad kārya bhāve api tad abhāva anivṛtteḥ kārya kāraṇe saha api astām kārya abhāve api tad kāraṇa abhāvā nivṛtteḥ kāraṇa bhāve api kārya abhāva iṣṭassyāt  tasmāt bhāvasya kāraṇa tve api kāraṇa bhāve kārya syāt eva iti niyama um na asti na ca abhāvasya kāraṇa tā iti vakṣyāmaḥ tathā sat api kāraṇam kārya kāle pūrva ca yadi syāt  tadā sati eva kāraṇe kāyem bhavati iti niyamaḥ na tu sati bhavati eva iti pūrvakṣaṇe kāryasya abhāvāt  kāraṇa bhāve api atha pūrvakṣaṇa eva asti kāraṇam na kārya kāle tadā api na kāraṇe sati kārya bhavati eva iti niyamaḥ kāraṇa kāle kāryasya abhāvāt  asati eva tu kāraṇe kārya syāt  kārya kāle tasya abhāvāt  ata dbhāva bhāvi tvāt ca tayoḥ na kārya kāraṇa bhāva ssyāt  nanu pūrvasmin  uttarasmin  ca kṣaṇe tayoḥ bhāva eva kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tad bhāva bhāvi tvam ca tad eva na tu eka kāla tā atas  kṣaṇikasya eva kāraṇa tā nyāyyā nityasya tu kāraṇa tve pūrva uttara kṣaṇayoḥ tasya viśeṣa abhāvāt kramānupapatta rekasmi na iva āṇe marva kārya jananāt uttarakṣaṇe artha kriyā bhāva ādama lakṣaṇa tvac ram aṅgāt iti ced  tad na pramiḍḍi virodhāt  tathā hi yasmin mati yad bhavati amati ca na bhavati te kārya kāraṇe iti pramiḍdiḥ tayaḥ bhinna kālatā eva iti vadataḥ  virudhyate atadbhāva bhāvi tvam eva tad bhāva bhāvi tvam iti ca vadataḥ śabda artha prasiddhi virodhaḥ ca kṣaṇika tvam ca kāraṇa āde vadataḥ anyathā prasiddhi virodhaḥ na hi tvad kutarkān upahata mataunām kasyacid lāṇika tā pramiḍā kim punar  kāraṇasya neka kārya anuyāyinaḥ na ca marva loka pramiddi virodhena kiṃcid kvacid bodhayitum śakyam tasmāt kārya kāraṇa ādi bhāva micchatā ma yathā prasiddhaḥ tathā abhyupeyaḥ nāmau śiṣyaḥ nityasya kāraṇatva ayogāt tad prasiddhiḥ bādhya iti ced  na bādhyā kṣaṇikasya eva tad ayogāt  tathā hi kṣaṇikam ced kāraṇam tasya pūrva uttara kṣaṇayoḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt kārya ced tatas  bhavet  madā bhavet  na ced  na kadācid  nanu pūrva uttaraṣkṣaṇayaḥ stasya abhāvāt tad kṣaṇe ca bhāvāt  tadā viśeṣaḥ asti bhāvaḥ tarhi tad kāryam api tadā eva bhavet  tadā eva viśeṣa bhāvāt  tadā tad kāryam tad kārya ca tadā eva iti na utta rakṣaṇa bhāvi kiṃcid kāryam syāt  uttarakṣaṇaḥ api pūrvakṣaṇa kārya ced  tadā eva bhavet  na ced  pūrva apara bhāvaḥ  bhāvayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva iti ayuktam nanu na pūrva apara bhāva mātrāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kim tu pūrva apara kālayoḥ bhāvāt  kālayoḥ tu na pūrva apara kālayoḥ bhāvaḥ kālasya kāla antara abhāvāt atas  na anayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva iti ced  tarhi na kālasya kālataḥ paurvāparyam na api deśata iti apūrva aparatvāt kālasya tad saṃbandhinaḥ  vayoḥ api na paurvāparyam iti pūrva aparaṣkṣāṇayaḥ rbhāvaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  bhāvayoḥ pūrva uttaraṣṭāṇayoḥ bhāvaḥ  na amita madhye ca amtotya ādi uktara yukta tvāt yad bhavati tad bhavati eva yad na bhavati tad na bhavati eva iti na kadācid amtunaḥ anyathā abhāva iti vācyam syāt  nanu eta codyam anyasya api tulyam na tulyam bhavata eva prasiddhim tyatā sūkṣma īkṣikām prakurvatam ta dṛpaṇam syāt  na tu anyasya yathā prasiddha kārya kāraṇa bhāvam bhyupagacchataḥ nanu eka kāla tve sati ayam kārya kāraṇayoḥ dopa msyāt  tad ca na asti kāraṇa kṣaṇa āyatta rakṣaṇa kārya syāt  atas  na ayam doṣa iti ced  satyam kim tu anyaḥ  doṣam syāt  tathā hi kāraṇa abhāve ced kārya syāt  kāraṇa kṣaṇāt pūrvaḥ  ttarakṣaṇeṣu sarveṣu eva syāt  viśeṣa abhāvāt na ca prāga bhāva pradhvaṃsa abhāvayoḥ viśeṣaḥ abhāva tvāt viśeṣavat tve ca bhāvatva prasaṅgaḥ viśeṣaḥ api abhāvaḥ ced  kaḥ  viśeṣaḥ tayoḥ bhāvaḥ ced  katham bhāvaḥ abhāva dharma ssyāt  viśeṣavat tve api bhāvayoḥ kāraṇasya viśeṣa abhāvāt pūrva uttara kālayoḥ tad kārya mad eva syāta atas ca tad avyāpta kāla abhāvāt na tasya kiṃci kārya syāt  tad kāraṇa kāle syāt iti ced  tad na tasya tadā abhāvāt  bhāve tad kāraṇam api tad saṃbandhi bhavet  tadā na prathamam api kārya syāt  kutaḥ dvitīyam atas ta kārya kāryam eva na kasyacid kāraṇam evam tad kāraṇam api kārya ced  na kāraṇam tad kāraṇam tad kāraṇam api evam eva iti akāryam eva kāraṇam na kāryam iti ata ekasya eva nityasya kāraṇasya anekāni kāryāṇi krama bhāvauni yāvanti vā kāryāṇi tāvantyakāryāṇi nityāni kāraṇāni kramavat  kārya kartṛṇi abhyupagantavyāni syuḥ tatas ca kāraṇa bhāve kārya bhavati eva iti niyamaḥ  na syāt  kāryasya kārya antara abhāvāt mattvāt tad kāraṇasya api asattva prasaṅgāta artha kriyā kārī eva sat  iti eṣā api paribhāṣā tyājyā syāt  tasmāt  kṣaṇikatat kāraṇa tvayoḥ aprasiddha tvāt ayukta tvāt ca nitya tad kāraṇa tvayoḥ sarva jana pramiyoḥ bādhā yogāt nityasya eva kāraṇa tvam anapavādam sthitam kiṃca kṣaṇikayoḥ ced  kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ kāraṇān anva yāt  kāryasya prāk utpatteḥ atyantāmattvāt pūrva uttara kālayaḥ  viśeṣe asati tad kim tadā eva jāyate na punar anyadā kadā cit  sadā vā tadā eva kāraṇa bhāvāt anyadā ca abhāvāt iti ceta tad na kāraṇa bhāve abhāve ca tasya asataḥ aviśeṣāt  katham ca asataḥ kāraṇa saṃbandhaḥ asaṃbandhasya ca katham kāraṇa tā kāryasya ca kāraṇa saṃbandhaḥ  na prāgabhāvasya tasya akāraṇa tvāt sidasya ced kāraṇa saṃbandhaḥ prāviśeṣa abhāvāt yadā kadācid  sadā vā sidhyet  siddhasya ca kim kāraṇena yadi prāk api kāraṇa saṃbandhaḥ asti saṃbandhi api asti na hi tena vinā saṃbandhaḥ asataḥ ced kāraṇam aṃbandhaḥ na sataḥ kāryasye tyakāraṇam eva tad syāt  kārya saṃbandhāt ced kāraṇam kāryam iddheḥ prāṅga kāraṇam astauti na tena maṃbandhaḥ prāk api kārya maṃbandhaḥ asti ced  kāryam api astauti na tad  kṣaṇikam syāt  kāraṇam ca kāryam aṃbandhāt kāraṇam kāraṇa saṃbandha āca kārya miti itaretara āśraya tā ca tayoḥ atha akāraṇena eva prāk u tpatteḥ saṃbandhaḥ saḥ anyadā api mamastauti anyadā api kārya syāt  yad saṃbaī mad  kāraṇībhavet  tena saṃbandhe kārya syāt iti ced  sarvam eva tathā syāt  na vā kiṃcita viśeṣa abhāvāt na hi atyantān anvitānām kṣaṇānām atyanta vilakṣaṇānām kasyacid kenacid eva maṃbandhe viśeṣa ssaṃbhavet  pūrva apara tā viśeṣa iti ced  tathā api ayam eva asmā dapara iti viśeṣa abhāvādyatas kutaścit aparatva saṃbhavāt anyadā api kārya syāt  pūrva uttara kṣaṇa bhāvitva mātreṇa kārya kāraṇa niyame pūrvakṣaṇa bhāvi sarvam utta rakṣaṇa bhāvinam marvasya yad kim cit dā yasya kasyacid  ekaikasya vā sarvam sarvasya vā ekaikam aniyamena kāraṇam syāt iti kārya kāraṇa niyamaḥ  na syāt  yasya yad  kāraṇam prasiddham tad eva tasya kāraṇam na anyata anyasya pūrva uttara kṣaṇa bhāvi tve apauti ceta tarhi prasiddhiḥ eva tvayā api āśritā nyāya abhimānam tyaktrā prasiddhi rapi nyāya eva iti ced  tarhi yathā prasiddha kārya kāraṇa ādi tad tathā eva abhyupeyam na hi kṣaṇikayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  ī dṛśyate mṛḍhena api tvad kutarka upahata buddhiḥ api vadati eva kevalam na tu paśyati katham ca paśyet  svayam kṣaṇikaḥ  dvayoḥ kṣaṇayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvam akṣaṇikaḥ ced svayam darśana hāniḥ kim caḥ kṣaṇikam ced kāraṇam tad  sva kāraṇa abhāve na midhyet  tad kāraṇam tad kāraṇam api evam iti anavasthānāt na kiṃcitmidhyet  ekasya api svatasmiḍya bhāvāt  svatasmiḍya bhāve api anādi tvāt anyatamsiddheḥ na doṣaḥ  boja aṅkuravat iti ced  tad na na ṭekekasya kṣaṇasya anādi tvam kṣaṇika tvāt eva na ca anyat kṣaṇikam vastu iṣṭam iṣṭam ced  darśana hāniḥ bauja aśreṣṭhapi yad ekam anvitam mṛd iva ghaṭa ādiṣu tad eva kāraṇam bojānā makarāṇām ca mud iva piṇḍa ādaunām na tu kāryāṇām kāraṇa tā iti boja aṅkuravat iti adṛṣṭāntaḥ tasmāt kṣaṇikasya kāraṇa tvam apramiddham prasādhaka abhāvāt ca atas  kārya kāraṇa ādi niyama artham prasiddhim ced āśrayasi kṣaṇika kāraṇam kārya ca bāhya arthaḥ ca na asti iti evamādi lakṣaṇām kutaka eka mūlā buddhim parityajya matām mārgam āśraya anyathā manda buddhaunmaḥ  hayan svayam ca amomuhyamānaḥ  vinadhyami tathā prasiḍya na āśrayaṇe api tasmāt kāryasya kāraṇatva anupapatteḥ nityam eva kāraṇam iti kāraṇa bhāve kārya bhavati eva iti niyamaḥ  na asti e vā iti sthitam nityam ced kāraṇam kim iti sadā kārya na bhavet  sadā ced bhaveta kāraṇavat nitya tvāt  tad  kāryam eva na bhavet  vicchidya vicchidya tathā astu iti ced  bhavati eva tathā kṣaṇa mātram eva vicchedaḥ astu na dīrgha kālam iti ced  kṣaṇa mātra cevicchedam icchasi kāryasya kāraṇe sati api kim iti kṣaṇa vayam ahorātram pakṣam māsam saṃvatsaram kalpam vā na icchami kṣaṇa mātra vicchedam vinā kāryasya am aṃbhavāt  tam icchāmi na anyam iti ced  tad ayuktam kāraṇe nitye kāryasya vicchedam vinā asaṃbhavāt  sa iṣyate ced  tasya tasya kāryasya tam tam vicchedam vinā asaṃbhavāt  ma ma eṣṭavyaḥ  yatas  astu vicchedaḥ tathā api kāraṇasya viśeṣa abhāvāt yad kiṃcid kārya yadā kadācid astu tad tadā eva iti ayam kāla niyamaḥ kuta iti ced  kāla niyamāt eva iti bamaḥ tathā ahi—sthāyinā mapi dṛkṣā ādaunām kāla viśeṣāt eva puṣya phala ādi kārya viśeṣaḥ  dṛśyate kālasya tu kāla antara abhāvāt na kāla niyama codya masti kālasya kāla antara abhāve katham tasya paurvāparyam iti ceta kāla antaram ced icchasi anavasthā atha kālamya paurvāparyam tam vā kālam na icchami–kāla niyamaḥ katham kārya sya iti mā cucudaḥ kaḥ ca kālā na astauti brūyāt  bravīmi yadā icchāmauti ced  tām ̐cchasi kālam ‘yadā iti kāla śabda uktaḥ katham ca icchan  tad daṣayasi tasya satya tvam dūṣayāmauti ced kāla tvam eva ced satya tvam tad  iṣṭa tvāt na dṛṣyam anya vettat  dṛṣyatām nāma na naḥ kiṃcid chidyate kālasya aduṣṭa tvāt  kālaḥ ca īdṛṣyate tad saṃbandhi sarvam eva janimabastu dūṣitam syāt  atas tad icchatā na kālā dūṣyaḥ tasmā kāla yoginām kāryāṇām kālena eva utpatti ādi niyama abhyupa gamena kāryāṇām kāla niyamaḥ katham iti asya ca udyasya pari hṛta tvāt  akāla yogini tu kārye asya codyasya eva anu tpatteḥ nitya kāraṇa pakṣe na kaścid doṣa iti sthitam ata anādikasya eva śukti ajñānasya śukti rūpya tad jñāna upādāna tā nyāyyā na tu anyasya kasyacid  nanu śuktarādimatyā ajñānam katham anādi syāt  na ayam doṣaḥ aśukti āśraya tvāt tasya jña āśrayam hi tad  jñaḥ ca na ādiḥ katham aśukti āśrayatve śukti ajñānam iti śuktyā vyapadeśa iti ced  śukti jñānavat na hi śukti nānam śukti āśrayam tasyāḥ  jaḍa tvāt  atas śukti viṣaya tvāt śukti jñānam tad  tathā śuktyajñānam api nanu jña āśraya tvejñānasya tad jarūpyasya śukti sāmānādhikaraṇyam katham iti ced  śukti āśraya tve api tad jarūpi ajñānasya jñātṛ dharma tvam katham na ca ubhaya āśraya tvam ekasya virodhāt  daya kalpanāyām ca kalpanā gauravam śukti āśraya tve ca mādi tvā an na rūpya kāraṇa tā syāt  śukti anugatam śukti kāraṇam eva rūpya kāraṇam iti ced  śuktivat rūpyam api satyam syāt  śukti kāraṇam api ajñānam eva iti ced  tad na adya api siddham tasmā jña āśrayam eva śukti ajñānam nanu ajñānam viṣaye na asti iti te sthitiḥ manda mā evam vācaḥ na hi aham viṣaye tad jñāne ca sati api tatra ajñānam na asti iti bravīmi tayoḥ abhāve tu ajñāna abhāvassarveṣām samānaḥ na hi śukti rūpye kasyacid  jñāna ajñāne staḥ satyatva prasaṅgāt  satya rū pyavat  na ca tad satyam bādhāt  atas śu klaya jñāna jam eva tad  jña āśraya ajñāna jasya api rūpyasya śuktimāmānā dhikaraṇyakhyā tiḥ kha sthasya iva arkasya kūpe khyātivat na virudhyate bhrānti tvāt  na hi yathā sthita khyāti rdhāntiḥ amañceta rūpyam khyāti tasya śukti sāmāna adhikaraṇyam asat  kim na khyāyāt  viṣaya āśrayam ajñānam iti ca apramiddheḥ ma ma atrā jñānam iti ca jñasya maṃvitteḥ viṣaya āśraya ajñāna abhyupagame api jña āśrayasya abhyupeya tvāta tena vinā rūpya jñānāmiddheḥ tena eva ca rūpyasya api middheḥ tad eva ca rūpyata jñāna ādi upā dānam iti miḍam nanu avocaḥ  rūpyasya jñāna ajñāne na sta iti idānom katham tabiruddham tasya jñānam icchasi kim ca ajñātam ced rūpyam katham tad pyam katham vā tasya bādhaḥ kādācid ka tayā kā kārya tā katham na ca tad mānam vinā sidhyati asvayam prakāśa tvāt  na ced tad aparokṣam bhāti tad āditsayā pravṛtti ntiānām na syāt  ajñāna jam ced ta tyarokṣam eva syāt  parokṣa tvāt ajñānasya jñānam api hi anumeya tvāt  parokṣam kim punar tad abhāvaḥ ajñānam atha saṃvid abhāvaḥ ajñānam tasya api na īdṛśya parokṣa tā īdṛś vā kārya samasti ajñānam ca jñānasya prāc abhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ  vā sa ca jñāna antara m anya tā kārya viśeṣa eva tad kāraṇa samavetaḥ  bhāva rūpa eva na hi kāraṇam eva prāc abhāvaḥ kārya bhāve tad nittaḥ kāraṇa abhāva prasaṅgāt  na api pradhvaṃsaḥ kāraṇam kāryāti ākāraṇa abhāva prasaṅgāt  pradhvaṃsasya prāk  abhāvāt  atas  jñāna prāgabhāva pradhvaṃsau  api kāya om bhāvau ca ghaṭasya iva piṇḍakapāla ākhyau tasmāt nānā ādi na api anirvacanīyam ajñānam atas  na tad tava rūpya ādi kāraṇam syāt  syāt ced  kāryasya api kāraṇa tvam rūpya ādeḥ ca matya tvam iṣṭam syāt  yadi kaścid rūyāt  na bhāvaḥ pradhvaṃmaḥ kṛtakasya api tasya nitya tvāt  bhāvaḥ ced  ghaṭa paṭa vada nityam syāt  pradhvaṃsaḥ api anityaḥ ced  naṣṭaḥ anaṣṭa ssyāt  tasmāt nāmau bhāvaḥ prāgabhāvasya ca kāryatve tasya anyaḥ prāga bhāvaḥ apekṣyaḥ tasya api anyaḥ tasya api anya iti evam anavasthānāt na kaścid midhyet  prāgbhāva eva vā prāc abhāvaḥ syāt  maḥ api marvaḥ pūrva uttarasya prāgabhāvastyāt  viśeṣa abhāvāt yaḥ  yasya pradhvaṃmaḥ ma tasya prāgabhāva iti ced  tad na pradhvaṃsaḥ  na bhāva iti ukta tvāt  tarhi pradhvaṃma mācavyavadhānaḥ  yaḥ pūrvaḥ bhāvasma prāc abhāvaḥ na anya iti ced  tathā api na sa sākṣā
