tyāka na api abhāva iti na sa prāc abhāvaḥ tarhi pradhvaṃma eva astu prāc abhāvaḥ prātvāda bhāva tvāt ca atas  kāryatvam prāgabhāvasya api midhyati iti ced  tathā api bhāva tvam na midhyati iyoḥ ca bhedaḥ  na syāt  pradhvaṃsa eva ceti āga bhāvaḥ tasya anivṛtte ttaram kārya sidhyet  na hi anivṛtte prāc abhāve kārya siddhiḥ iṣyate apica– jñānasya prāc abhāvaḥ kāryaḥ ced  tad siddeḥ prāk  sadā eva jñānasya bhāvān na tasya prāc abhāvaḥ sidhyet  na ca ūrdhvam pradhvaṃsa vyāpta tvāt  na ca anādeḥ bhāvasya pradhvaṃmaḥ atas anādyanantaḥ  jñāna bhāva ssyāt  atas  na bhāvaḥ prāc abhāvaḥ na ca kāryaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ kāryaḥ api na bhāva iti asau praṣṭavyaḥ katham pradhvaṃsaḥ kāryaḥ na ced sa bhāvaḥ kāryaḥ ced  katham vā na anitya iti bhāva eva kārya tvāt anityaḥ  na abhāva iti ced  bhāva eva kāryaḥ api dṛṣṭaḥ na abhāvaḥ kārya tā ced tulyā bhāva abhāvayoḥ anitya tā ca tulyā eva nyāyyā na hi abhāvaḥ kaścid kāryaḥ  nityaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ abhāvom api pradhvaṃsaḥ kāryaḥ ced  kim iti na prāc abhāvaḥ kāryaḥ anādi tvāt iti ced  tad na antavat tvasya iṣṭa tvāta anta vataḥ ca ādimattvāt ghaṭavat  na hi antavat anādi anādi vā antavat  kiṃcid ṛṣṭam ata ādi antavat tvāt ca bhāva eva abhāvaḥ api itara bhāvavat  itaretarābhāvavat ca bhāvatva mabhāvānām nyāyyam jñāna prāc abhāva nivṛttiḥ ca jñānam eva uta anyat  yadi jñāna bhāva eva pradhvaṃmasya bhāva tvam tvayā eva iṣṭam syāt  yadi anyat kiṃcid  ma kim bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ  vā yadi abhāvaḥ prāgabhāvasya bhāvatva prasaṅgaḥ na hi abhāvasya eva bhāvaḥ nivṛtti ssyāt  syāt ced  tadā api pūrvasya abhāvasya jñāna prāgabhāva tvam na syāt  nivṛtti vyavadhānāt  bhāva tve api tathā atha nivṛttiḥ bhāvaḥ tasya api pūrvam abhāvāt  prāga bhāvaḥ tad nivṛttiḥ ca abhyupeyā tasya tasya api evam iti ukta dā upa prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt na jñānāt anyā tad prāgabhāva nivṛttiḥ jñāna mā iva ceti āga bhāva nivṛttiḥ pradhvaṃsasya bhāva tvam iṣṭam sya ādi tyuktam nanu bhāva pradhvaṃsasya abhāva tvam uktam na tu abhāva pradhvam sasya tasya tu bhāvatā eva iti ced  tathā api tasya pradhvastaḥ pradhvaṃsasya api pradhvaṃsa iṣṭa eva atas ca prāgabhāvasya apradhva statvam punar utpattiḥ vā abhyapeya iti anādi tvam tasya na sidhayet  pūrva manā ditvam eva iti ced  tad na na hi anādeḥ nirhetu tvāt naṣṭasya punar utpatti ssaṃbhavet  ata utpattimat tve pūrvam api nānā dissaḥ tasya ca apradhvaṃse na kārya bhāva ssyāt  na hi anivṛtte prāc abhāve kārya siddhiḥ iti hi avocaḥ tasmāt  pradhvaṃsa prāga bhāvau jñānasya bhāvī kāya om ca abhyapeyau yadi nāma tau  abhāvau akāryom ca tathā api na anirvacanīyau atha jñānāt anyat ajñānam tathā api na anirvacanīyam asti na astauti vā marvasya jñeya ādeḥ pratīteḥ nirucyamāna tvāt  atas  na anirvacanīyam ajñānam nāma kiṃcid asti atha asti na asti iti vā yantra kenacid  pramāṇena jñāyate na api tathā nirvacanīya aham pratibhāsate ca sarva prāṇinām tad ajñāna manirvacanīyam jaḍa rūpam tādṛgḥ api ādi kāraṇa miti ced  tada yuktam apramāṇam jaḍam pratibhāsate ca iti vipratiṣedhāt  tasmāt mad akta prakāram prāc abhāva ādi svarūpam yadi vā anyathā sarvathā asti na astauti vā pramāṇa gamyam eva jaḍam bhāti asvayaṃprabha tvāt itya nirvacanīya avidyā rūpya tajñāna ādi kāraṇam iti anupapannam iti abā ucyate na ayam doṣaḥ avidyā tad kāryayoḥ nitya anu bhavam ācāt  siddheḥ anubhavasya ca nitya tvam vakṣyāmaḥ avocāma ca tathā api tad prasādāt eva sarvasya jaḍasya siddhiḥ anyathā svata smid himiddhiḥ vā syāt  rūpa ādaunām tu cakṣuḥ ādya pekṣa tvāt anubhavasya nitya tve api kadācid asiddhiḥ yathā nityaḥ api sa vitṛ maṇya ādi prakāśaḥ tad prasādāt prakāśyasya middhau  asiddhau ca prakāśayati na prakāśayatauti ca ucyate evam anubhavaḥ api kūṭastha nityaḥ asaṅgaḥ api tadābhāma tayā jaḍasya siddhau  asiddhau ca tathā ucyate na tu tasya kaści viśeṣaḥ kadācid  yadi tādṛś anubhavaḥ ajñāna ādi mādhakaḥ  na iṣyate asiddhiḥ eva ajñānāt aunāma teṣām pramāṇa āgamya tvāt  na hi pramāṇam api pramāṇa gamyam kim punar ajñāna ādi pramāṇa tad abhāvau ca phala tad abhāvābhyām na anumeyau  iti vakṣyāmaḥ smṛti bhrānti saṃśayānām tu phalasya api abhāva annatarā manumeya tā phalam ced syāt  teṣām api pramāṇa tā eva syāt  na ca jñānam jñāna antara pratyakṣam jñānam hi jñātuḥ vikriyā guṇa u vā syāt  yasya ca yā vikriyā mā na tam tadikriyām ca samāna jātīyām vijātīyām vā viṣayaukuryāt  yathā mṛdādi vikriyā yasya ca yaḥ  guṇa u na ma tam tad guṇam ca mama ana jātīyam vijātīyam vā viṣayaukuryāt  yathā agnyādi guṇaḥ prakāśa ādi gni ādaun na api ātmānam vipayokuryāt  evam jñānam api jñāna antaram tad dantam tadi kriyāḥ ca tad guṇān  ca tmānam ca na viṣayaukuryāt  mṛdādi vikriyā agni ādi prakāśa ādivat viṣayaukriyante ced  tahat eva anyasya eva sva aviṣayasya viṣayā bhavitum arhanti tasmāt pramāṇa jñāna smṛti bhrānti saṃśaya ādivat  tad samāna āśrayāṇām sukha duḥkha icchāt deṣa prabhṛtaunām pratyakṣāṇām api na jñāna pratyakṣa tā na api tad abhāvānām iti yathā ukta anubhava pratyakṣa tā iva abhyupeyā anyathā teṣām asiddheḥ na ajñānasya nirvacanīya tu apramaṅgaḥ na api aprasiddha tvam anubhavāt siddheḥ atas jñānam anirvācyam rū pyādi kāraṇam iti siddham nanu bhāva abhāva pramāṇa agamya tvāt ced aniḥ vacanīya tā mā ātmanaḥ api syāt iti ced  na āgama pramāṇa tvāt  tasya maḥ ajaḍa tvāt āgamasya aviṣaya iti cet—matyam ata eva gama pramāṇamsaḥ anyathā pratyakṣa ādaunām eva viṣaya ssyāt  na vā kasyacita vipayyantara abhāvāta tasya jaḍa tvāt  vipaci antara bhāve tu sa eva ātmā āgama pramāṇaḥ ca syāt  tarhi jñāna mukha ādaunām api bhāva abhāva pramāṇa agamya tvāt nirvacanīyatā syāt iti ced  yadi syāt  astu kim naḥ chinnam nanu anirvacanauya tve brahma jñānasya api aprāmāṇyam syāt  na syāt  satya vipaya tvāt yatasmati aviṣaya tvam tada bhāvaśa prāmāṇyam aprāmāṇyam ca na svarūpam atya tvam amatya tvam ca matyasya api ghaṭa ādeḥ aprāmāṇyāta tad vipaya jñānasya ca matya viṣaya tvena prāmāṇyāt  amatyasya api varṇa dairdhi ādemmati aviṣa yasya prāmāṇyāta jāgrat svapna bhrāntaunām asatyānām api matya śubha aśubha sūcakānām satya viṣaya tayā prāmāṇyāt  na ca evam mantavyam na asatyasya satya viṣaya tā mithyādhum anye vā iti asatyasya api varṇa ādessatya viṣaya tvasya darśita tvāt  mithyā dhūmasya avyāpta tvāt  matyā agni aliṅga tvāt tad abodhaka tvam vyāptasya tu asati rūpasya api pratibimba ādesmatya bimba ādi bodhaka tā dṛṣṭā eva ghaṭa ādeḥ satyasya api avyāptasya agni abodhaka tā dṛṣṭā tasma ajñāna ādeḥ nirvācya tve api prāmāṇyam satya viṣaya tvāt  matyaviṣaya tvam ca tad pamiteḥ na na upapadyata iti ati prasaṅga abhāvāt bhāva abhāva pramāṇa agamya tayā eva anirvācyatva api ajñānasya iṣṭe na kaścid dopaḥ na ca vayam bhāva abhāva gramāṇā gamyatayā ajñānasya anirvācya tām brūmaḥ api tu jñāna mātrāpanodya tvāt  rūpyavat  na hi madaḥ tu jñāna apanodyam atiprasaṅgāt  na api śaśa viṣāṇam prāpti abhāvāt atas anirvācyam tad  jñāna apanodya tvāt tad ekam anekam vastu naḥ vā bhinnam abhinnam vā mā avayavam niravayavam ityādi prakāraiḥ ca niścitya vaktam aśakya tvāt ca bhāva abhāva pramāṇā gamya tvam tu mada mattva āśaṅkā vyātti artham ucyate na tu tena eva nirvacanīya tvam mādhyate tasya nirvacanauyeṣṭhapi bhāvāt  jñāna sukha ādiṣu na hi teṣām anirvacanīya tā idānom miḍdā mādhyate vā atas anirvācyam śukti anjānam eva tāha grapya ādi kāraṇam iti nyāyyam tad bhāve bhāvāt  tad abhāve ca abhāvāt  nanu śukti ajñāne naṣṭe api rūpya ādi punadṛśyate atas  ajñāna abhāve api bhāvān na tad kāryatā rūpyāriti ceta tad na punar api hi mati eva śukti ajñāne rūpya ādi dṛśyate na tu jñāyamānāyām eva śuktau kim anantāni śukti ajñānāni bāḍham anantāni eva yadi anantāni śuktinānāni yadi hi ekam eva aśukti ajñānam tadā ekena eva śuktinā anena nivṛtta miti kim anyaiḥ śakti jñānaḥ atha tāni ajñāna anivartakāni anarthakāni tarhi atha ajñānā nivartakāni api arthavanti tāni tarhi pūrvam api jñānam tathā eva iti ajñātā eva śuktismadā syāt  atha pūrvam nivartakam tathā eva uttarāṇi api avi śeṣāt  atha tāni nivṛtta ajñānasya bhavantauti viśeṣaḥ tarhi jātasya jantoḥ ādyena jñānena ajñāne nivṛtte tasya u ttarāṇi sarvāṇi eva anivartakāni syaḥ atha sarveṣu eva padā rtheṣu tatra api bhinna jñāna jñeyeṣu śabda ādiṣu viṣayeṣu maka tsakadajñānam nivartanīyam asti tīnantāni ajñānāni ekasya puṃmaḥ  nivāni mantauti ekasmin  api viṣaye aneka ajñānā bhyupagame na kaścid opa iti ajñāna nivartakāni eva sarvāṇi jñānāni eṣṭavyāni ajñāyamāna artha viṣayatva aviśeṣāt  na hi pūrva jñānena eva uttara kālam madā arthom bhāsyate atas  jāna bhedaḥ cediṣyate tad niva ajñāna bhedaḥ api eṣṭavya iti yasyāḥ  jñānasya yadrapyādi kārya na tad  tad abhāve bhavati iti na tad kāryatva virodhaḥ nanu ajñāna bhāvāced na bhāti śukti jñāna udite api na bhāmeta eka ajñāna abhāve api ajñāna antarāṇām tatra bhāvāt  atha satsu api teṣu jñāna bhāve śukti ti abhāve ca na bhāti na tarhi tāni abhāna kāraṇam śuktaḥ tad bhāve api tasyāḥ  bhānāt  atassā svata eva na bhāti jaḍa tvāt  jñāna bhāve tu bhāti abhāve svata eva na bhāti atas asyāḥ  jñānam prakāśakam eva na ajñānam nāma tad nivatyam tatra kiṃcid astauti ced  tad na ajñāna abhāve ajñāta abhāvāt jñānasya api abhāva prasaṅgāt  yadi api śuktarasvata eva ābhāna miti prakāśakam eva tasyāḥ  jñānam tathā api jñāna abhāve tasyāḥ  abhānāt  tava api jñāna abhāvaḥ  jānena nivartyata iti nivayam na na asti tava api anivṛtte api cejñāna abhāve sā bhāti jñāna udayāt prāk api bhāmeta na ced  na ūrdhva mapi jñāna abhāva anivṛtteḥ atha ucyeta jñānasya bhāna hetu tvāt  tad bhāve mā bhāti abhāna hetutva abhāvāt jñānā bhāvasya tad anivṛttau  api nābhānam tasyāḥ  iti tad ca ayuktam jñānasya abhāva anivṛttau abhāva ayogāt  abhāve api ced bhāvaḥ  jñānasya madā bhāvāt  madā bhānam śuktarasyāt  sadā bhāne ca śuktaḥ tad bhānasya jñāna hetutva asiddheḥ tajñānām iddhiḥ atha matam na anivṛtte api tasya abhāve jñānasya bhāvaḥ kiṃtu nivṛtta eva atas  kādācid kam śukti bhānam syāt  tad hetaḥ nisya kādācid ka tvāt  anyeṣu tu jñāna abhāveṣu ani vṛtteṣu api śukti bhānam syāt  teṣām śuktyabhānā hetu tvāt iti tājñāneṣu api etad samānam śuktyabhānā hetu tvāt tepām api ___ jñāna abhāva vyatirekeṇa ajñānam na jānāmauti ced  mā evam vocaḥ na ājñāsiyam śuktim idānom tu jānāmi ajñānam nivṛttam punar na jānāmauti ajñāna tad nittyoḥ prasiddha tvāt  tad eva ajñānam jñāna abhāva iti ced  tad na abhāva pramāṇa aprameya tvāt  pratyakṣam abhāvaḥ  vā abhāvasya pramāṇam na tābhyām jñānābhyām jñāyate ajñānam aparokṣa tvāca na abhāva jñeyam pratyakṣa viśeṣaṇaḥ ca abhāvaḥ pratyakṣa jñāna gamyaḥ na ca ātmā pratyakṣa jñāna prameyaḥ ghaṭa ādi vadana ātmatva prasaṅgāt  prameya tve ekasya pramāvṛtva prameyatva anupapatteḥ pramāvantarā bhāvāt ca bhāve api tasya eva ātma tvāt ata eva ātmanaḥ  aprameya tvāt  tasya ajñānam na abhāva pramāṇena api prameyam na hi abhāva āśrayam apratītya abhāvam pratiyanti abhāva vādinaḥ  api katham apramāṇam bhātauti ced  rūpyavat  na hi śukti rūpyam kenacityamāṇena bhāti amithyātva pramaṅgāt  tathā api bhāti evam ajñānam api bhāti anubhavāt eva uktam ca etad parastāt yadi na ajñānam pramāṇa abhāvaḥ kamtahyamau vimṛśyatām ma yadi kaḥ api anyaḥ prāmāṇikasmam asti na anyaḥ  api mamasti ātmani jñāna abhāvasya aprameya tvāt anyatra tasya abhāvāt  itaretarābhāvaḥ anyatra api astauti ced  maḥ api jñānasya ātmam aṃbandhinaḥ aprameya tvāt na prameyaḥ tasmāt na kaści jñāna abhāvaḥ prāmāṇikaḥ asti atas ajñānam eva jñāna abhāva iti ced  astu evam api na ajñānasya anirvacana auyatva hāniḥ jñāna abhāvasya abhāva pramāṇa agamya tvāt amattva aprāptaḥ na ca ajñānam eva sarvaḥ  jñāna abhāva iti niyantam śakyam itare tarā bhāvasya viṣaya āśraya tvāt ajñānasya ca ātmā eka āśraya tvāt  pradhvaṃsasya ca utyatteḥ iṣṭa tvāt  ajñānam utpannam mama iti ca pratītya bhāvāt  ajñānasya nivṛtti pratīteḥ pradhvaṃsasya ca nitya niṣṭeḥ atha ucyeta utpattimattva atyadhvaṃsaḥ api vināśau na hi bhāvāt anyasya utpattiḥ bhāvasya ca utpannasya ghaṭavat nāśaḥ nyāyyaḥ tasmāt uttara uttaraḥ  bhāvaḥ pūrvasya pūrvasya pradhvaṃsaḥ pūrvaḥ pūrva uttarottarasya prāgabhāva iti tadā api iyoḥ api abhāvayoḥ janimat tvāt ajñānasya ca tad apratauteḥ na tayoḥ ajñāna tā nanu naṣṭam jñānam iti nāśa janma bhāti bhātu tathā api na ajñānasya janma bhāti tasya prāc abhāvā pratīteḥ jñānasya eva hi prāgabhāvaḥ  bhāti na punar ajñāna sya api jñānasya jñāna antaram eva abhāvaḥ  vastu antaram veti asya pakṣasya dūṣaṇam vakṣyāmaḥ tasmāt na ajñānam jñāna abhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsa sya abhāva tve api janimattva anivṛtti abhāvāt ca tad vaiparotyā ca ajñānasya pradhvaṃmaḥ  na ajñānam iti aktam tad dat eva prāga bhāvaḥ api jñāna abhāva tve mati tattva pratīti abhāvāt na ajñānam bhavitum arhati atas  na kaścid abhāvaḥ ajñānam nanu na prāc abhāvaḥ anyaḥ  dṛśyate atas ajñānam eva ma iti ced  ki pradhvaṃsam anyam paśyami uta na na ced  tasya yā gatiḥ sā eva sya api bhaviṣyati nanu āsa aujñānam naṣṭam jñānam iti pradhvaṃsaḥ  jñāyate tarhi nāma aujñānam bhaviṣyati jñāna miti prāc abhāvaḥ api jñāyata eva spaṣṭam na jñāyata iti ced  pradhvaṃsaḥ api tathā yasya jñānam tad abhāvaḥ ca parokṣaḥ yasya tu pratyakṣam vayam tasya spaṣṭam eva tad  parokṣa jñāna vādinaḥ ca na jñāna abhāvaḥ ajñānam aparokṣa tvāt iti uktam jñāna prāgabhāva eva ajñānam jñāna bhāve tad nitteḥ iti ced  tad na ata tyāga bhāvasya api jñāna bhāve nivṛtti upapatteḥ pradīpa bhāvena iva tamasaḥ na hi pradīpasya prāgabhāvamtamaḥ tathā api bhavan  eva ma tad nivartayati nanu pūrva pradopa sya abhāvāt  tatyāga bhāva eva tamaḥ tena nivartyata iti ced  tad na jātena gacchatā api pradeśa antaram tatra tatra tamasaḥ  nivartyamāna tvāt  kṣaṇika tvāt  pradīpaḥ tatra tatra sva prāga bhāva tamaḥ nivartanena jāyata iti ced  ta kava eva tiṣṭhata uttara kṣaṇeṣu tatra sva prāgabhāva tamaḥ abhāvāt  nṛ śṛṅgasya iva pradīpasya tailavādi bhāve api anutpatteḥ tad pravāha ucchedaḥ anu cchede vā taila ādi abhāve api sthitiḥ prasajyeta atas  na prāc abhāvaḥ pradīpasya tamaḥ na api pradhvaṃmaḥ tamaḥ abhāve api kṣaṇānām pradhvaṃsāt  katham ca maṇyāt itya ādi prakāśānām prāc abhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ  vā tamassyāt  na api prakāśānā mitaretarābhāvaḥ tamaḥ prakāśānām anyonyam itaretara abhāva syātamaḥ rūpa tvāt aprakāśa āśraya eva maḥ abhāvaḥ tama iti ceta sarva prakāśānām ced saḥ abhāvaḥ marva abhāve na nivarteta sarva asmaraṇe ca na bhāmeta āśraya agrahaṇa ca na ca tamaḥ  dṛṣṭi kāle tad āśrayaḥ  gṛhyate smaryate vā adṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ na ca pratiyogi smaraṇa ādi pūrvaka tā tamaḥ dṛṣṭāṃti kasyacid  atha ekasya eva prakāśasya tamaḥ abhāvaḥ itareṣām bhāve api nivṛttiḥ atha ekaikasya prakāśasya ekaikam tamaḥ abhāvaḥ tadā e kasya prakāśasya bhāve tad abhāvasya eva nivṛtteḥ anantāni tamāṃsi tatra eva syuḥ ananta tvāt pradīpa ādi prakāśanām tadvatām atas ca na kiṃcid prakāśeta āvaraṇa bhūyaḥ tvāt eka prakāśa bhāve prakāśa antara abhāvāssantaḥ api tatra eka jñāna bhāve jñānā ntara abhāvā iva artha prakāśanam na vighnanti prakāśata eva artha iti ced  na tathā apratīteḥ yathā iha jñāyamāne arthe jñānā ntara ābhā vā jikṣā ādi bhāva bhāve vā bhānti na tathā prakāśamāne arthe tamāṃmi bhānti prakāśa antaram maraṇa jiṣṭa dhādi bhāve api abhāvāḥ tu bhānti teṣām atas  na prakāśa abhāvaḥ tamaḥ tathā api tad tena nivartyate tathā eva jñānam api ajñānam asvābhāvam api bhāva mātreṇa eva nivartayitum ala miti ajñānam na jñāna abhāva iti siddham tad ca ajñānam iti jñāna virodhāt  jñāna paryudāsena vā ucyate tad eva anirvacanīyam jaḍa ātmakam māyā ādi śabdara paryu dāsena api ucyate taba jñānam iti ajaḍaḥ  bodhaḥ tadā bhāmā vā citta vṛttiḥ matyā arthā yathāyogam āśrayaṇīyā ubhayatra jñāna śabda prayogāt ekaḥ mukhyaḥ arthaḥ aparaḥ  vācya iti tatra śukti nānam jāyamānam tad anānam nivartayati iti atra buddhitti nim ajñānam ca rūpya ādi kāraṇam tad nivartyam brahma jñāna miti atra api buddhittiḥ eva brahmā bhāmā matau jñānam ucyate brahma ajñānam iti sarva jaḍa upādāna bhūtāḥ  jaḍa ātmikā avidyā śaktiḥ ucyate ajñāna śarora tve api brahma jñānasya matyā artha tvāt brahmaka ābhāsa tvāt ca jñāna tvam tad ajñāna nivartaka tvam ca iṣyate satya artha tvāt prāmāṇyam na svarūpam atya tvāt jñānasyati hi uktam yathā veṇujaḥ api agniḥ tam ma mūlam dahati svayam ca śāmyati evam ajñāna jam api brahma jñānam ajñānam danda hauti tad ātmaka tvāt  svayam ca śāmyati brahmā eva vā ajaḍa bodha rūpam tanmātra ābhāsa buddhi vṛtti upetam svājñānam dahat  tad kāryam anyat  tām ca dṛttim dagdhvā ekam avaśiṣyate yathā rājā ekam coram labdhvā asādhyān api anyān mavān  corān nighnan tam ca coram hatvā svasthaḥ  bhavati yathā vādi yogāt kevalam adāhya mapi tailaṣṭatā ādi dahana vahniḥ vādī api dahati evam kevala madāhyam api anjānam viśiṣṭa buddhitti yuktam brahma dahet  eva manyatra api buddi yuktaḥ  bodha gvājñāna tad kāyem dahati buddhyā deḥ tu taba satya tvena adāhya tvāt na tu tam dahati yathā vāyu yatas agniḥ taṇa ādi dahati na vā ayama adāya tvāt tasya atas  bahis vā bodha dīptā bodhaḥ  vā bauddhaḥ ajñānam dahati iti jñāna tad kārya dāhassihaḥ jñāna vibhāvamoḥ nanu brahma ajñānasya api śukti ajñānasya iva dagdhasya api punar  punarbhāvāt anirmokṣa prasaṅga iti ced  tad na dagdhasya ajñānasya punarbhāvām aṃbhavāt  ajñānam dhana ādi atas  na asya kāraṇa masti atas  na asya janma na hi akāraṇakam jāyate atas anādinaḥ ajñānamya dāhāt  anyasya ca anutpatteḥ jñānā nmokṣa upapannaḥ na hi śakti ajñānam api dagdham punar bhavati adagdhatva pramaṅgāt  pratīti virodhāt ca na ca anyat apūrvam jāyate kiṃtu pūrvam eva anādyat nānam mākalyena adagdham śukta smākalye na aprakāśita tvāt na hi śuktiḥ ta jñāna kṣaṇa eva asti uttara kālā api bhāvāttanyāḥ na ca sarva kālam aṃbandhi rūpa grāhi pratyakṣam atas aneka jñāna prakāśya aneka rūpa tvāt śakte reka ekena jñānena kā arthena aprakāśita tvāt tad ajñānasya api kānyena anivṛttiyujyate nanu ajñānam ced sa aṃśama ghaṭavat kārya syāt  na ced  kā anyena nivṛtti nivṛttiḥ vā syāt  satyam ata eva sa aṃśatva anaṃśatva ādibhiḥ anirvācyam tad iti vādiṣma tathā hi ajñānam ced kāryam prāk makta bandhā bhāvaḥ muktānām bandhe anirmokṣa prasaṅgāt  ṅgaḥ kṛtsna nitya nivṛttyoḥ sadā muktatva mānyam vā jagata ssyāt  atas anirvācyam eva tasmāt yāvat jaḍam vastu asti tāvat na asyā jñānam aśeṣam nivartate brahmaṇaḥ tu aneka rūpatva abhāvāt tad jñānam dahati eva āśepamanānam na hi brahmaṇa śaktar iva svatas aneka rūpa tvam na api kāla ādi kṛtam śruteḥ yukteḥ ca atas  na rūpā ntara prakāśanāya punar jānameṣṭavyam śuktau  iva brahmaṇi svayam prakāśa tvāca atas  na ajñāna śeṣaḥ kanyaḥ punar jānakāra gṇā bhāvāca pramātṛ ādīnām tad kāraṇa ajñāna abhāve abhāvāt atas śatau  iva punar nāna abhāvāca na ajñāna śepaḥ kalpyaḥ punar api jñānasti ced  tad anurūpaḥ ajñāna śeṣaḥ kalpyaḥ prakāśakam avārthasya pramāṇam arthāt nittiḥ anyasya atas aprakāśa mānam eva artha ḍhaukate tad iti ced  astu tathā brahmā api hi na prakāśate atas tad api ḍhokata eva pramāṇam tarhi śuktivat jaḍa tvāt tasya marva ajñānā nittiḥ   tad na svayaṃprakāśa tvāt  tahim vipratiṣedhaḥ svayaṃprakāśam na prakāśate ca iti na vipratiṣedhaḥ svayam prakāśā api matī maṃvittiḥ na asti na prakāśate ca kepāṃcid  tathā eva te vadanti śreyaḥ arthinaḥ api na ca mā na asti na ca na prakāśate tathā eva brahmā api svayaṃprakāśam mad ca na asti na prakāśate ca ājñānām atas  pramāṇam tatra arthavat  yathā maṃvittemmattva ātma prakāśakatva pratipādanam arthavat  saṃvitte rasattva ādi vacanam bhrānti mūlam iti ced  bhrāntiḥ api ajñāna malai mami vā iti mā teṣām na prakāśata eva atas tad dacaḥ arthavat  tasmāt jaḍamya svayaṃprakāśasya ca na kaścidiśeyaḥ ajñān pati ata eva dharmaḥ  na asti ātmā na asti iti aviśepaḥ  bārha spatyānām tasmāt svayaṃprakāśam api pramāṇa prakāśyam eva tasya ca aprakāśanam ajñānam eva iti tad nivartanam eva tad prakāśaka tvam pramāṇasya yathā mūrta dravya apanayanam eva kūpa ākāśa ādi kara ṇam tasya akārya tvāt akṛta kalyatvāca pūrvam tathā svayam prakāśasya api aprakāśya tvāt aprakāśa kalpa tvāt ca pūrvam ata eva na dipayaukaroti jaḍam iva pramāṇam bodhayat api yathā gurum bodhayan  api śiṣyaḥ sva śiṣyam iva gurum na bodharyāta yathā ca nṛpam vadat mṛtyaḥ sva bhṛtyam iva na vadati tammāt prakāśakam eva pramāṇam iti ammin  api pakṣa ajñāna nivartaka tvam siddham tasya prakāśaka tvāya eva yadā tu nivartakam eva arthāt  prakāśanam iti sthitiḥ tadā sutarām nivartaka tvam midhyet  am idam tu nivartaka tvāt iti ca uktam vākya kāraiḥ tasmāt  brahmaṇaḥ aneka rūpatva abhāvāt svayaṃprakāśa tvāt ca tad jñāne pari pūrṇa udite niśeṣa janma ādi mamāra bauja ajñāna ucchitti apa patteḥ punar api janma antara ādi maṃsāra baujam ajñānam avaśiṣyate rūpya ādi bīja śukti ajñānam iva iti na śakyam kalpayitum pramāṇa abhāvāt  nanu eka rūpa tvam svayaṃprakāśa tvam ca brahmaṇaḥ  na ajñāna śeṣā maṃbhave hetuḥ jñāna udayāt pūrvam api tad brahma tathā eva tathā api tatra paripūrṇam ajñānam āsīt kim iti uttara kālam śeṣaḥ api na syāt  jñāna virodhāt iti ced  na jñānam api sa avaśeṣa meva ajñānam nivartayati yathā śukti jñānam na tathā svayam prakāśa jñānam iti ced  na svayaṃprakāśe api phale asti svayaṃprakāśam ca tad iti jñāte api tad jāyate naśyati bhidyata iti ca bhrama darśanāt  na ca tasya api aprakāśamānam rūpa antaram mamamti svayaṃprakāśa tā hānāt atas  brahma jñānam api māva śepam eva ajñānam nivartayatauti tad chepa nimittaḥ punar api janma antara ādi maṃsāramsyāt iti ceta tad na pramāṇa abhāvāt  yadi api svayaṃprakāśa vastu jānam api māvaśepa ajñāna nivartakam maṃbhavati tathā api yāvat ajñāna śepamadbhā vakalpanāyām pramā raṇam asti tāvat eva tam kalpayāmaḥ na punar  pramāṇam vinā api atas  yathā ukta paripūrṇa lakṣaṇa brahma ātma bhāvam māṣṭāt anubhavataḥ api pūrvavat  punar api janma antara ādi hetu ajñāna śeṣam ad bhāve pramāṇā bhāvāt  na punamtamya maṃmāra saṃbhavet prākta yathā ukta brahmā tmā anubhavāt  svayaṃprakāśe sva ātma bhūte brahmaṇi ajñāna nittiḥ krameṇa eva iṣyate ata eva astitva upakramam ātmanaḥ aśanāya at ya tauta advitīya brahma ātmatva antam rūpam śrāvayitvā tad asaṃbhāvanā viparīta bhāvanā nivṛtti artham yuktīḥ ca āha vedaḥ tatra tatra tathā atattvam asi atattvam asi iti tam tam bhramam nudan nava kṛtva ūcivān marva ajñāna nivṛttau ‘ta hāsya vijanau iti ca śravaṇa manana nididhya āsanāni darśanam ādhanāni jagau śama dama ādīni ca sarva karma saṃnyāsa antāni vidhatte yajñā dauni ca mattva śuddi dvāreṇa darśana arthāni vidadhau yadi etai msādhana vinā makṛcchravaṇa mātreṇa eva brahma ātma anubhavaḥ  bhaveta etāni anarthakāni myaḥ na ca parokṣam vastu parokṣa jñāna revā abhyamyamānaiḥ aparoṣṭhībhavet anumeya ādiṣu adarśanāt  tammād śravaṇa ādaunyabhyamyamānāni aparoṣṭhā eva ātmani aneka prakārān bhramān nivartayanti manti mākṣāt darśana arthāni bhavanti śravaṇa ādibhiḥ nithite api ātma tattve anumāna ādi niścita iva candra ādau bheda pratibhāmā nivṛtteḥ darśana nivartyam api ajñāna masti atas  darśana atyāk mā avaśeṣa ajñāna nitti yukti matau marva bhramāṇām makāraṇānām yugapada nivṛtteḥ ekaikasya nivṛttasya puna ranutpattara ātmanaḥ astitva svayaṃprakāśatva nityatva vibhutva ādīnām yad yad pratipannam tasya tasya punar bādha abhāvāt  mava baujasya ca ajñānasya darśanāt nitteḥ atas  dṛṣṭa brahma ātma tattvasya uttara kālam janma antara ādi hetu ajñāna śepaḥ  na maṃbhavati iti ātma darśanāt eva mokṣa iti sthitam nanu yadi api janma antara ādi hetuḥ ajñāna śepaḥ  vidapaḥ  na maṃbhavati tathā api ajñāna leśaḥ ati eva vidapaḥ api kaṃcid kālam śagaiḥ asthiteḥ iṣṭa tvāt  tasyāḥ ca ajñāna mūla bheda darśana ādi mā apekṣa aśana pāna ādi apeṣṭhā tvāt  yadi hi vidyā mama kālam eva vipaśśarīram patet  tasya tāvat eva ciram iti maṃsārā bhāma anutteḥ śaraura pāta avadhi śravaṇam na syāt  na cāvi dapaḥ tad  tasya uttara kālam api maṃma ārabhāvāta aācārya vān puruṣaḥ  veda tasya tāvat eva ciram iti vidupa eva tad śabdena parāmṛśyamāna tvāt  na ca adṛṣṭa tattvasya avadhi śravaṇam arthavat  na ca darśanasya avadhiśrutiḥ śaraura pāte jīvanmuktiḥ darśanām aṃbhavāt  śarīriṇaḥ  hi tad saṃbhavaḥ tasmāt na vidyā kāla eva vidayaḥ  dehapātaḥ itas ca ācāryāt vidyā prāptiḥ ma ca vidvān jauvan  ca vihān apya dṛṣṭa tattvasma iti ced  tad na aupadekṣyanti te jñānam jñāninaḥ tattva darśinaḥ iti tattva darśibhiḥ eva upadiṣṭam jñānam pum artham ādhanam iti yata īśvaraḥ anuśaśāma dṛṣṭa tattvasya ced tadā eva śarīram patet  tadā ācārya abhāva avidyā lābhāt modhā bhāvaḥ tasmāt idapaḥ api śarīram kaṃcid kālam tiṣṭhet  apica jānatām tu tad pratibhāsaḥ  bādhita dvi candra ādivat  bhrānti bādhayoḥ ca bādhya bādhaka tā avagamāt eva anirvacanīya tā avagama iti na anirvacanīya tā tayoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvam vihanti na ca śukti ādi bodhasya anirvacanīya tā atra bhrāntar eva tu bhā yadi tasya api syāt  tathā api ukta eva parihāraḥ  bādhakasya bādhakatva siddhau  eva anirvacanīya tā sidhyantau na tasya bādhaka tām vihantauti nanu satyasya bādhya tvam iva anirvacanīyasya bādhaka tvam api na dṛṣṭam kvacid  matyam tathā api matya sya abādhya tvavat asati asya ābādhakatva niyama adṛṣṭeḥ iha eva bādhaka tā dṛśyatām bādhya tvam iva nava nirvacanauya tvāt rapya jñānavada bodhaka tu ābādhaka tve śukti jñānasya api yukte iti ced  tad na śukti jñānasya bodhakatva ādi siyadhaunatva adrṣya jñānasya anirvaca nauya tābodhakatva ādi siddheḥ śukti jñānasya anirvacanīya tā siddeḥ ca  rūpya jñānavat śakti jñānasya api abodhaka tvam abādhaka tvam ca anirvacanauya tvāt iti anumāna anupapatteḥ hetu dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt śukti jñānasya ābodhaka tve mati na ca evam satya tvam bādhā dhaunam abādhyasya api satya tvāt  matyasya ca abādhya tvāt  tathā tucchasya api atasmat tudh chayoḥ abādhya tvāt anirvacanīya mā iva bādhyam iti tad eva asatyam na mad tucche tammācśukti rūpya ādi bādhya tvāt asatyam eva iti miham nanu yadi api bādhyam asatyam tathā api bādhakam matyam eva bodhaka tvāt  na hi abodhakam bādhakam iṣyate atas  baḥ dhaka tvāt  matyam eva ghaṭa ādi jñānavat ghaṭa ādi jñānasya api matya tvam mama asiddham tasya sa viṣayasya bādhita tvāt śratyā iti ced  tad na śrautam api hi jñānam matyam eva bodhaka tvāt  tad artha pada padārtha ādi viṣaya pratyakṣa ādi jñānam api matyam eva artham ādhaka tvāt  yadi api jñāna kāraṇam amatyam api dṛṣṭam tathā api na amatyam jñānam artha sādhakam kiṃcid ṛṣṭam atas  jñānānām matya tvāt  tad arthā api matyā iti teṣām śukti rūpya ādivat  bādhyatva ayogāt śrateḥ anyaḥ arthaḥ  grāhyaḥ tasmāt rapya ādi eva jñānā panodyam na prapañca iti ced tad na śruti artha parityāga pramaṅgāt  tathā hi     aekam eva advitīyam aapūrvam anaparam aneti na iti aasthūlam anaṇu aprajñāna ghana eva aneha nānā asti amṛtya umma mṛtyum aindraḥ  māyābhiḥ iti ādauni śruti vacāṃmi prapañcam atya tve arthavanti vyarthāni syuḥ atas tad i ruī prapañcasya satyatva vacanam anumānataḥ api asya am atya tvam jaḍa tvāt i antavattva ādi hetubhiḥ śukti rūpya ādivat avagamyate tatas  ghaṭa ādi jñānasya api satya tvām iḍeḥ tadacśukti ādi jñānam brahma jñānam ca satyam ityādi anupapannam marvam eva ca jñānam bodhakam amatyam iti asatyam jñānam kiṃcid dodhakam adṛṣṭam iti ca asiddham amatya tve tu sarva jñānānām artha ābodhaka tvam asatya tvādrapi ādi jñānavat iti ced  na pratīti virodhāt  jñānāca artha asiddhau vyāpti grahaṇa āt yam aṃbhavāt  pakṣa hetu dṛṣṭāntā bhāvāt anumānasya ca asaṃbhavāt  tad saṃbhave tu jñānasya ābodhaka tvā asiddheḥ bodhaka tvam eva anapavādam su sthitam bhavet  atas sarvasya ana ātma jātasya asattve api bādhaka jñāna saṃbhavāt rūpya ādi bhrama iva śukti ādi jñānāt saṃsāra bhra maḥ api brahma jñānāt nivartata eva iti sthitam kā tarhi tad nittiḥ annāna nivṛttiḥ eva bhrama nittiḥ tad śaroḥ tvāt tasya iti ced kāma avajñāna nittiḥ kim tām pṛccham i mā tvayā api hi eṣṭa vyava na hi tām anicchan jauvitum api śanayāḥ kim punar vivaditum iti ced satya meṣṭavyā eva tathā api kasya pakṣe mā yujyata iti nirūpayitum pṛcchāmi atas tām brahi mā ced satī  sa dvitīyatva mā ātmanaḥ atas ca ajāna bhāvaḥ tam vinā api mad vitīyatā vā āpatet  mā ātmā eva ced  madā bhāvāt  madā ajñānā bhāvaḥ nirhetu tvam ca tasya asma hetu tve api ātmanaḥ api mādi tvāt ajñāna āśraya abhāvaḥ mādi tvam vā ajñānasya anityā śrayama jñānam iti ca vipratipitam atha abhāvaḥ ajñāna nivṛttiḥ  abhāvaḥ api ātmā eva ced  uktī dopaḥ tad dharmaḥ ced  dharmasya bheda ibhede ca uktaḥ  dopaḥ tathā madamattva ca na ca tad samasti anirvacanauya tve tad eva ajñānam anyadā asti iti nirmokṣaḥ na ca asti prakāra antaram na api tucchatā iṣṭā asaṃbhavāt  kiṃca  bhāvasya eva nittira bhāvaḥ prasiddhaḥ abhāvasya eva ca bhāvaḥ atas ajñānasya nittiḥ na abhāvī bhāvaḥ vā bhāva abhāvaḥ  vā anirvācya tvāt  na ca anyaḥ  nivṛtti prakāraḥ prasiddhaḥ asti na ca tad eva tasya nittiḥ prasiddhi virodhāt  na ca anirvacanauya antaram tad nittiḥ viśeṣā bhāvāt  jñāna hetutva ayogāt ca anirvacanīyam hi ajñānam tad kārya vā na ca ubhayam tad  jñānāt bhavati iti icchami anādi ca ajñānam na ca ajñāna antaram icchasi tad nitte śca anirvacanīya tve caitanyasya iva anivṛtti pramaṅgaḥ ajñāna hetu tvam ca syāt  atas anirvacanīyasya nivṛttyam aṃbhavā dajñāna nivṛtteḥ ca prasiddhatva at na anirvacanīyam annānam atas  bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ  vā syāt  tayoḥ eva nivṛtteḥ upapatteḥ pramiddeḥ ca abhāvaḥ ca bhāva antaram bhāva antara dharmaḥ  vā na tu tucchaḥ apra meya tvāt  abhāvaḥ tu prameyaḥ anyathā tad i avahārā yogāt atas  jñāna abhāvaḥ ajñānam tasya ca jñāna bhāvaḥ  nivṛttiḥ bhāvaḥ hi abhāvamya nivṛttiḥ jñāna ajñānayoḥ ca bhāva abhāva tvam bhāva abhāva pramāṇa gamya tvam ca mavaireṣṭavyam anyathā tu ajñāna nivṛtteḥ prasiddhāyāḥ  anupapatteḥ na hi tām anicchataḥ  jauvanam apautyuktam yadā tu ajñānam bhāva eva  tadā api jñānam tasya abhāvaḥ bhāva antara tvāt atas tad eva tad nittiḥ jñāna bhāve ajñāna nitti prasiddheḥ na ca rūpya ādi ajñāna kāryam ajñānam hi nāma ātmanaḥ apariṇāmaḥ anya vastuni vā vijñānam ubhayathā api ātma samavāyi tad  rūpya ādi tu na tathā bhāti atas  na ajñāna kāyam tad  kiṃtu śuktiḥ eva samyak agṛhyamāṇā bhāva antara rūpya ākārā bhāti tasyām tu samyak gṛhītāyām na idam rajatam iti śukti rūpyayoḥ itaretarā bhāva grāhi jñānam utpadyate atas  nābānirvacanīyam kiṃci dāti dahmate nivartyate vā jñānena na hi jñānam kasyacid āhakam prasiddham na api nivartakam svābhāva vyatirekeṇa svābhāvasya api nivṛttiḥ eva na nivartakam jñānam bodhakam eva tu arthasya atas  yadi nāma atra asat kiṃcid bhāmeta tasya bodhayet eva abhāvam tad  na tu kuryāt  yadi kuryāt  tathā api abhāvavataḥ  na anirvacanīya tā ata ādi antavataḥ  jaḍa syānirvācyasya kasyacid abhāvāt na anyasya api jaḍatva ādinā anirvācya tā anumeya iti sarvasya sattvāt  jñāna anivartya tvāt ca bandhasya karmaṇā eva tad nivṛttiḥ jñānasya tu anivartaka tvāt na āca mamuccayaḥ api karmaṇā upāsana ajñānam nivartakam iti ced  tad api kama eva mānasam atas  na samuccayaḥ pramāṇa jñānasya atas  brahma jñānam api kartṛm aṃskāra dvāreṇa karmaṇi eva upayujyate tajñānasya para artha tvāt  phala śrutiḥ artha vādaḥ karma hetu tve api mukta nityatva manāt ti śruteḥ nitya tvāt dā bandha pradhvam sasya anyathā tu ātmanaḥ amuktiḥ eva ajñāna jatvā bhāvāt bandhasya jñāna anivartya tvāt na hi jñānam svābhāvāt anya bastu nivartayati iti uktam ajñāna ja tve api tasya anirvācya tve nivṛtti asaṃbhava uktaḥ tasmāt na jñānāt mokṣaḥ karmaṇā eva mokṣaḥ  na vā mokṣa iti ced  na ayam doṣaḥ ajñāna nihatteḥ prakāra antara saṃbhavāt tad asaṃbhava eka nimittaḥ  hi ayam doparāśiyペḥ tvayā prapañcitaḥ mad asat sat asat anirvacanīya prakārebhyaḥ  hi anya prakāra eva ajñānasya nittiḥ ī uktā anirvacanīya tvāt tasya ukta prakārāṇām tvayā eva nirasta tvāt  nirvācyānām eva hi te nivṛtti prakārā anirvacanauyāntāḥ anirvacanīyā api nivṛttiḥ sata eva ātma ākāśa ādeḥ atas anya prakārā iva ajñānasya anirvācyasya nitiḥ anurūpā yakṣa anurūpaḥ  hi baliḥ tarhi tad eva tasya nitiḥ  na prasiddhi virodhāt  jñāna hetutva ayogāt ca ata eva na anyat anirvācyam na api śūnyam śūnyāt kaḥ viśeṣa iti ceta ajñāna nitti tvam eva na hi śūnyasya idam lakṣaṇam syāt ced  astu aikyam ajñāna nivṛttau kim pramāṇa miti ced  nivṛttim ihiḥ eva yasya svarūpe api na asti pramāṇam tasya nivṛttau kaḥ pramāṇam mugayate tammādyathā anirvacanīyam prasidda mayana ātma vidā nyāya balāt abhyu petam  evam tad nitti prakāraḥ api nyāya balāt eva aprasidaḥ  api abhyapeyaḥ itas anyathā ajñāna tad nityoḥ asaṃbhavāt na hi ātmanaḥ apariṇāmaḥ anya vastuni vijñānam vā anjānam jñāna pariṇāmaḥ ca tad nittiḥ iti yuktam  ātmanaḥ pariṇā mā anupapatteḥ niravayava tvāt  māvayavasya eva hi mṛd ṣṭaura ādeḥ pariṇāmaḥ  dṛśyate na tu niravayavasya ākāśasya atas  na ātmā pariṇāmau sāvayavaḥ cevaṭādi vanityam syāt  niravayavasya api ced  pariṇāma ssyāt  ma kasnasya eva iti apariṇatam rūpa antaram na asya avaśiṣyeta atas tad āśritāni apari ṇāma antarāṇi api tadā eva na myuḥ iti sarve jñāna pariṇāmā stadā eva syaḥ sarva prāc abhāvānām nivṛtteḥ na ekadā eva sarve sya virodhāt iti ced nā ekaḥ api aviśeṣāt  atha eka  ssyāt tathā api itare na anyadā api syuḥ tadā sva prāga bhāva abhāvāt atha taiḥ vinā api te syuḥ  ajñānasya jñānam nitti riti na midhyeta jñānānām utpattim vinā api tad prāga bhāvānām nivṛtteḥ teṣu ca nivṛtteṣu api jñānānām anutpatteḥ paśāt ca utpatteḥ evam na ekam api jānam annānasya nivṛttiḥ artha tahāṣa parijihīrpayā svābhāva nittiḥ jānam eva iti ṣe tadā ekasya ātmanaḥ  ekam eva jñānam jñāna abhāvaḥ api eka eva tad āśraya iti vācyam anyathā marva jñānānām yugapad bhāva pramaṅgāt  marva abhāva nivṛttaḥ na ca ekanya niraṃśasya aneke pariṇāmā yugapad saṃbhavanti na api krameṇa krama pakṣa jānamya svābhā nivṛttitva anupapattet pamya akta tvāt syā nmatam  jāna antarasya svābhāva tvāt  jānamya tad nitti tvam yujyata iti tad ca ayuktam    niraṃśasya krameṇa api aneka pari ṇāmām aṃbhavāta pūrva pariṇāma anupayuktasya tasya apariṇatasya rūpa antaramya abhāvāt  tad bhāve ca māśatva prāpteḥ pūrva pari ṇāma upayuktasya ca tad abhāve abhāvāt tad bhāve ca pariṇāmā ntara abhāvāt  bhāve ca marva pariṇāmānām yugapad bhāvaḥ ma ca na iṣṭaḥ virodhāt  yathā ca aikamya niraṃśamya an eka pariṇāmā eka rūpa tvāt ekammin kṣaṇe virudhyante tathā krameṇa api eka rūpatva aviśepāt na hi tanya pūrva uttara kālayoḥ upacayaḥ apa cayaḥ  vā svarūpa bhedaḥ asti mṛd ādīnām tu vāyu ādi bhṛtā vayavānupraveśena upacaya apacaya ādim abhava akrameṇa api pariṇāmā bhavanti ātmanaḥ tu eka rūpa tvāt eka pariṇāma abhyupagame api tatra eva mama āpta tvāt tad abhāve abhāvāt na pariṇāma antaram aṃbhavaḥ tad abhāve api ātmā bhavati iti ced  na bheda abhāvāt tayoḥ bhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ vā mahā eva syāt  anyathā ekasya eva yugapad bhāvā bhāvau  iti viruddham uktam syāt  tathā hi kṛtsnaḥ api ātmā pūrva pariṇāma ātmanā eva jātaḥ na asya kiṃcid pūrvarūpam sthitam asti atas  pariṇāma nivṛttau katham ātmā na nivarteta tad sthitau vā katham pariṇāmaḥ  na tiṣṭhet  yadi api ātmā pūrva pariṇāme samāptaḥ tathā api na sa pariṇāma ssarva ātmanā nivartate kim tu tasya ekaḥ aśaḥ
