param jñānam na asti tad eva abādhyam anyat sarva bādhyam eva syāt  rūpya jñānasya aniṣedha ātmaka tvāt pūrva ābādhaka tā iti ced tad na viruddha artha tvāt tadā adhakatva upapatteḥ niṣedha ātmakam api hi virodhāt eva bādhate anyathā tu aviruvā arthāni api bādheta na ayam purupaḥ  na jīvati iti vā bhramaḥ sarvān eva puruṣa jīvati pratyayān pūrvān niṣedha ātmaka tvāt  bādheta eva abhramaḥ tu na jīvati iti pratyayaḥ jīvati pratyayān sutarām bādheta abādhya tvāt  tasya ca antya tvāt punar jīvati pratyaya abhāvāt atas ca kadācid api jīvanam na syāt  tad ca tava aniṣṭam atas  viruddha arthatva ādiḥ na bādhya bādhaka bhāve hetuḥ nanu puṃsaḥ jauvane nivṛtte tad pratyayeṣu ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupa labdhau jīvana abhāva jñānam tatra iti avirodhaḥ tatra iti ced ā iva matrā api rūpye asati tajñāne ca prāpta anupalabdhau rūpyā bhāvanānam nyāyyam atas atra api virodha eva yuktaḥ anyathā tava api evam virodhāt ukta doṣa prasaṅgāt antavatām prāga pyabhāva eva iti uktam syāt  kaḥ ca virodhaḥ  nāma sva artha niṣṭhayoḥ jñānayoḥ na hi ekasmi bapi rūparama ādinānānām virodhaḥ tvayā iṣṭaḥ nanu ekasya api ane kāni rūpa ādauni bhāva rūpāṇi saṃbhavanti tathā dṛṣṭa tvāt  na tu ekasya eka rūpasya ekasmin  eva deśe kāle ca bhāva abhāvī maṃbhavataḥ anyatra adṛṣṭa tvāt tathā atas ta jñānayoḥ virodha iti ced tad na dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭyoḥ ta jñānayoḥ avirodhāt  tau ced bhāva abhāvau dṛṣṭau dṛṣṭa tvāt eva ekasya api tau maṃbhavataḥ rūpa ādivat  atas ta jñāna yona virodhaḥ rūpa ādi jñānavat  adṛṣṭau ceta tad jñānayoḥ abhāvāt na tad virodhaḥ nanu anekāni api bhāva rūpāṇi saṃbhavanti ekasya na tu bhāva abhāvau anyatra adṛṣṭa tvāt  na ayam dopaḥ anyatra adṛṣṭa tve api atra dṛṣṭa tvāt  maṃbhavata eva yathā anyatra mahādṛṣṭam api rūpa dayam namake dṛṣṭa tvāt  saṃbhavati –evam rūpyasya api bhāvā bhāva ākhyam rūpa dayam dṛṣṭam ced  saṃbhavati eva bhāva rūpaiḥ api aneka rūpa tā ekasya dṛṣṭa tvāt eva maṃbhavati ced  saṃbhavatu na punāyataḥ ekam aneka rūpam ca iti vipratiṣedhāt purastā nirasta tvāt ca aneka rūpa tāyāḥ  ekasya ata ekasya api bhāvasya bhāva rūpaiḥ api aneka tvam bhāva ātmanā eka rūpaiḥ api dṛṣṭa tvāt  saṃbhavati ced  kim iti na saṃbhavati bhāva abhāvābhyām virūpa tvam ekasya dṛṣṭam saṃbhavatitarāma dṛṣṭa tvāt  dairūpya saṃbhavāca kiṃca  bhinna abhinnam vastu iti icchana bhinnam bhavati na bhavati ca iti bhāva abhāva rūpam vastu iccha ti eva yena rūpeṇa bhinnam na tena eva rūpeṇa abhinnam kiṃtu anyena iti ced tathā api ekam rūpi bhinnam bhavati na bhavati ca rūpa antara kalpanāyām anavasthā na at nanu abhinnam iti bhinnasya abhāvaḥ  na ucyate kiṃtu tad eva abheda dharmakam atas  bheda abheda dharmakam vastu iti bhinnā bhinna śabda arthaḥ atas  na bhāva abhāva ātma tā iti ced  tau bhedā bhedau bhinnau ced astunaḥ na tad damaum vastu antaravat  abhinnau ced  dharmi vannatat dhamaum bhinna abhinnau ced maya uktam siddham dharma antara kalpanāyām anavasthā prāptaḥ na bhinnau na api abhinnau na api bhinna abhinnau vastunaḥ  bheda abhedau na ca mithas  na api anyata iti ced bheda śabde nañaḥ kaḥ arthaḥ yadi bhedāt anyaḥ  bheda virudyaḥ  vā tadā bheda abhedayoḥ bhedassiṅghaḥ na hi bhedam vinā anyatva virudda tve maṃstaḥ bheda abhāvaḥ ced abhedaḥ bheda tad abhāvau  ekatra eva prāptau atas ca yad bhinnam bhavati tad eva bhinnam na bhavati iti bhinna abhinna śabda artha ssaṃpannaḥ evam ca sati yad svataḥ anyat asvayam tad api svayam yad ca svayam tad api svatas anyat asvayam iti svayam anyat ca svayam bhavati na bhavati ca anyat ca anyat  svayam ca bhavati na bhavati ca iti marvasya vastunassarvadā sarva ātmanā bhāva abhāva avicchan kim iti rūpyam āce tau na icchasi na ced tad jñāne na staḥ atha rūpya deṣāt anyatra api tau na icchasi tarhi bheda abheda vāda āgraham tyaja tān icchataḥ tasya asiddheḥ na tyajāmi tam tau ca na icchāmi na hi abhedaḥ  bhedasya abhāvaḥ na api tabiruddhaḥ maha sthiteḥ kim tu anyasman  eva na ca anyān anyaḥ tasmāt na uktadopaprāptiḥ iti ced evam tarhi bheda abhedayoḥ abheda haunayoḥ bhedasya iṣṭa tvāt  bheda vastunoḥ api abheda hīna tvāt  bheda eṣṭavyaḥ bheda abhedayoḥ iva tathā bhedāt eva na dharma dharmi bhāvaḥ tayoḥ evam abhedasya api bhedaḥ  vastunaḥ ataharma tvam ca iṣyatām atas  na asti bheda abheda dharmakam kiṃcid  evam atas anye api dharmā abheda haunāḥ ced  bhinnā eva iti na vastu dharma āssyuḥ atas adharmakam eva vastu syāt  atha te dharmā bhinna abhinnā iṣyante dharmatva siḍī artham tarhi bheda abhedau  api tathā eva iccha na anyathā tau dhau syātām atas ca mad aktam siddham nanu abheda śabdaḥ  na najma māsaḥ akṣa ādi śabdavat atas  nañartha cayān āśrayaṇāt mithas  bheda abhāvāt bheda abhedayoḥ na kutaścid bheda abhedau tayoḥḥ taḥ na api anyeṣām dharmāṇām atas anayoḥ teṣām ca dharma tvam api na virudhyate atas  dharmiṇām eva anyonya apekṣayā bheda abhedau dhau dṛṣṭau na tu dharmāṇām kutaścid apauti dharmiṇām eva bhinna abhinna tā bhāva rūpa dharma dvayavat tayā na punarbhāva abhāva rūpa tayā atas  na ukta doṣa prāptiḥ iti ced tad ca ayuktam bheda abheda dharma kavaḥ tu abhāva prasaṅgāt  na hi mithas  bhedā bheda haunānām dharma dharmi bhāvaḥ  nyāyyaḥ dharmāṇām iva para sparam anyathā dharmāṇām api anyonyam dharma dharmi bhāva ssyāt  atas ca sarva dharmāṇām sarva dharma dharmi tvam marva vastu dharmāṇām ca sarva vastu dharma tvam iti aniyamaḥ  dharma dharmiṇām syāt  tatas  asmin pace adharmaka tvam vastunaḥ aniyamaḥ  vā ukta rasyāt  atas  na ayam pakṣam mādhīyān apicedam bhavān praṣṭavyaḥ kim ekaikaḥ  dharmaḥ  bhedaḥ anyaḥ  vā svataḥ api svayam na bhinnaḥ na abhinnaḥ uta abhinna eva na bhinnaḥ yadi abhinna eva tadā yasya bhedaḥ  yatas  na asti tanya abhedaḥ tatas tad svarūpa tvam ca ekasmin dṛṣṭam iti anya api bheda haunāḥ tatas  tad abhinnāḥ ta svarūpāḥ ca bhavitum arhantauti eka eva dharma ssyāt na dvitīyaḥ  dharmaḥ  dharmom vā  marveṣām eva dharma dharmiṇām tatas  bheda abhāva sya iṣṭa tvāt  tathā ādye api paṣṭaḥ  tasvarūpa antra kiṃcid ati ricyate tatas  bheda abheda hīna tvāt  tasvarūpasya anyasya api tad lakṣaṇa tvāt marvasya tad svarūpa tvasiīḥ ata ubhayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ ekam eva vastu eka rūpam midam tad api yadi bhinna abhinnam iṣyeta tad eva tathā asti na asti ca iti bhāva abhāva rūpam iṣṭam syāt  atas  bhinna abhinna pakṣāṇām ayam pakṣaḥ pāpiṣṭhaḥ nanu pakṣa antare api anupapatti smamānā bhedā bhedayoḥ bheda abheda antara abhyupagame anavasthā prāptaḥ atha ucyeta abhedaḥ  bheda hīna tā eva vastunaḥ na tu dharmaḥ  bheda ādivat iti tathā api bhedasya bhede bheda abhede vā anavasthānāt abhede ca vastu mātram eva iti abhinnam ekam vastu syāt  tatra kutaḥ bhinna abhinna tvena dharmadhā ādi bhāva iti ced  satyam ata eva ayam pakṣaḥ pāpiṣṭha uktaḥ abheda śabda sya anasamāma tvam abhedasya ca dharma tvam tasya ca vastu antara apekṣa tvam svarūpā pekṣayā ca abhedasya abhāvaḥ  vastunaḥ  dharmāṇām ca vastunaḥ  bhedena bhedena ca abhāvaḥ tathā api astitvam sva para dharmāṇām ca bheda abheda honatayā aviśeṣa ityādi pratīti viruddham nyāya viruddham ca asmin pakṣe bahu kalpitam iti atas anye api pakṣāḥ pāpā eva ayam tu pakṣaḥ pāpiṣṭha iti na ca atra bheda abheda dūṣaṇam sādhanam vā prastutam kiṃtu bheda abheda vādinā yugapad bhāva abhāvau  ekasya vastana eṣṭavyau atas  rūpyasya api tau tasya na virudhyete tajñāne ced sta iti etad siyartham eva anyat uktam atas tad siddham tasmāt na rūpyasya bādhaḥ  nyāyyaḥ tad niṣedhena abheda jñānena iva bhedasya atha ūcyeta  rūpyasya mithyātva āt ta jñānasya apramāṇa tvāt  tad irodhi tvāt niṣedhasya pramāṇa tayā ca balauya tvāt tena rūpyasya bādhaḥ  nyāyya iti kutas tarhi tad mithyā tvam siddham bādhya tvāt iti ced  tarhi bādhya tvāt mithyātvam tatas tajñānasya apramāṇa tā tatas  niṣedhasya balauyaḥ tvam tatas  rūpyasya bādhyatā iti pūrva pūrva āśraya tvāt attarottarasya na ekam api sidhyet  na hi eṣām ekam api anyatasmiddham na evam amithyātva pramāṇatva tulya bala tā bādhya tvānām anyonya āśraya tā bodhakasya jñānasya svata eva pramāṇa tvāt niṣedhavat tad siddhau ca itareṣām middheḥ anyathā mithyātvam bhedasya api syāt  abheda jñānena bādhāt  bheda abheda jñāne api hi idam ammāt bhinnam na ida masmāt bhinnam iti niṣedhya niṣedha ātmanā eva iṣya anyathā tayoḥ eka ca asaṃbhavāt tathā ahi yad apekṣayā yatra bheda jñāna mabhūt tad apekṣayā eva taca eva ced abheda jñānam api bhāva prameyam bhavet  tad api bheda prameyam eva syāt  na bhāva antara prameyam bheda jñāna antaravat na hi yad apekṣayā yatra dīrgha jñānam abhūt  tad apekṣayā eva tatra hasva jñānam syāt  tad apekṣayā eva tu tatra sthūla jñānam syāt iti ced na aṇu apekṣa tvāt tasya hasvā pekṣam ca dīrgha jñānam atas apekṣyam tayaḥ bhinnam viṣayaḥ ca bhinnaḥ bheda abheda jñānayoḥ api apekṣyau viṣayau ca bhinnau mthūla dīrgha jñānayoḥ ivā iti ced  tarhi na bhinnasya abhinnatā na api bhinnamya bhinna tā midhyet  bhinnam hi apekṣya bheda jñānam bhinne bhavati iti iṣṭam tvayā atas  na evam abheda jñānam eṣṭavyam api tu abhinnam ātmānam eva apekṣya tatra eva bhavati iti anyathā tayoḥ pekṣya viṣaya abhedāt abhinna arthatva prasaṅgāt  evam ca mati bhedā bheda jāne anyonya viṣayam na eva spaśata iti bhinnayoḥ abheda jñānam na syāt  atas tad icchatā bheda jñāna pratibhāta rūpa niṣedhā tmakam eva tadā iṣṭavyam iti abheda jñānam api bheda bādhakam syāt  yadi rūpya niṣedhaḥ  rūpya bādhakasya at  na bhedaḥ  bādhyaḥ tajñānasya pramāṇa tvāt artha kriyā kāritayā iti ced tathā rūpyam api arūpyasya rūpya tvām abhavāt  tad rapyam mithyā iti ced tad na tajñānena tasya maṃbhāvita tvāt  bhedasya iva abhinna saṃbandhinaḥ ta jñānena kim bahunā uktena sarvathā yā rūpyasya gatissā prapañcasya api prāpnoti atas tam icchatā na rūpyam bādhyam kiṃca  rūpyasya mithyātvam tvayā iṣṭam na tāvat asattvam sattvasya iṣṭa tvāt  na api pramāṇa abhāvaḥ tad dodhaka jñānasya iṣṭa tvāt  jñānam tasya asti na tu pramāṇam iti ced  nanu jñānam eva pramāṇam matyam tathā api na mavam jñānam pramāṇam kiṃtu yathārtha pramāṇam ayathārtham apramāṇam iti ced  kim ida mayathārtha tvam nāma jñānamya kim artha nyūnatva muta ādhikyam yadi nyūna tā tadā na kiṃcid api jñānam marva ātmanā artha vyāpnota auti marvam eva ayathārtham apramāṇam syāt  atha dhikyam tadā api artha śūnyam api jñāna rūpam prāpnoti tad ca niṣṭam ayuktam ca jñāyate arthaḥ anena iti hi jñānam atas  jeyā artha abhāve tajñānam api na syāt  atas  yāva dyathā ca iṣyate jñānam tāvān  tathā eva arthom jñeyaḥ asti iti abhyupeyaḥ anyathā na tad  jñānam syāt  pratyakṣam api anumeyam tu dara utsāritam tad  jñānam tāk artham aṃvid abhāve tad abhāvāt maṃu id api tathā artha abhāve na tad saṃvid syāt  atas  yadi api na kṛtsnam artham ekaikam jñānam bodhayati tathā api yāvantam bodhayati tāvān  tathā eva asti jñānam ca na artha śūnyam asti tasmāt ayathā rtha jñāna abhāvāt sarvam eva jñānam yathārtha tvāt  pramāṇam atas  jñānam asti ced  pramāṇam asya iva rūpyasya na idam rūpyam astauti ced  tad jñānam api na asti asti ced  rūpyam api asti eva sārthatva ajñānasya na asti ced rūpyam katham tad asti iti avocaḥ asti rūpyam na tu śakti ātmanā astauti ced  tad yathā na asti rūpyam tathā tajñānam api na asya iva sārthatva ajñānasya atas asattvāt rūpyasya tajñānam apramāṇam iti na śakyam vaktum asataḥ  jñāna abhāvāta jñānavataḥ ca sattvāta na hi abhāva jñānam apaucchasi artha śūnyam kim punarbhāva jñānam atas tattvāt  pramāṇavat tvāt ca na rūpyasya mithyātvam mati arūpyavat  anyathā tasya api mithyātvam kaḥ  nivārayet  nanu na idam rajatam iti jñānāt  śukti ātmanā rūpyasya amat tvam niścitam tathā api idam rajatam iti tasya eva śukti ātmanā eva astitvam abubudha jñānam atas asya abhāve api bhāva jñānam stauti ced aḥ tu tarhi pūrva uktam bairūpyam rūpyasya gati antara abhāvāt abhayoḥ api jñānayoḥ artha śūnyatva anupapatteḥ yadi nāma śukti rūpyayoḥ akyam jñātam api mad  na asti eva tathā api tasya eva āmattva mithyātva apramāṇaka tvāni syuḥ na tu rūpyasya mad tvāt tasya atha tasya api tāni syuḥ aikya abhāvāt śukti rūpyayoḥ tarhi ata eva śukrapi tāni syuḥ ekyā bhāva aviśeṣe api yadi na śuktamsyuḥ rūpyasya api na syuḥ mad tvam ceṣṭam dvayoḥ api śuktaḥ pratyakṣeṇa api dṛṣṭatva āt tāni virudhyanta iti ced  rūpyam api kvāpi pratyakṣam dṛṣṭam eva anyathā tasya mattva ayogāt śukya ātmakam tad na anyatra dṛṣṭam iti ced  śuktiḥ api rūpya ātmikā na dṛṣṭā eva anyathā abādhya rūpyā syāt  śuddhā śukti dṛṣṭā iti ced  rūpyam api tathā kvāpi bhrāntau dṛṣṭā śuktiḥ pratyakṣeṇa api pratyabhijñāyate na tathā rūpyam iti ced kimatas tava siddham yadi rūpyasya api aikyavat punar  pratyabhijñā abhāvāt amat tvam rūpyam mad iti mad pratijñā virodhaḥ atha śukti rūpyayaḥ lakṣaṇyam tathā api tayā usmad tve bādhaḥ abādhaḥ vā tulyaḥ  nyāyyaḥ tulya eva iti cetna tathā prasiḍya bhāvāt  bhavatām api tathā vyava idaṃrūpyayoḥ akyam na bādhyam hāra abhāvāt  tasmāt śukti rūpyayoīyoḥ api sattve tad aikya syā sattva bādhyatva aprāmāṇika tve ] api śuktar iva rūpyasya api na asattva ādīni syuḥ anyathā śukrapi tad prasaṅgāt  tasmāt na rūpyam bādhyam śuktivat  na api tayoḥ akyam bādhyam aikyam na astauti jñānā bhāvāta na idam rajatam iti tu jñānam   tad ca mattvāt na bādhyam iti uktam ekya ca jñāyate ced asti eva śuktyā divat  bādhā bhāvāca tasmāt sarva jñānānām pramāṇa tvāt tava na kiṃcid dādhyam paśyāmaḥ nanu aikya bādhyam na ca evayam na astauti jñāna abhāvaḥ  dopāya bhrama anumāri tvā dādhasya na hi anayorakyam astauti jñāta bhedayā uṭdhi karaṇa tayā bhramaḥ kiṃtu idam rajatam iti māmānādhikaraṇyena vājñāta bhedayoḥ atas  na idam rajatam iti eva bādhaḥ  nyāyyaḥ na punar aikyam na astauti  tad anurūpa bhrama abhāvāt yadi tu anayā urakyam na astauti bādhassyāt  saḥ aprāpta bādhassyāt  tathā aprāpta tvāt  tasmāt idam rajatam iti aikya bhramasya na idam rajatam iti eva bādhaḥ  yuktaḥ ata aikya bādhyam iti ced  todam brūhi kim śukti rūpyayoḥ māte bhede bādhaka jñānam syāt  uta ajñāta eva yadi ajñāte tadā kim bheda jñānam eva bādhakam uta anyat  abhāva jñānam yadi anyat tadā bheda sya ajñāta tvāt  yathāprāptam marvam eva bādheta  rūpyam idam tayoḥ akyam ca tad ca aniṣṭam atha bheda jñānam eva bādhakam taca ayuktam aniṣedha rūpa tvāt tasya aniṣedha ātmaka tve api aikya jñāna virodhāt bheda jñānam tahādhata iti ced  aikya jñāna viruddham ced  bheda jñānam tad ākrānte viṣaye na syāt  bheda jñānam avirodhāt eva syāt ced  na tad virodhi tabādhaka ca syāt  anyathā bheda jñāna ākrānte viṣaye punar aikya jñānam syāta tad ādhakam ca syāt  nanu bheda jñāna bādhitaḥ  rūpyam ādyai kya bhramaḥ punar na bhavet  bhavan api doṣa vaśāt  bheda niścayavataḥ  na tam bādheta tarhi aikya niścayavataḥ api na bheda nānam bhavet  bhavat api na tam bādheta atasmaḥ api na bhramaḥ tasmāt aikya bheda niścayayoīyoḥ api jñāna tvāt maṃśaya ātmaka tvāt  sva artha avyabhicārāca pramāṇa tvāt na bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ  yaktaḥ anyathā tayoḥ anyonya bādhya tvāt na aneka rūpam kiṃcid syāt  syāced  na kiṃcid ādhyam syāt  tasmāt na bheda nāna mātra bādhakam aikya jñānasya atha jñāte bhede tayoḥ itaretarābhāva jñānam aikya bādhakam tadā api itare tara abhāva jñānānām marveṣām eva bādhakatva prasaṅgaḥ itaretara bhāva jñāne jāte tad abhāva jñānam bādhakam na anyathā iti na ati prasaṅga iti ced   katham bhāva jñāna rakṣitam viṣayam abhāva jñānam tad agocara varti apaharet  yadi bhāva jñāna gocara eva bhāva jñānam api varteta tayoḥ eka artha tvāt bhāva jñānam tena dṛḍhau bhavet na tu bādhyeta tad eka artha bhāva jñāna antareṇa iva bhāva artha tve ca abhāva jñānani api bhāva jñāna tā eva syāt  tasmāt na eka gocara tvam bhāva abhāva jñānayoḥ bhinna gocaram ca abhāva jñānam prāpta anupalabdha avabhāva jñānam iva bhāva jñānam na bādheta nanu prāpta anupalabdha  abhāva jñānam deśa kāla antaraḥ bhāvam bodha yati idam tu tatra eva iti ced tathā api bhinna artham ced  tahat eva na bādhakam abhinna artha tve ca uktam tasmāt   jñānam mat na kiṃcid ādhyam asti api ca idam bhavān praṣṭavyaḥ kim śukti rūpyayoḥ itaretara bhāvaḥ bādhyaḥ kim vā idam aṃśasya rūpyasya ca na tāvat śukti rūpyayoḥ tayoḥ itaretara bhāvasya apratīta tvāt na apaudaṃrūpyayoḥ tayoḥ api bhrānti kāle bheda pratīteḥ aniṣṭa tvāditaretara bhāva pratītyabhāvāt   bheda apekṣa tvāt itaretara bhāvasya atas  yadi itaretara bhāvaḥ  nāma bhavet  ma bhinnayoḥ eva bhavet na tu ekasmin  abhinne na hi ekam abhinnam itare tara bhūtam vadanti tasmāt na idaṃrūpyayoḥ apautaretara bhāvaḥ  bādhyaḥ apratīta tvāt apratīta niṣedhasya ca ābādhaka tvāt  idaṃrūpyām śayoḥ api mithas  bhedaḥ pratīta iti ced  tarhi itaretara bhāvastayā ūna pratīta iti nāmau bādhyaḥ tathā api tayoḥ aṃśī ekaḥ  bhātauti ced bhātu na asau tayoḥ itaretara bhāvaḥ atas  ana tad niṣedhena niṣedhyaḥ na ca tayoḥ aṃśī na asti iti niṣedhaḥ asti tasmāt sa bhāti ced  san  ā iva iti na niṣedhyam paśyāmaḥ yadi nāma aṃśī niṣedhyaḥ tasya sa aṃśasya eva niṣe dhya tvāt śukti rūpyayoḥ api tad aṃśa tvāt niṣedha pramaṅgaḥ tad niṣedhena śukti rūpyayoḥ atad aṃśa tvasya niṣedhāt  prāk  asidatvāt  siddha tve ca niṣedha anarthakyāt tasmāt aṃśi bādha kalpa namana rthāya eva iti na tad  kāryam śukti rūpyayoḥ itaretara bhāva niṣedhena eva aṃśinaḥ api niṣedham iḍeḥ tad bhāne api na ukta doṣa iti cetna ukta uttara tvāt  śukti rūpyayoḥ bha de jñāte ajñāte ca itaretara bhāva jñānām aṃbhavāt  tad niṣedhaḥ aprāpta niṣedha eva iti na tena kiṃcid dādhyam iti yuktam api ca jñāte bhede anyonya abhāva jñānam iṣṭam na ca jñāta bhedayoḥ aanyonya bhāvaḥ tadā bhāti na api pūrvam tadā bhedasya ajñāta tvāt  atas api anyonya abhāva jñānam aprāpta niṣedhaḥ bheda jñānam ca aikya jñāna virodhi ced  na bhavet iti uktam bhavet ced  ekatva jñāna avirodhi eva bhavet bheda jñānam tadanu mārī ā iva ca anyonya abhāva jñānam ata idam rajatam iti jñānam susthitam eva na idam rajatam iti jñāne jāte api katham ca eka tvena jñātayoḥ bhedaḥ  jñāyeta bheda jñānam hi prati yogi apekṣam anyaḥ ca pratiyogī na hi svayam eva svasya na ca ajñāta bhedaḥ pratiyogī yathā na svayam svasya bhinnaḥ ajñāta bhedaḥ api jātaḥ pratiyogi iti ced  daśa svartha īṣa yugapa gṛhauteṣu navabhyaḥ  bheda ekakasya teṣām yugapad jñāyeta na ca tathā jñāyate atas  na ajñāta bhedaḥ jātaḥ pratiyogau yadā tu ajñāta bhedaḥ api na pratiyogī tadā natarāma jñāta bhedaḥ jñāta aikyaḥ ca atas  na idam aṃśasya rūpyam rūpyasya vā na idam aṃśaḥ pratiyogī syāt  tayoḥ anyatarasya jñāyamāna bhedasya pratiyogi tve anavasthā pratiyogi jñānam ca tayoḥ ekatva jñāna mabādhamānam na jāyeta bādhate ced  tad eva tasya bādhaka miti bheda jñānam abhāva jñānam ca vyartham syāt  tarhi tad eva astu kā bādhaka jñānam iti ced na syāt  anavasthānāt yakta hetubhyaḥ pratyakṣeṇa eva bhedam paśyāmaḥ sa katham macā pahūyeta iti yadi bhavatām abhiniveśa   tathā api nānayoḥ bhedaḥ pratyakṣa dṛśyaḥ rūpyasya apratyakṣa tvāt  amaṃnidhānasya tasya iṣṭa tvāt  tatra yadi ekaḥ  bheda ubhaya dharmaḥ yadi vā pratyeka mekaikaḥ   ubhayathā api rūpya dharma tayā na bhedaḥ pratyakṣa dṛśyaḥ rūpya sya apratyakṣa tvāt  yad ca rūpyamya bodhakam jñānam tad tasyāḥ  bhedam eva bodhayati idam aṃśāt  na tu bhedam atas  rūpyasya bheda āmiddheḥ abhedasya eva ca siddheḥ idam aṃśāta tasya pratyakṣa tve api idam aṃśasya na rūpyā daḥ draṣṭum śakyaḥ na ha audam rūpya aṅginnam rūpyam tu abhinnam eva asmāt iti yuktam atas  nānayoḥ bhedaḥ pratyakṣa dṛśyaḥ na api anumāna ādi gamyaḥ tad saṃbaddha liṅga ādi abhāvāt  atas  bheda jñāna abhāvāt na anyonya abhāva jñānam api tasmāt aikya mapi na bādhyam katham ca bheda jñānam abhāva jñānam vā ekatva bhrama nivṛttau  upa yogi syāt  yadi bheda jñānāt aikya bhramaḥ  na nivarteta abhāva jñānam tam katham nivartayet  tad api hi anyonya abhāvam sva prameyam bodhayat tad ajñānam eva nivartayet na anya dastu na ca ajñānam aikyam tajñānam vā vastu ca jñānam iṣṭam atas  naikyata jñāne abhāva jñānam nivartayati aikyasya abhāvam tajñānam bodhayatauti ced  asti ta|kyam yatas tasya abhāvaḥ  bodhyate na hi asataḥ abhāvaḥ  bodhyaḥ kaḥ ca tasya abhāvaḥ aikyam eva na astauti ced  kaḥ arthaḥ tad eva tasya abhāva iti arthaḥ uta      āāṝ abhāva eva aikyam iti na tāvat tad eva tasya abhāva ssyāt  bhāva antaram abhāva iti ukta tvāt  na api aikyam abhāva eva bhāva jñānena bhāvavat  pratīteḥ abhāvavat ca abhāva jñānena apratīteḥ abhāvaḥ ced syāta abhāva jñānena bodhyam syāt  na tu bādhyam tena bādhyam ca tena aikyam iṣṭam na tu bodhyam atas  na abhāvaḥ yadi abhāvaḥ kasya āmau yadi śukti rūpyayoḥ yadi tayoḥ prāc abhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ  vā tad jñāna kāle ma na jāyeta atha anyonya abhāvaḥ tadā na idam rajatam iti ma jñāyeta na vidam rajatam iti bhrānti bādhayoḥ ca vaiparautya māpadyeta tasmāt na tayoḥ abhāva aikyam na api anyasya kasyacita tathā apratīteḥ abhāvaḥ ceta pratiyogi mmaraṇa ādi apekṣam prāpta anupalabdhau  abhāva pramāṇena kasyacid dharma tayā jāyeta aikyam na ca tathā jñāyata iti uktam atas  na prāmāṇikaḥ abhāvaḥ aikyam tuccham ca na iṣyate anirvacanīyam ca tasmāt bhāva eva bhāva ātmanā ca khyāteḥ atas tasyāḥ  bhāvaḥ ced  bodhyaḥ anyaca eva ma bodhyaḥ na tu yaca aikya bhāti tatra eva tatra bhāva khyāteḥ yadi ca aikyam eva tad  abhāvaḥ yadi vā abhāva eva aikyam    ubhayathā api abhāva jñānam api tad eva yathājñātam jñāpayati iti tad aikya jñānam su dṛḍham syāt  tad  anyathā bodhayati abhāva jñānam na tu yathāpūrvam iti ced ki tasya eva rūpa antaram bodhayati uta anyat  ubhayathā api pūrva jñātasya rūpasya na kācid kṣatiḥ tasya ca abhāva jñāna aviṣaya tvam siddham tasmāt sa deva aikyam sattve api tasya śukti rūpya maṃbandhā na asti iti ced maḥ api bhāva jñānena jñātaḥ ced  ekī avatman  eva tasmāt na kiṃcid api bhāva ātmanā jñātam bhāva jñānam apahotum śaknoti iti bhrānti nivṛttau tad na upayogi tathā bhaṃda jñānam api bheda mātra niṣṭha tvāt aniṣedha ātmaka tvāt ca atas  nivartaka abhāvāt idam rajatam iti jñānam pramāṇam musthitam tad aktam  abhāva abhāva dhiyoḥ eka meya tve bhāva dhauḍhā tathā eva bhinna meya tve na atas  bādhyāmti dhaurdhiyā jāna antaram utyadyamānam jñāna antaram nivartayatauti ceta marva jñānānām bādhya bādhaka tvāt  bhrāntyabhrāntitva pramaṅgaḥ bhrānti tvam eva vā marvamya bādhya tvāt  tammādanyatha ākhyāti vādinī bādhyat nānā bhāvāna kācid  bhrāntiḥ marvam eva vā jñānam bhrāntim syāt  tathā ātma khyāti vādinā api syāt eka arthayoḥ bhinnā rthayoḥ ca bādhya bādhakatva ayogāta buddhi ākāraḥ  rūpyam bahivat bhātīni tayā buddhyā jñātum aśakyatvāt evasyā buddheḥ niraṃśāyā grāhya grāhakatva asaṃbhavāt buddeḥ ca buddhi antara aviṣaya tvāt sama tvāt kṣaṇika tvāt ca buḍi antara viṣaya tve ca marva buddhaunā masvayaṃprakāśa tvāt ekasyāḥ  api amiddheḥ svayaṃprakāśa tve ca budda antarasya ātmanaḥ ca aviṣaya tvāt  buddheḥ sā eva ced hiḥ madā kāraḥ  bahisvat bhāti iti tadā eva jānīyāt  bhrāntina syāt  na ca mānya dā jānauyāt  kṣaṇika tvāt  na ca sā sva ātmānam rūpya ākāram bāhyam iva ca jānauyāta na ca anyā tām anya aviṣaya tvāt  kṣaṇikatva ādeḥ ca tatra katham bhramasmidhyet  na ca avidyā ātma vaḍhuveḥ api asti asti ced  tathā api anirvācyā na iṣṭā atasmataḥ  ced  sā anyā ananyā vā buḍeḥ ananyā ced mā api na viṣayaubhavet  buddheḥ ātmavat  anyā api sva saṃvedyā ced  tathā anya saṃvedyā ced avidyā iṣyate anyam aṃvedyā ghaṭa ādayaḥ api eṣṭavyāḥ tadā ātma khyātina sidhyeta atha baddha rūpya ākāra tā bāhya tā ca sva saṃvedya eva  kim tad eva buḍḍhe rūpam uta anya dapi asti yadi tad eva  tad ced mithyā kṛtsya eva buddhiḥ mithyā syāt  atha anyat api asti rūpam amithyā  tarhi tahat eva itara dapya mithyā buddhi rūpa tvāt  anyathā tad api itaravat mithyā syāt  tasmāt sakalā eva buddhi mithyā amithyā vā syāt  na tu asyāḥ kiṃcid rūpam mithyā kiṃcid amithyā iti yuktam mithyā rūpam api sva saṃvedyam ced mithyā syāta tathā eva khyāteḥ na hi yad svayam khyāti tad anyathā khyāti yathā hi khyāti tathā eva tad  yadi tad anyathā khyāti katham tad jñāyeta na hi tad anyena vedyam sva saṃvedya tvāt  na api tad ātmāna manyathā khyātauti vidyāt  avedya tvāt  vedya tve ca anya vedya tvāt  sva saṃvedya tā hāniḥ asva saṃvedya tve na taḍhuḍhe rūpam syāt  tasyāḥ  api asvasaṃvedyatva prasaṅgāt  na hi ekasya baddhesu asaṃvedyam asvasaṃvedyam ca rūpayamanyonya viruddham saṃbhavati buddheḥ ced  kiṃcid rūpam asvayaṃprabham  anyat api tathā eva yuktam buddhi rūpa tvāt  svayaṃprabham ced  kiṃcibuddhi rūpam  anyat api tathā tad rūpa tvāt eka rūpā eva ced uddhiḥ svayaṃprabhā asvayaṃprabhā vā syāt  asvayaṃprabhā eva ceḍuddhiḥ sarva buddhaunām tathā tvāt anyasya ca svayaṃprakāśasya niṣṭa tvāt na kiṃcid bhāmeta tasmāt duddemsvayam prabha tvam icchatā na jaḍam rūpam abhyupeyam yasyāḥ ca tad jaḍam rūpam na tayā tabāhyam ekasya grāhya grāhakatva ayogāt kṛtsnāyāḥ  aṃśaḥ grāhyaḥ ced  grāhakaḥ api aṃśa eva tau ca vyavasthitau aṃśī api grāhyaḥ  grāhakaḥ  vā sya at na ubhaya rūpaḥ ekasya rūpya ayogāt aṃśa antara kalpanāyām anavasthānāt atas  grāhyaḥ  na grāhakaḥ grāhakaḥ api na grāhya iti grāhakāt anyaḥ  bāhyaḥ arthaḥ  na apalapanīyaḥ svayaṃprabha tve ca janma nāśa bheda aśuḍyāt ayaḥ  budhaunām na syaḥ pramāṇa abhāvāta na hi buddhiḥ ātmanaḥ  janma ādi svayam eva jānauyāt  na api bhedam svata eva anyatas  hi bhedaḥ  jñeyaḥ na ca anyonya viṣaya tā buddhaunām ata svayaṃprabha tve buddhaunām ekā abhinnā kūṭasthā buddhiḥ eṣṭavyā atha janma ādaya iṣyante baddaunāma asvayaṃprabhāḥ sarvā buddhayassyaḥ tatas ca ekaḥ abhinnaḥ anantaḥ kūṭastha nitya ātmā abhyupeyaḥ anyathā jagata ānthya pramaṅgāt  tasmāt ātma khyāti vādinaḥ api na bhrama bādhau saṃbhavata iti sthitam __ tathā akhyāti vādinaḥ api akhyātimā ced  bhramaḥ marvassarvadā bhramati eva  yatra kvāpi viṣaye akhyātesmarvadā vidyamāna tvāt asarvajñasya sarvasya yā ani athā pravartayati akhyātiḥ mā bhrāntiḥ anyathā pravṛtti hetaḥ ntitva prasiddheḥ iti ced   tad na na hi akhyātiḥ pravartayati suṣupta ādiṣa pratteḥ yadya pyanyathā pravartamānasya api akhyātiḥ asti tathā api na tambā   khyātiḥ pratihetuḥ suṣuptasya apratteḥ eva khyātiḥ api na anyathā pratihetuḥ vyabhicārāt iti ced  tarhi tābhyā manyā tahetuḥ bhrāntiḥ iṣyatām kā ca iyam akhyātiḥ kim khyātiḥ eva uta khyāti abhāvaḥ na tāvat sya ati abhāvaḥ abhā vasya aniṣṭa tvāt na api khyāti reva marva khyātīnām bhrānti tu apram aṅgāt  amamyakasya atimā̍ntiḥ iti ced am amyavā mapi na mamyavābhāvaḥ abhāvasya aniṣṭa tvāt mamyaktvam eva ca idam amyaktvam samyakasya atiḥ eva amamyaka khyātiḥ ata msamyaya atiāntiḥ iti vipratipivam uktam khyāti śced dhāntiḥ mā kena bādhyeta na hi khyātiḥ khyāti bādhate atipramaṅgāt  na ca ākhyāti sti akhyātya bhāve ca maū janam marvadā marvanasyāt  marva pramāṇānām ca ānarthakyam ajñāta artha abhāvāt na ca jātam eva jñāpayanti pramāṇāni anavasthā prāptaḥ tasmāt na ākhyāti vādinaḥ kācid dhāntiḥ marvā vā khyāti ntimsyāta tathā amatsya ativādinaḥ api amañcat rūpyam buḍyā jñāyate tad amadātmanā eva jāyeta mad ātmanā tu jñāyate atas  na tad asat  khyāti kiṃtu mad eva tanyāmat tvam bāghaka nānam bodhaya tauti ced tamyāmat tvam nāma kim tad eva kim vā tasya eva rūpa antaram uta anyat  vidhā api na tasya kṣatiḥ tathā hi tad eva ceta bādhakam api tad eva mad rūpam dṛḍhaukuryāt  rūpa antara mapi hi tasya tasmin mati eva bhavet  tathā tatas anyat api ekasya he rūpe viruddhe iti ced mā bhūttī sapam apūrva pratipanna sat rūpa virodhāt  sat rūpam ca avirodhena eva pūrva prati panna tvāt  su pratiṣṭhitam atas  na tad na bhavet  yadi na bhaveta asat rūpam api na tasya syāt  na api tad saṃbandhi tad  bodhyeta atas tad asat rūpam tamya bhāve ced na bhaveta   na bhavati eva abhāve tasya abhāvāt  kaḥ ca virodhaḥ pramāṇam cahe rūpe ekasya bodhayati pramāṇam api virudda na bodhaya tauti ced  amattva bodhakam eva tad  na bodhayet  mattva bodhaka tu avirodhena pūrvam eva ābabadhat atasmat tvam eva rūpyasya nāma tvam atas  na tasya rūpa antaram amat tvam bodhyate taba yadi tad eva bodhayet  bādhakaḥ yadi vā tatas anyat ubhayathā api tad  sthitam eva iti uktam nanu tad eva bodhyate kiṃtu tad nā stauti atamtat na asti iti ced nā asti iti api tad svarūpam eva ced  bodhyate tad sthitam eva atha anyaḥ  na asti arthaḥ tathā api sthitam eva anyasmin  api na asti arthe bodhite rūpyam amatsyā diti ced na tāvat tajñānam rūpyam abhāvīkaroti akāra katvāt  jñānasya anyathā atiprasaṅgāt  atas  bodhakam eva jñānam ajñānam tu nivartayet  na ca na atyartha ajñāna rūpyam iṣṭam atas  yadi api na asi artha rūpyam aṃbaddham api bodhayet  tathā api na rūpyam amat syāt  jñānasya jñeyānāśaka tvāt  na atyartha eva rūpya buḍyā gṛhyata iti ced  tad na na asti iti pratauteḥ astauti ca pratīteḥ atas  na asti buddhiḥ na rūpyam spṛśati amadevāstauti bhātauti ced tad na tathā tve pramāṇa bhāvāt  bhāve api tad  sattvam bādhakavat eva na vārayet  kim tad asat  yad sat ātmanā khyāti sat antaram ced  pratyuktam na aham asat sat antaram vacmi kiṃtu tuccham iti ced  tuccha śabdaḥ alyādau prayujyamānaḥ  dṛśyate tad eva kim tuccham uta anyat te matam nissvabhāvam tuccham iti ced  na tādṛś  mamasti kiṃcid  tad api hi na asti jñāna meyam ced  tad eva tasya svarūpam yad na asti jñāna meyam asti jñāna meyā ādi lakṣaṇam meyam ced  tad api atuccham ghaṭa ādivat  te api tucchā iti cetna ukta lakṣaṇa abhāvāt teṣām ghaṭa ādi tulya lakṣaṇam cat tuccham  tad api asi eva teṣām sattvāt  atas asat sadā tmanā khyāti iti uktā ismad eva sat ātmanā khyā ti iti artha ssyāt  atas  na kā cit asat sya atimā̍ntiḥ mata eva sat ātmanā khyātesmad antarātmanā khyāteḥ aniṣṭa tvāt  pratyukta tvāt ca atas  yadi bhrāntiḥ iṣyeta amatsyātiḥ eva mā iṣyatām athavā asat  khyātoti iyam eva bhrānti sva yā eṣṭavyā amataḥ akhyāteḥ khyātau ca uktaḥ  doṣaḥ yad yamat api meyam asyāta amat api mānam kim na syāt  syāt ceta sadā eva āmataḥ khyātissyāt  mā ced hāntim nudeta tasya asmadā bhāvān na kadācid api bhrāntissyāt  asat api ced mānam syāt  matsyātiḥ api mada eva syāt  sadamat khyātyoḥ ca virodhe na ekā api syāt  aviśeṣāt  avirodhe iyam api sadā eva syāt  māna abhāve kim khyāpayet iti ced  meyā abhāve kim khyāti asat api khyāti ced  amat api khyāpayatu nanu amañcet na bhāti katham tad yavahāraḥ tad i avahāraḥ ced asti katham tad na asti tad ced asti katham tatra na astauti buddhiḥ na hi mati ghaṭe sā astauti ced  buddhiḥ ced asti bodhyam na tuccham ghaṭa ādivat iti uktam kaḥ tarhi na asti buddheviṣayaḥ na hi tuccha viṣayam icchasi na ca mad nāsti buddhe viṣayaḥ asti buddi viṣaya tvāt tasya na ca nirviṣayām buddhim icchasi atas  vācyaḥ tad diṣayaḥ ucyate yaḥ  na mannā api tuccham ma tasyāḥ  viṣayaḥ īdṛś arthaḥ aprasiddha  iti ced m ā evam vocaḥ anayā eva buḍyā prasiddha tvāt  na hi asyāḥ matta  chau viṣayau na apauyam nirviṣayā atassa prasiddha eva bhāva antaram bhāva antara dharmaḥ  vā na asti buddeviṣaya iti ced  astu yadi maḥ api atā lakṣaṇaḥ ma yadi pramāṇavān vastu anyathā avasta syāt  maḥ api abhāvaḥ  na rūpya ātmanā khyāti amadrapya miti am at adhiṣṭhāna tayā rūpyasya apratīteḥ idam rūpyam itivat  na apauṭam aṃśaḥ abhāva ātmanā khyāti idam na asti iti apratīteḥ tasmāt ajñānam bhrāntim tad nittim ca icchat hiḥ madatta eva mārga āśrayaṇīyaḥ anyathā tad ami dardarśita tvāt  _ aasti nāsti dhiyoḥ eka meya tve su dṛḍha astidhauḥ tathā eva bhinna meya tve asacātuccham mita tvataḥ na ātma prabham vinā annāna bhrānti bādha ādi sidhyati tad ca anantam atas  bhrāntau śūnya vijñāna vādinau akhyāti akhyātī pṛthak  ced te alya bhāvaḥ api pṛthak yadi khyātiḥ sarvā bhramaḥ  naḥ vā bhrama śāstram tathā tadā yad ukta makhyāti vādinā anirvacanīyasya api sat rūpya rūpeṇa khyāti abhyapagame amatkhya atipramaṅgaḥ anirvacanīyasya sa drapya rūpa abhāvāt iti  tad api parihṛtam rūpyasya tena eva rūpeṇa sattve pramāṇa bhāva pradarśanena kiṃca madrapi ātmanā jyātau matsya atipramaṅgaḥ  vācyaḥ na punar amat khyāti pramaṅgaḥ rūpyasya mattvena anirvācyasya mad rūpam na astauti ced ta deva ced tathā bhāti katham tad tasya rūpam na asti iti jñāyate yasya ca abhāvaḥ  na asti ma katham evam jānīyāt  na aham evam jāne tvad mata meva āśritya vadāmauti ced  mama api na evam matam na anirvacanīyasya etad rpamaḥ tauti abhāva pramāṇa vādī api na evam jānauyāta rūpyasya amat tvam tamyā nirvācya ajānam aṃbandha abhāve vā pramāṇa abhāvāt  na hi tad rapyam yathā bhāti tathā niṣeḍhum śakyam iti uktam na ca anyathā niṣedhaḥ asti iṣyate vā na ca anyathā tasya mattva pramāṇam asti tathā eva ca mad tvam na iṣyate bādhāt  atas  rūpya nirvācyam atas tasya ajñānasya ca svarūpe maṃbandha ca pramāṇa abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ api na pramāṇa gamyaḥ tam māda jāna tad kāyaya abhāva abhāva pramāṇā spṛṣṭa tvāt atat rapa tvāta anjāna kārya majjāyate uta āsata ajñānam api tathā eva bhavat anyathā bhavati uta anyathā bhūtvā anyathā bhavati kim bhavat eva tad na bhavati uta abhṛtvā tad na bhavati tad nittiḥ ca abhāvaḥ  bhāvaḥ vā iti ādayaḥ  bhāva abhāvam asparśinaḥ vikalyā bhāva abhāva vasu iva na ajñāna tad kārye ḍhokante kriyamāṇā api te na tayoḥ pratimā vahanti ākāśasya iva muṣṭi dhātāḥ tasmāt anirvacanīyasya eva kārya kāraṇa bhāva upapannaḥ sarveṣām vastu dharma āśrayāṇām doghāṇām tatra aprāptaḥ avastu tvāt  anirvācyam ced rapyam katham amtauti bhātauti ced  bhrānti tvāt adoṣaḥ anirvacanīyamya ca tad rūpāmattva pramāṇa abhāvāt  nāmat khyāti āśaṅkā iti uktam atas  bhrāntau yāvat kiṃcid bhāti tasya sarvasya bhāve abhāve ca pramāṇā bhāvāt anirvacanīyatā eva iti middham anyeṣām tu jātamya rūpya ādeḥ bādhām bhavasya uktatva ādhānyam iddeḥ bhrāntyā api anyathā khyānam na midhyet  mad pakṣe tu rūpya ādeḥ ajñāna ja tvāt ajñāna mātra śarora tvāt ca tad jñānānām ca tathā tvācchati ādi jānebhyaḥ  stad ajñāna tad kārya nitya papatta īśati ādi jānānām bādha katvam rūpya ādi pratibhāmānām ca bhrānti tvam bādhyatva ātmiham atas  pratyakṣa bādhasya evaṃprakāra tvāt anumāna ādi bādhā ayi evam prakārā eva draṣṭavyāḥ anyathā tepām api uktena nyāyena bādha katva ayogāt tatra liṅga ābhāma ādi atyabhramam mamyagliṅgāyati ena jñānena nivartyaḥ aparokṣa bhramat tu aparokṣa ajñānena eva nivartyaḥ na tu parokṣa jñānena liṅga ādi utthena ata eva anumāna ādinā nirjāta candra ādi tattvānām api vicandra diś bhramāt ayaḥ  na nivartante apara uṣṭa jñānam vinā tena tu nivartante vinā pyanumāna ādibhiḥ anumāna ādayaḥ ca aparokṣe api arthe pravartante atas taiḥ candra ādi tattvam pratipadya vicandra ādeḥ tad pratibhāsasya ca anirvacanīya ajñāna śarīram āvatvam pratipadyate pratyakṣa bādhe tathā vyutpatteḥ na tu abhāvam dicandra ādaunām vetti ukta hetubhyaḥ pratyakṣa bādhe ca anyathā eva vyatpatteḥ tatra hi ayathārtha pratibhāsasya tad arthasya ca artha yāthāni ājñāna ja tvam tajñāna heya tvam ca pratipannam na punar abhāva jñāna heya tvam bhrānti arthasya ata iha api tathā eva yuktam pratipattam candra ādaunām ekatva ādau jñāte na ca ekatva ādi jñānam vinā hicandra ādi jñānānām bhrānti tvam jñātum śakyam na ca dvau candrau na iyam prācau dik  iti etāvat e vā āpta vākyam yadi api bhavet  tathā api pūrva ukta vyutpatti balāt nirvācya tā eva candraditvā ādeḥ pratīyate na tu abhāvaḥ aneha nānā asti iti āgama vākyasya api evam eva arthaḥ  grāhyaḥ tasmā hicandra ādi bhramasya aparokṣa tvāt aparokṣa jñānena eva nivṛttiḥ eva mā ātmanaḥ abrahmatva bhramasya aparokṣa tvāt aparokṣa jñānam eva śrautam tad nivartayati śābdam api jñānam aparokṣa artham bhavati aparī dhātma viṣaya tvāt yathā aātmanam svayaṃprakāśa tā vyutpādaka pauruṣeyam vākyam prāk api aparokṣa jñānāt ekātmya paratve śrute niścite bheda darśanasya pratyakṣa abhimatasya api bhrānti tvam jñātum śakyam  ~ yathā anumāna ādibhiḥ candraka tve niścite candrabheda darśanasya pratyakṣa abhimatasya api bhrānti tvam jñāyate prāgaṇya parona bodhāt  na ca pratyakṣa virodha āśaṅkā avā api evam draṣṭavyam aneha nānā asti aindraḥ  māyābhiḥ amṛtyoḥ sa mṛtyam ityādi vākyaḥ anirvacana auyatva vyāpta rādi antavat tvā dibhiḥ hetubhiḥ ca jagataḥ  māyā maya tvam avagamyata iti uktam atas asmati akṣe ajñāna ja tvāt  bhramasya jñāna anivṛttiḥ yutā anye tu ajñāna jam bhramam na icchanti atas teṣām bhrānti bādhau na maṃstaḥ iṣṭaḥ api ajñāna jaḥ  bhramaḥ asat khyāti vādinaḥ  na siyet  amati ajñāna abhāvāt jñāna abhāvāt ca na bādhaḥ tathā ātma khyāti vādinaḥ api na hi buddhiḥ tayā anya yā api buḍyā jñāyata iti uktam ajñānam ca nirastam itarayaḥ  rapi vādinoḥ ajñāna jam bhramam icchataḥḥ sva pakṣa hāniḥ iti eṣaḥ arthaḥ amattvena bhrānti bādhau stām iti ādeḥ ślokasya ayam ca śloke  uttara granthasya sūtra bhūta  iti vakṣyamāṇaḥ api arthaḥ kaścid saṃ pataḥ  darśitaḥ atra atas  na anena paunarutyam uttara granyasya codanīyam vivaraṇamya tu paunarutyam na doṣāya asya tad artha kathana paratvāt naṣā akṣara yojanā yathā bhāti tathā rūpyasya sattva mati arūpyasya iva na bādhaḥ atas  na bhrāntim iddhiḥ tathā amattve na khyātiḥ ukta hetubhyaḥ tatas  na bādhassyāt  na sarva rūpam asat  kiṃcittvasya rūpam amat iti ced  yad rūpam amat tad na khyāti   atas  na bhramaḥ atha uccata nāmat ta  cham vadāmaḥ kiṃtu mad antaram taharmaḥ  mam vā abhāva pramāṇa pra meyam atas takhyāti iti tathā api na asti iti eva khyātena bhrānti khyātiḥ tad asat sat rūpeṇa bhātauti ced  tasya tad sat rūpam asti vā na vā asti ced  abādhāt na bhramaḥ na asti ced  na astikhyātiḥ asyāt na vā na tu bhramaḥ asataḥ tad sat rūpam na asti tathā api astauti bhāti iti ced  kim tad sadrapam svarūpe ṇā api na asti uta tasya amatā maṃbandha gva na asti ubhayathā api uktam eva uttaram draṣṭavyam atas amat tve na matsyāti riti bhramaḥ  na syāt  yadi nāma sat khyā ati ssyāt asati api tathā api na bādhassyāt  pūrva uktena nyāyena iti anāsattve khyāti bādhakau iti uktam athavā ādyaḥ pādaḥ satyakṣadṛṣakaḥ yathā bhāti tathā sattve rūpyasya na bhrāntissyāt  syāñcata kiṃcid rūpam amat iti tathā api na mattvena khyātasya bādha iti dvitīyaḥ pādaḥ asati akṣadṛṣakaḥ  amataḥ khyātyam abhavān na bhramamsyāt  rūpyasya atucchatva āśramamsyāt iti ceta tathā api tucchasya ākhyātena tad dodhamta dādhakam syāt  atas tuccham ka pyā tmanā khyātam iti na jānam syāt iti athavā amattvāt na khyātiḥ atas  na bādhaḥ ca iti arthaḥ athavā   dau  api pāṭau  mati akṣadapakaḥ  tad katham yad rayam bhāti tad kim tuccham bhāti uta mad rūpam tuccham ced  na bhrānti khyāti bādhakaḥ  sat rūpam ced  tad rūpam tucchasya asti uta na mattve na bhrānti bādhau mtām mad pakṣavat eva amattve api na tad ātmanā tucchamya khyātiḥ na api bādhakaḥ madrapya rūpam tucchasya na asti tathā api tad tad ātmakam bhātauti ced   mā kim tad ātma tā tucchamya tuccheva uta matau yadi satau mā kim tucchamya asti uta na vidhā api pūrvavat attaram yojyam tasya mā na asti tathā api tad saṃbandhaḥ  bhātauti ced m aṃbandhaḥ api vidhā vikalpyaḥ pūrvavat uttaram ca yojyam rūpyam api amat mad rūpam bhātauti ced  tatra api eṣa gva nyāyaḥ mati aṣṭaḥ api bādhyaḥ  yaḥ aśasmaḥ api mattvena ced bhāti  itara aṃśavat abādhyaḥ san  ca anyathā itarasya api bādhya tvāt amat tu pramaṅgāt  na ca tayoḥ bādha ātmā ac bheda ssiddhaḥ tatas  dayaḥ dhas abādhaḥ vā syāt  jñāte api bhede sattvena ced dayam bhāti bādhaḥ abādhaḥ vā iyaḥ stulya ssyāt  śukti rūpyayoḥ bheda jñānāt  tad abhedaḥ  bādhya iti ced jñāte api bhede tayoḥ abhedasmad tvena bhāti ced  na tasya api tayoḥ iva bādhaḥ  yuktaḥ anyathā tayoḥ api bādhaḥ  viśeṣāt syāt  bheda jñāne ced abhedaḥ  na syāt  maḥ ajñānam eva syāt  anyathā tasya api tayoḥ iva jānāt anivṛttaḥ bādhya aṃśasya api ca ījñānam amti itara aṃśa jñānavat mad artham anyathā tad api amadartha syāt  aviśeṣāt  sarva jñānānām ca jñeya śūnya tve na bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ jñeyavat tvam ca tathā amattvena ced bhāti bādhya aṃśaḥ tasya vā jñānam na asti tadā jeya śūnyam ~  tadā bhrāntiḥ kā kaḥ  vā bādhaḥ tasya jñānam jaya śūnyam ca iti vipratiṣiddham akhyāti paṣṭaḥ api yathājñānam na iyamat tvam na bhrānti bādhau tām amattve natarām yathā jñānam na iyamattve api avivekaḥ  bhrama iti ced  avivekaḥ api jānam jñeyaḥ  vā jñānam ced  tad yathārtham eva iti na bhramaḥ jeyaḥ api jñātaḥ ajñātaḥ  vā ubhayathā api na ma bhramaḥ jeyā antaravat jñāna jñeyābhyām anyaḥ ced maḥ api na anirvācyaḥ aniṣṭa tvāt  atam svayaṃprabha ātmā phalam vā syāt  ubhayapi na bhramaḥ tasmātyakṣa antareṣu bhrānti bādhayoḥ ama bhavāt tayoḥ ca prasiddha tvāt  mada mat tvābhyām anirvacanīyā vidyā eva idam rajatam ityādi bhrānti jñānam tajñeyam ca iti middham eṣā akṣara yojana ādi k athavā mattve rūpyāt enam bhrānti bādhau tad aṃśasya sarvasya vā amattve khyāti abhāvāt na bhrānti bādhau atas anirvācya avidyā eva bhramāḥ tad arthāḥ cetye tāvān eva asya ślokasya arthaḥ anyaḥ tu asya eva samarthana artham uttara grantha artha  eva atra uktaḥ pratipatti saukarya artham yāvat tu bādhyate tāvat hāntam sarvam na bādhyate sa adhiṣṭhānaḥ  bhramaḥ tasmāt yuktaḥ  bādhaḥ  hi sa avadhiḥ nanu yadi avidyai vedam rajatam iti jñānam jñeyam ca tadā sarvasya eva jñānāt dādhassyāt na vā kasya api aṃśasya aviśeṣāt  nanu bhrānteḥ tajñeyasya ca avidyā tvam uktam satyam eka ha audam bhrānti jñānam idam rajatam iti na de atasmarvasya eva bādhaḥ abādhaḥ vā syāt  na ca sarvasya bādha iṣṭaḥ na api yuktimān na hi niravadhikaḥ  bādhaḥ  niradhiṣṭhānaḥ ca bhrama saṃbhavati na hi bhinna viṣaya yoni yaḥ rūpa rasa jñānayoḥ iva bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ  yuktimān atas  yasmin  arthe bhramaḥ tatra eva bādhaḥ api nyāyya iti na marva bādhaḥ yuktimān atha idam rajatam iti sat asat aṃśa arthe he jñāne mamyak bhānti rūpe iṣyete tadā api na bhrānteḥ ta hiṣayasya ca marva ātmanā bādhaḥ uktena nyāyena atha ekam eva jñānam bhrānta āmra anta rūpam tadā api mad ātmanā khyāteḥ aviśeṣāt  sarvasya eva bādhaḥ abādhaḥ vā pakṣa antaravat tvat pakṣe api syāt iti ced tad na viśeṣa bhāvāt  na tāvat idam rajatam iti asya sarvasya jñānasya jñeyasya ca avidyā tvam uktam api tu tayoḥ bhrānta aṃśasya eva vedyaiḥ saha bhramā avidyā iti yuktam na ca sarvasya bhrānti tvam yāvat hi bādhyate tāvat eva bhrāntam na ca sarva bādhyata uktana nyāyena na ca na kiṃcid api bādhyate bhrānti bādha prasiṭvi virodhāt  na ca pakṣa antaravat mati akṣe api sarvasya bādhaḥ abādhī vā iti ayam doṣa āśaṅkitum api śakyate na hi jñāna prāptam rūpya ādi jñāna antaram niṣedhati prakāra antareṇa vā jñāna prāptam jñāna antaram bādhate iti mad pakṣaḥ kiṃtu ajñātam artha bodhayat  jñānam tad ajñānam nivartayati tani vṛttau ca tad jam rūpya ādi nivartate tantu nivṛttau  iva paṭa iti atas  na mati akṣa jñāna prāptam jñāna antareṇa bādhyate yasya tu tathā tasya eva virodhāt abādhaḥ marvasya vā aviśeṣāt  bādhaḥ prasajyate katham ca mad pakṣe marva bādhā śaṅkā artha hi ajñātam bādhayat  jñāna tad ajñāna tad kārye eva bādhata mama atā matya bodhyata eva arthaḥ  jñānena na bādhyate hi aṇamācaḥ  api yasya tu arthaḥ  bādhyaḥ tasya eva marva artha bādha prasaṅgaḥ arthatva jñātatva aviśeṣāt  ajñānasya tu sa avaśeṣamya api yathā bādhassaṃbhavati tathā darśitaḥ tasmāt śukti ādi artha eva tada jñāna tajja rūpya ādi bhramasya adhiṣṭhānam tad ādhe ca avadhiḥ iti mad pakṣa eva bādhyasya avadheḥ adhiṣṭhānasya ca saṃbhava atyakṣa antare cām bhavān mad pakṣa eva mā adhiṣṭhānaḥ  bhramamau  adhikaḥ ca bādhaḥ  yujyate na tu pakṣa antaredhiti abhiprāyaḥ rūpya abhāve kutas tad haudhauma atra syāt tu śuktivat  nanu evam na asti tad jñaḥ api bāḍham jastu asti śukti dṛś  bhrānti kāle akhyātasya avadhitva ayogāt avadhya bhāve ca bādhā saṃbhavāt  bhrāntau bhātam na sarva bādhyam yāvat dādhyam tāvat eva bhrānta tvāt avidyā ātmakam na anyat abādhyam tad tu vastu i tyuktam tatra idam ca udyatena idam rūpyam iti bādha prasiddheḥ rūpyam eva bādhyam na tu tajñānam api rūpya abhāve ta jjñānam api na asti iti ceta tad jñātā tad phalam ca na syāt    jñātra bhāve bādhaka jñānam api nirāśrayam na syāt  atas  na kiṃcid ādhyam syāt  syāt ced  marvam eva bādhyam iti śūnya vāda prasaṅgaḥ ma ca aniṣṭaḥ atas  jñāna ādi asti jñāna bhāve ca jñāna prāptam eva pakṣa antar avahādhyam iti pakṣa antaram eva āśrayaṇīya miti avocyate   rūpyata jñāna ādyamat tve api śukta odam aṃśa tajñāna tajñābādimattvāt bādhaka jñāna saṃbhavāt rūpya ādi  mātra bādha upapatte kta doṣa pramaṅgaḥ rūpya jñānam cadasti rūpyam api atyeva iti na tasya bādhaḥ mati arūpyasya iva anyathā tamyā api bādhassyāt  atas  yathā rūpyam na asti tathā tad jñānam api na asti eva iti na anyathā ākhyātim midhyet  tathā ātma khyātiḥ api bāhya rūpya abhāve tad ākāra jñāna abhāvāt amatsyātiḥ tu dṛra utsāritā akhyāti pakṣetva satya artha khyāti abhāvāt  bhrama abhāva eva doṣaḥ tasmāt rapya ādi bhāve tauḥ api na asti eva yāvaha ādhyam tāvat avidyā na ca ma bādhyam iti atam iyahādhyam iyan  bādhyam iti tu na uktam atas tad āha yāvaha ādhe api bhāti eva tāvat eva na bādhyate tāvat ca asya iva taca eva bādhitam tu na kutracid  yāvat dhāntau bhātam bādhake śakti jñāne api bhāti eva na na bhāti  tāvat eva na bādhyate yad anyat na bhāti tad sarva bādhyata eva yāvat na bādhyate tāvacā asti eva nāsadabādhyam na api vartamānam tatra eva ca asti deśe na deśa antare bādhitam tu na kuvacid deśe kāle buddhau vā asti ata idam aṃśa eva bādhe api khyāti iti abādhyaḥ na anyat  yahādhe api khyāti tad eva abādhyam iti kuta iti ced tasya eva avadhitva saṃbhavāta avadheḥ eva ca abādhya tvāt  bādhyasya avadhitva ayogāt nirava dhika bādhā saṃbhavāt ca na ca deśa antara ādi gatam rūpyam bādhaka jñāne khyāti na ca tad abhra antau khyāti doṣa hetutva ākhyāteḥ na ca kṣaṇika buddhi ākāraḥ  rūpyam kṣaṇa antare buḍi antare vā khyāti na ca smṛtam parokṣam rūpyam bādhaka jñāne grahaṇe tatrasthasya eva bhāti na ca smṛti jñānam bādhakam na ca asat  bādhe bhāti atasman  eva idam aṃśaḥ bādhe api bhāti iti abādhyaḥ rūpyam tu bādhyam eva abādhitam tu na kutracit iti etad  kuta iti āha na anyatra bhāti rūpyam tad iha bādhāt tu kalpyate iha asat bhāti ced rūpyam khyātiḥ sattām na kalpayet  na tāvat rūpyam anya cā asti iha bādhitam iti bhāti atas  na tad  pratītitaḥ anyatra asti iha bādhāt tu tad anya vāstauti kalpyate asat khyāti asaṃbhava yuktyā na ca sā kalpanā alabhyā iha āsata iha khyāteḥ khyātiḥ sattām na kalpayet yatas  yaḥ tu brūyāt anyacā eva tad rūpyam bhāti na iha iti tasya pratīti virodha ssyāt  yatas  na anyatra bhāti rūpyam iha eva tu bhāti iha bādhāt eva ca tad anyatra bhātauti kalpyate na tu sva anubhavata eva tad siddham yadi siddham na bhrānti bādhau syātām vādinām ca vipratipattiḥ na syāt  avya tpanna vyutpādana arthā smṛti pramoṣa ādi prakriyā ca bhavadīyā vyarthā syāt  tad dodhya abhāvāt ata iha eva bhāti rūpyam iha asat api iha astauti bhātauti ced rūpyam na tasya khyātim mat tām kalpayeta asattve apoha khyāteḥ atas  na asya anyatra bhānam kalpyam tatra sattve pramāṇa abhāvāt  rūpyasya mattām ced kalpayet  khyātiḥ asat khyāteḥ ayogataḥ yatra yad bhāti taca eva tasya tām kim na kalpayet  spaṣṭa arthaḥ ślokaḥ tatra bādhān na kalpyā ced na anyatra syāti abhāvataḥ khyātim vinā api ced sattā kalpyate niyamaḥ kutas  yatra rūpyam bhāti tatra tasya sattā na kalpayitum śakyā bādhāt  tatra abhāva khyāteḥ iti ced ta dayuktam yadi api abhāvaḥ khyāti tathā api bhāva khyāteḥ bhāvaḥ api aṣṭavyaḥ anyathā mā artha śūnyā eva syāt  na hi mā anyatra matā rūpyeṇa arūpyeṇa vā tatrasthena mā arthā syāt  atad khyāti tvāt  kiṃtu tatrasthena eva rūpyeṇa yadi anya cā api satā rūpyeṇa mā arthā syāt  arūpyeṇa kim na syāt  syāveta na rūpya khyātirasyāt  rūpyasya anyatra sattā kalpanam ca vyartham tasmāt  rūpya khyātiḥ ced  sārthā iṣyate yathā tad rūpyam khyāti tathā eva tad asti iti abhyupeyam yadi abhāvaḥ api khyāti saḥ api astu na ca virodhaḥ khyātī ced abhayam darśayataḥ kaḥ  virodhaḥ virodhe api bhāva khyāti virodhāt abhāva khyāteḥ eva aprāmāṇyam anya viṣaya tvam vā syāt  prāpta anupalabdhauvabhāva khyāteḥ iṣṭa tvāt atas  na tad virodhā dbhāva khyātiḥ apramāṇam anya viṣayā vā bhavet  balauyaḥ tvā       davi rodhena eva ca utpanna tvāt pratyakṣasya ca pramāṇa jyeṣṭha tvāta na ca rūpya khyātesmārtha tve aparokṣa artha tve ca sidde apratyakṣatā sidhyet  atas  rūpya khyātesmārtha tve yatra rūpyam bhāti taca eva tasya mattā kalpyā tatra bādhān na kalyyā ced natarām anyatra kalpyā khyāti abhāvāt  khyātim vinā api ced sattā kalpyate rūpyasya eva mā akhyātasya kalpyā na śaśa viṣāṇa ādeḥ iti niyamaḥ kaḥ tasmāt akhyātasya api ced  rūpyasya anyatra mattā kalpyate śaśa viṣāṇasya api kalpyatām na ced tasya na itarasya api ubhayoḥ api tatra ākhyātatva aviśeṣāt rūpyam kvacid bhāti itarat na kvāpauti ced  tarhi gavi viṣāṇam bhāti atas tad śaśa ādiṣu api kalpyatām gavi viṣāṇasya bādhya tvāt na anyatra sattā kalpyā rūpyasya tu iha bādhita tvā danī atra mattā kalpyā kvacid sata eva kvacid niṣedha dṛṣṭeḥ iti ced kim yatra asti taca eva niṣedhaḥ uta anyatra ādye kalpa gavi api viṣāṇasya niṣedhāt anyatra tasya mattā kalpyā dvitīye tu asya rūpyasya anyatra matta asiddheḥ iha eva ca sattva khyāte riha niṣedhām abhavāt  anyatra eva niṣedhāt iha eva mattā kalpyā na tu anyatra anyatra madeva iha niṣidhyata iti ced  asyāḥ  niṣedhāt na anyatra mattā kalpyā anyatra sa deva idam rūpyam iti ced  tarhi idānaum iha āgata tvāt anyatra eva niṣedhyam anyatra eva mad iha astauti bhāti na vihāgatam iti ced kutaḥ ajñāya odam na tāvat rapya khyāteḥ eva evam idam rūpyam iti eva khyāteḥ bādhasāmarthyāt ajñāyauti ced bādhaḥ api aca eva ced  sat  niṣedhati anyaca eva niṣedhet  anyatra sa ced na asyaḥ     niṣedhaḥ anyasya eva tu ubhayatra sat ced  tathā api tatas anyatra eva niṣedhaḥ na tu tatra eva yatra sat tatra eva ced niṣedhaḥ gavi api tad viṣāṇasya niṣedhaḥ prasajyata iti uktam atas  na khyāti vinā sattā kalyā śaśaviṣāṇa ādeḥ api tad prasaṅgāt  bādhaḥ api kalpayet tatra na ṛte prāptim asau bhavet  bādhaḥ ata eva na anyatra na tu bādhyasya sat tayā nanu yadi api rūpyasya anyatra khyāti abhāvāt na khyāti smattām kalpayet  tathā api iha bādhaḥ  rūpyasya anyatra sattām kalpayati sa hi tām na anyatra niṣedhati kiṃtu iha eva yadi mā anyatra api na asti iha iva anyatra api tām niṣedhet  na tu niṣedhati iha iva atas anyatra tām bādhaḥ kalpayati ta kalpanā hetuḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ tasmāt iha bādhitam rūpyam anyavā sti abādhāt iti ced na etad sārama yava astauti bhāti tatra tasya niṣedhasya aniṣṭa tvāt anya ca eva niṣedhya tvāt anya ca eva bādha iti ukta tvāt  yadi api yatra bhāti tava eva niṣedhaḥ tathā pi bādhaḥ api khyātiḥ iva tatra eva sattām rūpyasya kalpayet na anyatra na hi prāptim vinā bādhaḥ  bhavet  na ca anyatra prāptiḥ asti rūpyasya akhyāteḥ tava atas  yatra bhāti tatra eva prāptam sat  rūpyam niṣedhan  taca eva tasya sattām kalpayet  bādhaḥ asataḥ prāpti niṣedha ayogāt kvacid sata eva tu tad yogāt anyatra ca sattvena prāpti abhāvāt yatas ca prāpti mṛte na bādhaḥ  bhavet na ca anyatra prāptiḥ ata eva bādhaḥ  na anyatra bhavati na tu bādhyasya rūpyasya tatra sattvena tatra bādhā bhāvaḥ anyatra sat eva rūpyam idam rūpyam iti iha śuktau bhāti atas  na idam rūpyam iti iha tasya bādhāt anyatra sattvam siyati asataḥ khyāti ayogāt iti vadatām yathā anyatra sattvam iha ca asattvam na rūpyasya sidhyati tathā upapādya khyāteḥ bādhāt ca anirvacanauya tvam pūrva uktam eva upasaṃharati sacced bhāti katham bādhaḥ  bhāti ced tad asat katham madam ajhyām atas avācyam śuktau rūpyam iti sthitam na eva kalpyā anyathāmattā yathā bhāti tathā asti ced  naḥ ced na kalpanā bījam na hi asat khyāti asaṃbhavaḥ api ca idam bhavantassarve vādinaḥ praṣṭavyāḥ  kim yasmā dvijñāna ādyaḥ arthaḥ  bhāti asti na asti iti avā sa tathā eva sādhuḥ iti abhyupeyaḥ uta anyathā api syāt iti tatra ādye kalpa idam rūpyam na idam rūpyam iti jñānayoḥ tathā artha tvādrpya mapi anyathā asat ittham bhātauti anyathāsattā rūpyasya na kalpanauyā na api asattā asat eva bhātauti dvitīye tu na tad kalpanā baujam asti rūpya khyāteḥ ayathārthatva saṃbhavāt bādhakasya api atas anyathā sadityam bhāti rūpyam asat dā bhātauti mahā ādi nām sat dādinām ceṣṭam na sidhyet  yathārthatva niyama abhāve ca artha paricchedaka tvam jñānānām svabhāvaḥ  na syāt  asvabhāva tve ca tad na anyena kartum śakyate atas  na ayathārtha jñānam kiṃcid abhyupeyam yathārtham ca jñānam na bādhyam yathārthatva niyama abhāve api na bādhya bādhaka niścaya ssyāt  na ca | bhinna arthayoḥ abhinna arthayoḥ ca jñānayoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ  rūpa rasa jñāna yaḥ rūpa jñāna yaḥ riva ca iti uktam tasma ajñānānā mabādhya tvāt ajñānam eva bādhyam iti anye pakṣā niyuktikā iti siddham tathā bhāne anyathāsattvam upa yogi katham tava rūpyasya avidyayā bhāne ajñāta matta upayoginau yadi apaudam rūpyam iti khyātiḥ ātmanasmārtha tvāya anyathā mad tvam rūpyasya na kalpayati arūpyeṇa iva anyathāmatā rūpyeṇa api tasya āmma arthatva ayogāt  tathā api ātma lābhāya kalpayati iti ced  tathā ābhāne rūpyasya anyathā   ajñāya mānena rūpeṇa  mattvam upayogi hetumsyāt  katham tava avidyā nimitte tu bhāne ajñāta mattā upayoginau syāt  na ca tathā icchasi atas  rūpyasya api ajñāta rūpeṇa mad tvam ghaṭa ādeḥ iva mad tvam tathā ābhāne hetuḥ na syāt  atad diṣayatvā viśeṣāt  syāñcet  ghaṭa ādimattvam api syāt  nanu ghaṭa ādi na bhāti rūpya khyātau matyam rūpyam api bhāsamānāt rūpā drupa antareṇa na bhāti eva tasyām nanu rūpya jāteḥ bhānā na atyantam abhānam anyathāsataḥ api rūpyasya iti ced tad na na hi jātiḥ api bhāti vyaktara bhāvāt  na iha vyaktisti asti ced  tad khyātiḥ satya arthā syāt  na ca anyā vyaktayaḥ bhānti atas anyathā asat rūpyam na bhātauha katham ca tad asyāḥ syāteḥ ātma lābha hetuḥ na tāvat tad  tad avidyāvat asyā upādānam na api cakṣuḥ ādivat hetuḥ na api viṣayaḥ tad viṣayatva ākhyāteḥ yadi api na paripūrṇaḥ  viṣayaḥ asyāḥ khyāte rūpyam tathā api viṣayaḥ  bhavati eva idam aṃśaḥ aparipūrṇaḥ  viṣayaḥ asyām khyātau  upayogauṣyate evam rūpyam apauṣya tām tasya api idam aṃśavat asyām khyātau sphuraṇāt iti cetna vaiṣamyāt  śuktyajñāna ja tvā drūpya bhramasya tad sattā upayoginau rūpya ajñāna jaḥ tu bhramaḥ  na iṣyate tvayā mayā api atas asya mad tvam na upayogi asyām syātau ama tā apya ātmanā bhāti mad eva atas anyathā sthitā tathā ābhānasya hetuḥ ced kim rūpyeṇa asti śuktikā amatā api rūpeṇa mad eva bhātauti rūpyasya api sattva miṣyata iti ced kim rūpyeṇa kalpitena asti śukti rubha yava ādim apratipannā sā eva amatā rūpya ātmanā bhāsyati na cāmadātmanā vinā avidyām sadbhāta auti uktam ekena miḍa yomā̍nti bādhayoḥ kalpanā dvayoḥ na yuktā śuktivat rūpyam sat ced ādhe na bhāti kim nanu śuktivat rūpyam api mad  kasmāt na iṣyate iyoḥ api bhrānti bādhau dṛṣṭau dvayoḥ ca mattve māmānādhikaraṇya mātra mamat kalpayitum śakyam anyathā rūpyam api amatkalpanīyam syāt iti ced  na na hi rūpyasya asat tvam kalpanauyam bādhāt eva tasiddheḥ sattvam eva tu tasya kalpanauyam taca na śakyam kalpayitum ekena eva satā saṃpratipannena bhrānti bādhayossiddhayoḥ dvitīyasya kalpakā bhāvāt yadi śukti vadrūṣyam api sat syāt  śuktivat eva rūpyam api bādhaka jñāne na tu dṛśyate atas  na sat  rūpyam yatra yubha yoḥ bhamaḥ tatra ubhayam bādhaka jñāne dṛśyate na ca atra dṛśyate atas  na ubhayoḥ atra bhramaḥ tasmāt śuktiḥ eva sva ajñāna ja rūpya rūpā bhātauti miḍḍam śukti rūpyayoḥ viviktayoḥ bādhaka jñāne iyoḥ apratīteḥ tayoḥ avivekaḥ  bhrama iti etad api pratyuktam tasmāt rapyasya khyāteḥ bādhāt ca yad sanna bhavati tad api syātauti siddham atas sat eva khyāti na asat iti ayuktam uktam kiṃca nāma khyātauti vāṇauyam na ajñāte asati yujyate idam augiti yukti tayoḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ asat śabdena atra anirvacana auyam vivakṣitam tasya prakṛta tvāt  tad eva sanna bhavati iti etāvatā asat iti upacaryate na punar asadeva anirvacanīya tvāt  abhāvaḥ  vā amad śabda na atra ucyate yaḥ  nāsti buḍvyivahāra viṣaya iṣyate ubhaya sa akṣara yojanā uttareṣu keṣucid lokeṣu draṣṭavyā ye anirvaca nauyam asat ca na icchanti yepi anirvacanīyam eva teṣām sarveṣām dūṣaṇam ucyate asat samarthanam ca sat eva khyāti na anyat iti niyama abhāva pradarśana artham asaca nirūpyamāṇam anirvacanīya mā iva bhaviṣyati iti tad samarthana artham eva vā asanna khyāti iti iyam vāṇī asati ajñāte akhyātau ca na yuktā jñāta eva tu yuktā yathā paṭaḥ śukla iti ādhuktiḥ dharmiṇi dharme ca jñāta eva atas asanna khyāti iti uktiḥ pramāṇataḥ  na khyāti sa drapeṇa vā na khyātauti sa viśeṣaṇā eva nyāyyā anyathā abuddhi pūrvā eva syāt  ātmā aprameya iti vacanam na virudhyate svayam jyotiṣṭvāt  tasya śruti ukta tvāca iti āha ātmani ameya tokti ssyāt svayaṃjyotiṣi api śruteḥ nāma daurakta daudṛś  ced ātmā syāt na anya daudṛśam asataḥ asvayaṃjya utiṣṭvāta svayaṃjyotiṣṭve ca ātmatva prasaṅgāt  ātmanaḥ asataḥ ca vaiṣamyānna ātmani ukta doṣa prasaṅga iti arthaḥ sataḥ artha ādi vekena amataḥ ajñāne tasya āsa tvām iddheḥ asanna bhātauti vacanam mātā me vanyā iti vahi ruddha artha syāt  na ced sa viśeṣaṇam iti amum artham āha sataḥ asanna vivekena jñāyate cedamat katham tasmāt asanna bhātauti mātā vandhyā itivat vacaḥ asat rūpam asat bhāti na sadra peṇa bhāti ced  nāma khyāti niṣid vaivam niṣiddhā tu anyathāmatiḥ yadi sa viśeṣaṇa mucyeta asat  sva rūpeṇa bhāti na tu sat rūpeṇa iti tadā api asat khyāteḥ na niṣedhassyāt  kiṃtu anyathā khyāteḥ sa ca tad vādinaḥ aniṣṭaḥ __ma yadi brūyāt na anyathā khyāti mātra niṣidham kim tu anyathā khyāti mad  na tvad iti tatra hetuḥ vācyaḥ na ātmā asataḥ anyaḥ san sataḥ api na ātmā asan nā sat dausmadyauḥ saddhauḥ api na asat yauḥ atas  na asat sat rūpeṇa khyātauti ced  tathā sataḥ api na anya ssan  ātmā sat asataḥ  stādātmyam tvayā eva nirastam atasman  api sat antara rūpeṇa khyāti iti tulyasmad asatoḥ anyathā ākhyāti asaṃbhavaḥ tvad uktena nyāyena katham ca satasmad ātmanā khyātiḥ anyathā ākhyātiḥ asyāt  mad antarātmanā khyātiḥ anyathā ākhyāti ssyāt iti ced na syāt sadantaram api sat eva ced  marvāmām satsyātaunām anyathā khyātitva prasaṅgāt  atha amad sat antaram na tad sat ucyate ata ekam eva satsyāta dvitīyavat tve dayoḥ sat antara tvāt amattva pramaṅgāt  amacet sat acyeta mahā amat  mad amat śabdayoḥ paryāya tvam amañcet sat antaram mad antarasya mad antarātmanā khyātiḥ anyathā khyātiḥ iti vadatā asata eva anyathā khyātiḥ mā ca asat ātmanā iti uktam syāt  katham cāmataḥ amadātmanā khyātiḥ anyathā khyātimsyāt atipramaṅgāt  amad antara ātmanā khyātiḥ anyathā ākhyātimsyāt iti ced sat antaram api amadeva ced  na anyathā ākhyātismidhyeta   saceta amatam mada ātmanā khyātiḥ anyathā khyātiḥ iti uttā syāt  tasmāt na matassat ātmanā khyātiḥ anyathā khyātiḥ na apyam atas asat ātmanā sadamataḥ  ranyonya ātmanā khyātiḥ anyathā khyātiḥ ced  amataḥ api anyathā khyātiḥ iṣṭā syāt  asat api mad eva ced nāni atha ākhyāti smidhyet  uktena nyāyena amat  mad rūpeṇa bhāti na ani rvacanīyam iti ced  tad ayuktam anirvacanīyasya api rūpyā dessat rūpeṇa khyāteḥ darśita tvāt  tad ca amat kim sat eva uta tuccham na ubhayam iti ced  prāptā anirvacanīya tā asya pramāṇavat tvāt  na hi prāptā iti ced  yathā na asya pramāṇavat tvam tathā darśayiṣyāmaḥ apramāṇavat tve api asya śukti rūpya ādivat pratibhāmaḥ  niyata vyavahāra hetu tvam ca sata iva astauti na tad khyāteḥ apahnavaḥ  yuktaḥ tad apahnavasya api tad abhāve amabhavāt  tasmāt anirvacanīyasya eva ajñānasya anya tha anyathā spharaṇam na vastunaḥ kathaṃcid api ajñānam vinā iti siddham tad etad āha anyathā khyāti sat nāmat iti ce turucyatām na ātma asataḥ anyaḥ tad dhaurvā sat khyātiḥ ced tathā mataḥ amat akṣaram aṃyogi katham bhāti akṣa ja bhrame madapyauriyāt yogam katham deśa antara ādi gam amataḥ akṣāmaṃyoginaḥ akṣaja bhrame bhānā yogāt mad eva deśa antara ādi gam rūghya ādi bhātauti ced  mataḥ api deśā ntara ādi gasya akṣām aṃyogitva aviśeṣāt akṣaja bhrame bhānā yogammamāna iti abhiprāyaḥ doṣāt iyāt kha yogam madyat yamat ca evam iṣyatām rūpyam bhāti yathā bhrāntau tathā asti na ca kasyacid  deśa antara ādigam api mad  doṣāt indriya yogam iyāt iti ced evam avidyā doṣaḥ api indriya yogī iva kuryāt  rūpya ādi asat  anindriya yogya pauti iṣyatām yadi api deśā ntara stham rūpyam akṣṇā yojayet dopaḥ tathā api na kāla antara stham asattvāt tadā na hi doṣa sahasam api tadā amat  rūpyam cakṣuṣā yojayet  tasya vartamāna yogi tvāt  dopaḥ api cakṣuṣa ssahakārī ā iva syāt  na cakṣarantaram mṛjet  tad eva vā anyatra nayet  nayet ced  tabasthā śuktiḥ na dṛśyeta saṃtatam ced cakṣuḥ madhyasthā api ca padārthā dṛśyeran na ca tathā dṛśyante atas  na deśa antara stham api vyavadhānāt ca samīpa stham api vyavahitam na dṛśyate kim punar dūra stham katham ca uddhṛta cakṣuṣassvapne sphurat rūpyādi cakṣuḥ yogi syāt  tasyāḥ  nakṣaja tvāt adoṣa  iti ced jāgarite api bhrānti aṃśasya anakṣaja tvam samānam anyathā idam aṃśat nānavat  rūpya jñāna sya api asatyatva pramaṅgāt  idam ātmanā ca bhrāntau rūpyam bhāti tathā tad tava api na asti atas akṣa jabhrame api mad eva bhātauti niyantum na śakyam atas  na tasya akṣaja tvam api asahiṣayatvāt  atas anirvācyam eva rūpya ādi bhātauti middham atas asat anirvacanīyam vā na khyāti iti vacana mayuktam eva sat antaram asat yeṣām te asat khyātim upāgaman tuccham niṣidhyate taiḥ ced tad śamuktvā niṣidhyatām mad antaram amat iti yeṣām matam teṣām atitarāma yuktam asanna khyātauti vacanam asat khyāteḥ svayam iṣṭa tvāt anirvaca nauyam na khyātauti te vadantauti ced tad ca ayuktam tad khyāteḥ api darśita tvāt  amataḥ api anirvacana auya tvāt tuccham na bhātauti api teṣām ayuktam asanna khyātautivat  nanu abhāṇi tvayā apaudam na asat khyātauti tad katham avidyā siddham āśritya yuktyā siddhi niṣidhyate nanu uktam tuccham na khyātauti tvayā api taba yaḥ tvad ukta doṣa parihāraḥ tava sa eva asmākam asat anirvacanīyam tuccham vā na khyātauti vadatām sarveṣām eva parihāraḥ  bhaviṣyati aatas tam brahauti ced  bravīmi śṛṇu tam tuccham khyāti iti tuccha vādinaḥ avidyā uttham bhramam tad dacanāt uddhā tuccham khyāti iti tad uktam eva anūdya tantra yujyata iti yuktyā tuccha khyāti bhramaḥ  mayā nirasyate na punar tuccham khyāti na khyāti iti vā ucyate na cedṛś bhramaḥ  bhavadbhiḥ tri bhiḥ apyāśrayitum śakyaḥ śakyaḥ ced  na niṣedhum śakyaḥ katham iti ced  ucyate na tāvat anyathā ākhyāti vādi nā ayam atucche tuccha bhramaḥ atucche atuccha khyātau vā tuccha khyāti bhrama iti śakyam vaktam tucchasya tad khyāteḥ ca kvacid rūpyavat siddha tvena anabhyupagamāt  siddha tve ca tuccha khyāti niṣedhum na śakyā tathā akhyāti vādinā api tucchātucchayoḥ ta khyātyoḥ vā tucchasyātuccha khyāte ratucchasya tucchakhyā teḥ vā viveka ākhyāti bhramaḥ ayam iti na śakyam vaktum tucchasya tad khyāteḥ vā rūpyavasmaryamāṇa tayā śuktivat  gṛhyamāṇa tayā vā kvacid asiddha tvāt siddha tve ca taniṣedhaḥ  na śakya iti uktam etena asat khyāti bhramaḥ  vyākhyātaḥ akhyāta  asat khyāti tuccham khyātauti vā bhrama iti ced kim sarva ākhyātau uta yasya kasyacid  ādye kalye suṣu tādau  eva tad bhamassyāt dvitīye tu sarvadā tad dhama prasaṅgaḥ yasya kasyacid akhyātesmarvadā saṃbhavāt  kaḥ ca satsyā ati bhramaḥ  nāma khyātiḥ uta khyātiḥ akhyāti śced  uktaḥ  doṣaḥ akhyāta avakhyātiḥ iti bheda uktiḥ ca  vṛthā syāt  na vṛthā akhyāti asat khyātyoḥ viveka ākhyāti bitauyā akhyātiḥ iti ced  amatkhya atiḥ iṣṭā syāt  atha khyātiḥ eva asatsyā tibhramaḥ tasya ākhyātiḥ ceviṣayaḥ ukta eva doṣaḥ asat khyātiḥ eva ced  asat khyātiḥ iṣṭā abhrama tvam ca atha ākhyātim amatsyātiṃ manyate anyathā khyātiḥ sā ceṣṭā syāt  akhyātiḥ api khyāti abhāvaḥ ced  amat  tad khyātiḥ ceṣṭā syāt  khyātiḥ eva ced  tava api khyātiḥ eva bhrama iti akhyāti vāditva hāniḥ tasmāt satkhyāti anirvacanīyam khyāti tuccham khyāti iti vā bhrama iti akhyāti vādinā nāyitum śakyate tathā ātma khyāti vādinā api tucchādeḥ tad khyāteḥ ca rūpyavat duddhi ākāra tvena anabhyupagamāt  abhyupagame ca taniṣedhaḥ  na śakya iti u ktam katham ca abhāvam anirvacanauyam vā anicchadbhiḥ idam na asti na yuktam iti vā niṣedhum śakyam kiṃcid api mati aṣṭaḥ tvam idi asya eva bhrāntau bhānāt na kaścid doghamsyāt  na hi rūpya ādi api kvacid sivam iti uktam atyantam amaṃbhāvya māna  chinna sva śiraḥ darśana nabhaḥ bhakṣaṇa ādi api bhrāntau bhāti eva tuccham bhāti iti api bhrāntiḥ bhavet  dṛṣṭā hi sā bhrānti staha ādinām mā ca bhrāntiḥ eva iṣyate bhavadbhiḥ api tasyāḥ bhrānti tvam ku pakṣa āśrayaṇa doṣāt saṃpādayitum aśana vadbhiḥ api tasmāt yaḥ  mama parihāraḥ  na ma bhavatām bhavet  sadādinām atas asanna khyāti ityādi vacanam bhavatām ayukta meva iti sthitam bhavatām anyonya pakṣā api na bhrama asmidhyanti mama tu anye sarve pakṣā bhramā eva iti sidhyanti uktena nyāyena avicāritam aṃsiddham āśritya anye api yuktibhiḥ nirākuryaḥ pareṣṭam vā yathā bhedam vayam yadi avidyā śaraṇāḥ te api na anyathā tad nirākriyā nyāya āghāta asahiṣṇu tvam vastunaḥ  na hi yujyate yathā vayam vicāraṇā tyāga vicārita avidyotya bhrama maṃsiddha masat khyāti ādi pakṣam pareṣṭam vā bhedam ca sarva prāṇi bhrama siddham pareṣṭam vā ātma bhedam pratikṣaṇa bhedam ca vastunaḥ  yuktibhiḥ nirā kurmahe tam tam eva avicārita avidyotya bhramam aṃsiddham eva āśritya na pramāṇa ta smiddham pramāṇata smid hasya asiddhasya vā anirā kārya tvāt ta thā eva yadi bhavantaḥ api amad khyāti ādi paṣṭvam nirākaryaḥ avidyā śaraṇā eva bhavantaḥ api vayam iva na hi avidyām idda tvam vinā tasya nirākāryasya nirākaraṇam yuktam amidyasya pramāṇa tasmid hasya ca nirākaraṇasya naiṣphalyāt aśakyatvāt ca na hi pramāṇa siddham vastu tvāt  nyāya āghātam na mahate avastu eva hi tam na sahate tama iva bhānum na tu vastu atiprasaṅgāt  atas avidyā miī avastu eva nyāyena nirākāryam atas  nyāyena kiṃcid nirākurvadbhiḥ na avidyā anirvācyā apalapanauyā atas asmat pakṣam eva āśritya sarva nirācikā aurṣitam nirākārya miti asmati akṣa eva na nirākārya iti siddham ata upasaṃharati atas avidyām vinā bhrānteḥ ayogāt abhyupeyatām māyā mātram tu śukti ādau rajatāt auti vādibhiḥ spaṣṭa arthaḥ ślokaḥ māyā avidyā ādi śabdaryā śrutiṣu smṛtiṣu uditā sā jagat prakṛtiḥ māyā yatas  māyā mayā bhramāḥ māyā avidyā tamaḥ kāraṇam layaḥ śaktiḥ suptiḥ mahā suptiḥ nidrā akṣarama ākāśam ityādi śabdaḥ amāyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt ityādi śruti smṛtauti hāsa purāṇa ādi vākyeṣu uktā yā māyā sā eva mahat ādessamaḥ tasya jagataḥ prakṛtiḥ iti yad uktam ādya śloke tad upapannam eva yatas  loke api śukti rūpya ādi bhrama asma viṣayā māyā mayāḥ pradarśitāḥ tasmā drupya ādi bhramavat ātmanaḥ abrahma tā bhramasya api jñāna mātra apanodya tvam miḍam na iha nānā asti mṛtyosma vācā ārambhaṇam iti api daitata dṛṣṭi abhāva uktarmāya anirvacanīya tā nanu māyā śabdaḥ prajñā nāmasu api padyate atas  jaga tprakṛteḥ māyāyā anirvacanīyatā eva iti kutasmiddham iti ced  tad na tad kāryasya daita prapañcasya tajñānasya ca śruti mukhāt evā nirvacanīyatā avagamāt tathā hi yathā iha ghaṭaḥ  na astī tyanyatra siddhaḥ  ghaṭaḥ anyatra niṣidhyate na tathā aneha nānā asti kiṃcana amṛtya usma mṛtyum āpnoti ya iha na anā iva bhāskara abhimata kārya kāra mātva khaṇḍanam paśyati ityādi vākyaiḥ anyatra siddha ha etam tad darśanam vā anyatra niṣidhyate kiṃtu tatra eva avidyā upasthāpitam na idam rajata mitivat  atas  rūpya vaītata dṛṣṭyoḥ śrutyā eva anirvacanīyatva niścayāt  tad kāraṇam api tāhak eva śruti uktam iti niścauyate kārya anurūpa tvāt kāraṇasya na ca vastunaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  yuktimān iti uktam vakṣyate ca prajñā nāma tve api māyā śabdasya na brahma nāma tvam  itareṣām nāmnā ām abrahma nāma tvāt ‘māyinam tu maheśvaram iti brahmaṇaḥ pṛthakṛta tvāt  tasya ca kūṭasthasya bodha mādhava pupassākṣāt jagat prakṛtitva ayogāt atas  buddhi nāma syāt  buddheḥ ca na kāraṇa tvam    nitya tvāt svayam kārya tvāta kāryasya ca kāraṇa tvasya pratyakta tvāt  buddhi kārya tve ca ākāśa ādeḥ tad ananya tvāt anitya tvam tad abodhya tvam ca prasajyeta na hi buḍeḥ buddhi bodhya tvam iti uktam vakṣyate ca na ca buddhi kārya jagat iti veda vādinām iṣṭam atas  jagat prakṛtiḥ māyā anirvācyā avidyā iva iti midam na anyatra anān eva      ] jagataḥ anirvācya tve śrutiḥ paśyati iti apye tena eva vyākhyātam nānā vastunaḥ tad arśanasya ca kvacid api abhāvāt aktena nyāyena ata eva upama artha tvām abhavāt  aiva śabdena api rūpya ādi darśanasya iva nānā vastu darśanasya abhāma tā ajñāna mātra tā ucyate atas  amāya āmaya tvam bhedata darśanayoḥ siddham yatra hoti ādya vidyāyām bheda dṛṣṭim vacaḥ  jagau yatra tvasya iti vidyāyām tad ayuktim jagau  api ayatra hi daitam iva bhavati tad itara itaram paśyati ityādi vākyam avidyā avasthāyām eva bheda darśanam svapna iva iti āha ayatra tvamya marvam ātmā eva abhūt tad kena kam paśyet ityādi vākyam vidyāyām uditāyām bheda darśanasya aghaṭam ānatām akena akam iti mā ākṣepam āha tammācchateḥ eva sarvasya kāryasya ani vacanīyatva niścayāt tad kāraṇam api māyā anirvāt ca eva śrutyā uktati niścauyata iti sūktam dṛśya dṛṣṭyoḥ abhāve api dṛṣṭiḥ asti ātmanaḥ acalā avināśau na hi draṣṭum svayaṃjyotiḥ iti śruteḥ nanu sarvasya dṛśyasya tad arśanasya ca abhāve tad daṣṭuḥ tad phalasya ca abhāvāt  na kiṃcid jaḍam ajaḍam vā syāt  atas  bādhaka jñānam api na bhavet  śukti ādi sthānīyasya jñeya ādeḥ abhāvāt  atas  ha etam tad avastham eva pratyakṣa ādi siddham bhavet iti ced  na ayam doṣaḥ yatas  dṛśya tad darśana ādi abhāve api ātmana ssthā strī ssthā snvī dṛṣṭiḥ ananyā mokṣa suṣupta svapna ādiṣu api astauti śrūyate aavināśa vā are ayam ātmā anucchitti dharmā ana hi draṣṭa dṛṣṭeḥ viparilopaḥ  vidyate avināśi tvāt  ana tu tad vitīyam asti atatas anya vibhaktam yad paśyet  aavāyam puruṣa ssvayaṃjyotiḥ bhavati ityādi śruti vākyebhyaḥ atas tāhac ātma jñānasya tad avidyā atad kārya apanodina ssaṃbhavāt na daitata darśanābhyām ca ābādhāśaṅkā yuktibhiḥ ca ayam om darśitaḥ  darśayiṣyate ca tathā pratyakṣa ādi avirodhaḥ ca ata śśrutitaḥ  yuktitaḥ ca mahat ādeḥ sarvasya kāryasya makāraṇasya nirvacanauya tvam rūpī avasiddham jñāna mātra apanodya tvam na anyathā bandha rūpyayoḥ hetuḥ na anyaḥ tayaḥ vaṃse śrūyate na api yujyate anicāyya tam mṛtya mukhāt pramucyate atarati śokam ātma vit ityādi mantra brāhmaṇa vākyebhyaḥ  jñāna mātra apanodya tvam yad saṃsārasya śrūyate dṛśyate ca rūpyasya tad tayoḥ ajñāna ātma katve yujyate na tu anyathā ā yatas  jñānam ajñānasya eva nivarta kam na tvalpa auyasaḥ api vastunaḥ na ca jñānāt anyaḥ  hetu bandha nāśe śrayate marva karmaṇām ca sattva śuddhi artha tvena jñāna utpattau  eva śrutau smṛtau ca viniyukta tvāt  atam etam veda anuvacanena brāhmaṇā vividiṣanti akaṣāya paktiḥ karmāṇi jñānam tu paramā gatiḥ kapāye karmabhiḥ pakke tatas  jñānam pravartate adharmāt sukham ca jñānam ca jñānāt mokṣaḥ adhi gamyate ityādi vākyaiḥ hetu antarābhāvaḥ ca śrūyate atam eva viditvā atimṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthā vidyate aya na aya aiha ced aveda audatha satyam asti na ced iha avedaunmahataḥ  | sarva bhāva rūpyasya mukti śuktau kriyete ced sādhanaiḥ bandha rūpyayoḥ bandhasya nā śassyāt rūpye mṛdan na bhrānti bādhakau anāpi yujyate iti uktam tām eva ayukta tām darśayati yadi vastu vṛttyā eva bandhasya rūpyasya ca piṇḍasya iva ghaṭībhāvaḥ muktiḥ ca śukti bhāvaḥ ca sādhanaiḥ kriyate tadā bandhasya nāśa ssyāt  mukti kṛtau piṇḍasya iva ghaṭa kṛtau rūpye ca mṛd piṇḍa vatsatye na tajñānam bhrāntissyāt uttaratra idam tena na atra prapacyate na ca vastunaḥ anyathā bhāvaḥ  na āśaḥ vā yuktitaḥ  ghaṭate katham yathā pūrva tahastu vyavasthitam tathā eva bhavataḥ tasya na anyathā abhāva ssyāt  tathā abhāva virodhāt na api anyathā bhūtasya anyathā abhavataḥ  vā anyathā bhāvaḥ anavasthā prāptaḥ na api naṣṭasya bhavataḥ  hi anyathā abhāvaḥ  na abhavataḥ nāśaḥ api na bhavataḥ  na api abhavataḥ uttaratra ayam arthaḥ tasmāt anirvācya ajñāna jaḥ  bandhaḥ jñāna mātra apanodyaḥ ca abhyupeyaḥ anyathā mokṣa asaṃbhavāt rūpyam ca tathā anyathā bādhā yogāt  nanu anirvacanīya tve mada mattva amataḥ khyāteḥ tvayā api aniṣṭa tvāt sataḥ ca iṣṭa tvāt  śukti rūpyam api mad eva khyātimat tvāt  bādhaḥ api mata eva yuktaḥ khyātasya eva bādha saṃbhavāt  sataḥ anyasya ākhyāteḥ ana ca ākhyātasya bādhaḥ atasmata eva khyāti bādhaḥ masta iti na tābhyām rūpyasya nirvācya tā siddhiḥ kiṃca asaced na bhavati tad sat eva syāt  dvau pratiṣedhau prakṛtam atham gamayata iti tasmāt sata eva kathaṃcid śrutitaḥ na hi anirvacanīya śabda śśrutaḥ  vede kacid  śrutaḥ api sa na tvad iṣṭa artha ssyāt  tasya ayuktimat tvāt na hi ayuktimān śrautaḥ artha ssyāt  api ca— amṛttikā iti eva matyam abauṇi rūpāṇi amaṃbhavāt iti siddham ucyate nāmataḥ khyātiḥ janma ceṣṭam tvayā api ca vinā aniḥ vacanīya tvam bādha nāśau sataḥ katham mada majjanma nāśau na jagat janma layau śrutau atas anirvacanīya tvam prasiddham śruti yuktitaḥ tvayā api asataḥ khyāti jātī na iṣṭe na ca mataḥ śuddhasya bādha nāśau yuktau śukteḥ brahmaṇaḥ ca tad prasaṅgāt  atas anirvacanīya tvam rūpya ādeḥ siddham nanu sataḥ api jātasya nāśaḥ na ajā tasya brahmaṇaḥ sataḥ api ced  kāryasya janma syāt  brahmaṇaḥ api tad syāt  aviśeṣāt  ata eva nāśaḥ ca kāraṇa abhāvāt na brahmaṇaḥ  janma iti ced na jagataḥ api sattva aviśeṣā brahmaṇaḥ ananya tvāt ca kāraṇam na asti asti ced brahmaṇaḥ api tad syāt  tad ananya tvāt  svatas ananya sya api ced  jagataḥ  brahma kāraṇam syāt  svasya api syāt  na ced na jagataḥ api aviśeṣāt  anya tve api saced  jagat ajam akāraṇam ca bhavet  brahmavat  atas  na mataḥ  janma nāśau asataḥ tu tvayā api tau na iṣṭau jagataḥ ca tau śratau atas asya anirvacanīya tvam śrati yuktitasmiham mataḥ api bādhya tā ced syāt śuktiḥ kasmāt na bādhyate bādhya itara aṃśaya usmat tve mame bhrāntismamā na kim mataḥ api bādhya tve śukrapi bādhassya adrapyavat rūpya aṃśa buveḥ dhānti tvāt  tad eva bādhyam na tu idam aṃśaḥ tabuddheḥ abhrānti tvā diti ceta tad na bādhya itara aṃśaya usmat tve samāne tad daḍyoḥ api bhrānti tvam abhrānti tvam vā samānam nyāyyam yatas  tasmā didaṃ  rūpya aṃśayoḥ api sattva aviśeṣāt bādhya tvam abādhya tvam vā samānam yuktam na tu ekasya bādhya tvam na itarasya iti tasmāt na sataḥ  bādhaḥ  yuktaḥ asataḥ tu khyāti bādhau tvayā api na iṣṭau atas anirvācyam bādhyam iti siddham kiṃca aṣṭākṣaḥ api tad paśyet sati rūpye anya rūpyavat  śuddha akṣā darśanādādhātta drūṣyam sa dilakṣaṇam sat ced śukti rūpyam śuddhacakṣuḥ api tad paśyet satya rūpyavat  na tu tad paśyati satya rūpyam paśyan  api tasmāt tad rūpyam bādhya tvāt ca satya rūpya vilakṣaṇam yadi api khyātatva anna sat tathā api bādhya tvāt na sat iti tasmāt khyātam sarva mad eva iti vadataḥ  bhrānteḥ bādhasya ca niyamaḥ  na syāt  nanu māyā eva te sarvam bhrānti bādhau samau na kim svapnavat yavahāre me niyamaḥ  bhrānti bādhayoḥ prabodhe svāpnavat sarvaḥ  vyavahāraḥ  nivartate tad datva vidyām dahati brahma jñāna āśu śukṣaṇau śukyāde rūpyāt eca sarvasya māyā ātmaka tve api yathā tava bhrānti bādha niyamaḥ tathā mama api syāt  marvasya mattve apauti ced tad na yatas  māyā ātmaka tve api marvasya svapnavat prāk  prabodhāt mama niyamaḥ  yujyate prabodhe tu svāpna vyavahāravat  jāgradi avahāraḥ api tad kāraṇa avidyām brahma jñāna agnau dahati mati nivartata eva vyavasthā vyavahāre api na te tattve tu dūratas  nanu sā dṛśyate bāḍham kim tu mā na eva yujyate tava tu bhrānti bādha vyavasthā vyavahāre api na yuktā idam satyam asatya mada iti vastu tattva vyavasthā tu dūra utsāritā mama tu aikātmyam eva satyam na daitam iti va stutattva vyavasthā api asti nanu bhrānti bādha ādi vyavasthā vyavahāre dṛśyata eva na tu yujyate tvad pakṣe api sarvasya māyā maya tvāt satyam tathā api bhrāntasya api kasyacid abādhassvapne sihaḥ tava api na tu evam   āṇā satyasya api bādhaḥ kvacid siddaḥ mama atas sarvasya māyā maya tve api dṛśyamānā vyavahāra vyavasthā mama yujyate dṛṣṭānta bhāvāt na tu tava tad abhāvāt tasmāt māyā tmakam eva rūpya adyeṣṭavyam yatas  māyām anicchataḥ tucchakhyātiḥ prāpnoti anaumayā yatas  na śuklaḥ  rūpyam tad sa margaḥ  vā asti kutracid  māyā ātmakam rūpya ādi iti evam anicchataḥ tuccham rūpya ādi khyāti iti aniṣṭam pramajyeta yata śatau khyātam rūpyam rūpya maṃmargaḥ  vā śukrtana kvacid asti atas tasya kathaṃcid api mattvām abhavāt anirvacanīya tām anabhyapagacchataḥ tuccha abhyapagamaḥ  balāt prāpnoti eva atas  māyā abhyapagama eva śreyān iti abhi prāyas  avāha tuccham bhātauti tathā bādha ādi gamyate na hanti bādhadhaurvastu mā hi tattva prakāśikā ana śuktau rūpyam tad samargā vāmita kutracit iti śrutvā atra avamare tucchava ādyāha  tuccham eva rūpyam bhāti tasya na idam rajatam iti bādhāt  tucchatā avagamāt  na ca bādhaḥ  vastu nāśayati tattva nivedaka tvāt  jñānasya bādhaka jñāne hi mati rūpyam na bhāti na asti ca yadi mad  rūpyam tad kim na bhavet na bhāti vā na astauti ca bhāti na ced  tad na kucidamtauti katham māyā vādī api yāt  bravīti ca atas saḥ api tasya asattvam vetti eva bādhāt  na sa rūpyasya asat tvam betti kiṃtu sattva abhāva mātram ta na bādhaka jñānāt  tasya mad artha tvāt iti ced kaḥ anyasmattva abhāvaḥ amattvāt atam mattva abhāvam vetti ced  amat tvam vetti eva bādhakaḥ ced nāmattvam rūpyasya bodhayet  kaḥ anyaḥ  bodhayet  mattvena khyātasya tasya katham ca sa bādhaka ssyāt  atas  bādhadhau rūpyasya tucchatā mā iva bodhayati na anyathā bādhadhaumsyāt  ghaṭa ādi dhauvat  mad artha tvāt  tasmāt tuccham eva bhātauti na syāt dhāntiḥ tayā mad chedodhyate kātra bādhya tā tatas  bādhādamati eva maurdhāntiritoṣya tām nanu na bhrāntaḥ  bādha buddhau ca tuccham khyāti tasya khyātya yogāt iti ced na etad yuktam yatas tayā bhānyā bādha dhiyā ca mad cat dodhyate bādhya bādhakatva ayogāt bhrānti ma na syāt  na hi mad daurbādhyate mad iyā amahiyā vā na api maddau abarbādhate maḍiyam amaḍiyam vā matya rūpya ādi budvivat  anyathā atipramaṅgāt ca atassat viyoḥ bādhya bādhakatva ayogāt tad arśanāca asata eva mad rūpeṇa khyā tiḥ dhāntiḥ tasya ca āmattva bodhanam bādha iti upeyam na asat sattvena bhātauti gauḥ bādhena virudhyate yad pratyabhādadaḥ  na iti bādha eva hi ababudhat  tuccham nimsva rūpa tvāt  sva rūpeṇa api na khyāti atā natarām sat rūpeṇa khyātauti vacanam bādhakena virudhyate ma hi yad  pratibhātam rūpyam tad na asti iti tasya tucchatām bodhitavān atas tena virodhamsyāt  tasmāt  aamati eva mad daurdhānti ritoṣyatām iti yuktam eva uktam na bhāti tuccham iti gauḥ tucchakhyātyā virudhyate na ced tad bhāti tuccha tvam kutas atuccham na kim bhavet  nanu tuccham tuccha tvāt eva na khyāti atas  rūpyasya tucchatām bādhaḥ  bodhayati iti ayuktam uktam iti ced etad dacanam na idam rajatam iti anayā eva tucchakhyātyā virudhyate na hi na idam rajata miti rūpya sattvam bodhyate naḥ vaiphalyāt pūrva jñān vada bādhakatva pramaṅgāt ca yadi rūpya abhāvaḥ  nāma dharma śakta ranyasya vā vastu bhūtaḥ  bodhyeta tadā api abādhaka tvam sya ahaḥ tu antara jñānavat  pratyakṣamramasya pratyakṣam eva bādhakam na abhāva jñānam daurbalyāt iti ced nāyam da upassyāt  bhrama tvāt  abhrama tve pratyakṣam api na bādhakam syāt tulya bala tvāt  iyoḥ vā bādhassyāt  pratyakṣam ca bhāva viṣayam katham rūpya bādhakam syāt  virodhāt  bādhakam iti ced  bhāva jñāna yaḥ bhinna viṣaya yona virodhaḥ  yuktaḥ ghaṭa paṭa jñānayoḥ iva abhinna viṣayayoḥ natarām ghaṭa jñānayoḥ iva māyā vādinā api rūpyasya sattva abhāvam vadatā tad pramāṇam bādha rāṣṭavyaḥ bādhaḥ ced tam abodhayan parya vasyet  rūpya sattvam abādhitam tiṣṭhet  atas tucchatā eva bādhena rūpyasya bodhyā iti na bhāti tuccham iti gauḥ tucchakhyātyā viru dhyata eva na ced tuccham bhāti kutas tasya tuccha tvam niścitam atuccham kasmāt na bhavet  tasmāt tuccham na bhāti ced  tuccham na bhātauti na śakyam vaktum tasya ajñāta tvāt  jñātam hi idam ityam iti brūyāt lokaḥ tasmāt bhāti eva atas tuccham na bhātauti vadana mṛṣāvādī syāt  jñātvā eva anyathā vacanāt mātā vandhyā itivat  viruddha artha vādī ca tuccha śabdena eva artha ajñātatva uktaḥ tvad dhānti nivṛtti artham tad vacana miti ced  na sat ādi nāmaudṛś  bhramasmam asti tuccha khyāte  tucchasya vā rūpyavat  kvacid siddhatvena anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame ca tucchakhyāteḥ sarva ātmanā apalāpaḥ  na yuktaḥ māyā vādinā api tuccha bhrāntim icchatā tuccha bhrāntau tucchasya khyātiḥ eṣṭavyā rūpya bhrāntau  iva rūpyasya anyathā na tad dhāntissyāt  atas  na tucchasya khyāti anahatvam bhrāntau khyāteḥ na bhrāntau tuccham khyāti na api rūpyam kiṃtu māyā eva rūpya rūpā tuccha rūpā ca khyātauti ced tathā api tuccha rūpam nāma kiṃcid rapya rūpavat  khyāti aham midam tasmā nmāyāvādinā api mahā ādibhiḥ iva na tuccham khyāti iti maṅgham nivṛtti artham api na yuktam vaktum tuccha bhrama abhyupagame api tuccha khyāteḥ avaśya abhyapeya tvāt na anyathā āmau tucchabhrasassyāt  yad  khyāti tena hi bhramaḥ  vyapadiśyate rūpya bhrama iti yathā tasmāt sarvathā tuccham na khyāti iti vacaḥ  na yuktimat  kiṃca eṣṭavyā eva ca sat māyāvādibhyām api tucchadhauḥ tathā na asti eva tatvā api yathā bhāt na anyathā bhramaḥ śukti sāmāna adhikaraṇyena rūpyam bhrāntau bhāti na ca tathā asti anyathā sat api anyathā bhramaḥ  na syāt  atas śukti rūpya sāmānādhikaraṇyasya sat dādinā tucchasya khyātiḥ eṣṭavyā tathā māyāyāḥ  atuccha tvepi tasyāḥ  rūpya tvam sattvam ca na asti eva anirvācya tvāt  atas tad ubhayam tuccham eva atucchavat dhāntau khyāti sattve api bādhe rūpya ātmanā asti na mattvā api avyakta rūpeṇa vyakta rūpeṇa na asti tad  yadi māyā vādau brūyāt māyā vivarta tvāt rūpyasya tada stitvasya ca sva kāraṇa māyā ātmanā sattvāt na bhrāntau tuccham khyātauti tathā api na bādhe rūpya ātmanā astauti ca bhāti kiṃtu tuccham ava bhāti atas  bhrāntau  api tuccham eva ābhānnā tuccham anyathā bādhaḥ api atucchatām eva āmi bodhayet  na
